207/**
208 * Regions store data for a certain region of a table.  It stores all columns
209 * for each row. A given table consists of one or more Regions.
210 *
211 * <p>An Region is defined by its table and its key extent.
212 *
213 * <p>Locking at the Region level serves only one purpose: preventing the
214 * region from being closed (and consequently split) while other operations
215 * are ongoing. Each row level operation obtains both a row lock and a region
216 * read lock for the duration of the operation. While a scanner is being
217 * constructed, getScanner holds a read lock. If the scanner is successfully
218 * constructed, it holds a read lock until it is closed. A close takes out a
219 * write lock and consequently will block for ongoing operations and will block
220 * new operations from starting while the close is in progress.
221 */
222@SuppressWarnings("deprecation")
223@InterfaceAudience.Private
224public class HRegion implements HeapSize, PropagatingConfigurationObserver, Region {
225  private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(HRegion.class);
226

228    "hbase.hregion.scan.loadColumnFamiliesOnDemand";

231  public static final int DEFAULT_MAX_CELL_SIZE = 10485760;

234      "hbase.regionserver.minibatch.size";
235  public static final int DEFAULT_HBASE_REGIONSERVER_MINIBATCH_SIZE = 20000;

328  // The internal wait duration to acquire a lock before read/update
329  // from the region. It is not per row. The purpose of this wait time
330  // is to avoid waiting a long time while the region is busy, so that
331  // we can release the IPC handler soon enough to improve the
332  // availability of the region server. It can be adjusted by
333  // tuning configuration "hbase.busy.wait.duration".

339  // we can limit the max multiplier.

343  // purge timeout, when a RPC call will be terminated by the RPC engine.
344  final long maxBusyWaitDuration;

373  //
374  // Context: During replay we want to ensure that we do not lose any data. So, we
375  // have to be conservative in how we replay wals. For each store, we calculate
376  // the maxSeqId up to which the store was flushed. And, skip the edits which
377  // are equal to or lower than maxSeqId for each store.
378  // The following map is populated when opening the region
379  Map<byte[], Long> maxSeqIdInStores = new TreeMap<>(Bytes.BYTES_COMPARATOR);

389  /**
390   * @return The smallest mvcc readPoint across all the scanners in this
391   * region. Writes older than this readPoint, are included in every
392   * read operation.
393   */
394  public long getSmallestReadPoint() {
395    long minimumReadPoint;
396    // We need to ensure that while we are calculating the smallestReadPoint
397    // no new RegionScanners can grab a readPoint that we are unaware of.
398    // We achieve this by synchronizing on the scannerReadPoints object.
399    synchronized (scannerReadPoints) {
400      minimumReadPoint = mvcc.getReadPoint();
401      for (Long readPoint : this.scannerReadPoints.values()) {
402        if (readPoint < minimumReadPoint) {
403          minimumReadPoint = readPoint;
404        }
405      }
406    }
407    return minimumReadPoint;
408  }
409
410  /*
411   * Data structure of write state flags used coordinating flushes,
412   * compactions and closes.
413   */
414  static class WriteState {
415    // Set while a memstore flush is happening.
416    volatile boolean flushing = false;
417    // Set when a flush has been requested.
418    volatile boolean flushRequested = false;
419    // Number of compactions running.
420    AtomicInteger compacting = new AtomicInteger(0);
421    // Gets set in close. If set, cannot compact or flush again.
422    volatile boolean writesEnabled = true;
423    // Set if region is read-only
424    volatile boolean readOnly = false;
425    // whether the reads are enabled. This is different than readOnly, because readOnly is
426    // static in the lifetime of the region, while readsEnabled is dynamic
427    volatile boolean readsEnabled = true;
428
429    /**
430     * Set flags that make this region read-only.
431     *
432     * @param onOff flip value for region r/o setting
433     */
434    synchronized void setReadOnly(final boolean onOff) {
435      this.writesEnabled = !onOff;
436      this.readOnly = onOff;
437    }
438
439    boolean isReadOnly() {
440      return this.readOnly;
441    }
442
443    boolean isFlushRequested() {
444      return this.flushRequested;
445    }
446
447    void setReadsEnabled(boolean readsEnabled) {
448      this.readsEnabled = readsEnabled;
449    }
450
451    static final long HEAP_SIZE = ClassSize.align(
452        ClassSize.OBJECT + 5 * Bytes.SIZEOF_BOOLEAN);
453  }
454
455  /**
456   * Objects from this class are created when flushing to describe all the different states that
457   * that method ends up in. The Result enum describes those states. The sequence id should only
458   * be specified if the flush was successful, and the failure message should only be specified
459   * if it didn't flush.
460   */
461  public static class FlushResultImpl implements FlushResult {
462    final Result result;
463    final String failureReason;
464    final long flushSequenceId;
465    final boolean wroteFlushWalMarker;
466
467    /**
468     * Convenience constructor to use when the flush is successful, the failure message is set to
469     * null.
470     * @param result Expecting FLUSHED_NO_COMPACTION_NEEDED or FLUSHED_COMPACTION_NEEDED.
471     * @param flushSequenceId Generated sequence id that comes right after the edits in the
472     *                        memstores.
473     */
474    FlushResultImpl(Result result, long flushSequenceId) {
475      this(result, flushSequenceId, null, false);
476      assert result == Result.FLUSHED_NO_COMPACTION_NEEDED || result == Result
477          .FLUSHED_COMPACTION_NEEDED;
478    }
479
480    /**
481     * Convenience constructor to use when we cannot flush.
482     * @param result Expecting CANNOT_FLUSH_MEMSTORE_EMPTY or CANNOT_FLUSH.
483     * @param failureReason Reason why we couldn't flush.
484     */
485    FlushResultImpl(Result result, String failureReason, boolean wroteFlushMarker) {
486      this(result, -1, failureReason, wroteFlushMarker);
487      assert result == Result.CANNOT_FLUSH_MEMSTORE_EMPTY || result == Result.CANNOT_FLUSH;
488    }
489
490    /**
491     * Constructor with all the parameters.
492     * @param result Any of the Result.
493     * @param flushSequenceId Generated sequence id if the memstores were flushed else -1.
494     * @param failureReason Reason why we couldn't flush, or null.
495     */
496    FlushResultImpl(Result result, long flushSequenceId, String failureReason,
497      boolean wroteFlushMarker) {
498      this.result = result;
499      this.flushSequenceId = flushSequenceId;
500      this.failureReason = failureReason;
501      this.wroteFlushWalMarker = wroteFlushMarker;
502    }
503
504    /**
505     * Convenience method, the equivalent of checking if result is
506     * FLUSHED_NO_COMPACTION_NEEDED or FLUSHED_NO_COMPACTION_NEEDED.
507     * @return true if the memstores were flushed, else false.
508     */
509    @Override
510    public boolean isFlushSucceeded() {
511      return result == Result.FLUSHED_NO_COMPACTION_NEEDED || result == Result
512          .FLUSHED_COMPACTION_NEEDED;
513    }
514
515    /**
516     * Convenience method, the equivalent of checking if result is FLUSHED_COMPACTION_NEEDED.
517     * @return True if the flush requested a compaction, else false (doesn't even mean it flushed).
518     */
519    @Override
520    public boolean isCompactionNeeded() {
521      return result == Result.FLUSHED_COMPACTION_NEEDED;
522    }
523
524    @Override
525    public String toString() {
526      return new StringBuilder()
527        .append("flush result:").append(result).append(", ")
528        .append("failureReason:").append(failureReason).append(",")
529        .append("flush seq id").append(flushSequenceId).toString();
530    }
531
532    @Override
533    public Result getResult() {
534      return result;
535    }
536  }
537
538  /** A result object from prepare flush cache stage */
539  @VisibleForTesting
540  static class PrepareFlushResult {
541    final FlushResultImpl result; // indicating a failure result from prepare
542    final TreeMap<byte[], StoreFlushContext> storeFlushCtxs;
543    final TreeMap<byte[], List<Path>> committedFiles;
544    final TreeMap<byte[], MemStoreSize> storeFlushableSize;
545    final long startTime;
546    final long flushOpSeqId;
547    final long flushedSeqId;
548    final MemStoreSizing totalFlushableSize;
549
550    /** Constructs an early exit case */
551    PrepareFlushResult(FlushResultImpl result, long flushSeqId) {
552      this(result, null, null, null, Math.max(0, flushSeqId), 0, 0, MemStoreSizing.DUD);
553    }
554
555    /** Constructs a successful prepare flush result */
556    PrepareFlushResult(
557      TreeMap<byte[], StoreFlushContext> storeFlushCtxs,
558      TreeMap<byte[], List<Path>> committedFiles,
559      TreeMap<byte[], MemStoreSize> storeFlushableSize, long startTime, long flushSeqId,
560      long flushedSeqId, MemStoreSizing totalFlushableSize) {
561      this(null, storeFlushCtxs, committedFiles, storeFlushableSize, startTime,
562        flushSeqId, flushedSeqId, totalFlushableSize);
563    }
564
565    private PrepareFlushResult(
566        FlushResultImpl result,
567      TreeMap<byte[], StoreFlushContext> storeFlushCtxs,
568      TreeMap<byte[], List<Path>> committedFiles,
569      TreeMap<byte[], MemStoreSize> storeFlushableSize, long startTime, long flushSeqId,
570      long flushedSeqId, MemStoreSizing totalFlushableSize) {
571      this.result = result;
572      this.storeFlushCtxs = storeFlushCtxs;
573      this.committedFiles = committedFiles;
574      this.storeFlushableSize = storeFlushableSize;
575      this.startTime = startTime;
576      this.flushOpSeqId = flushSeqId;
577      this.flushedSeqId = flushedSeqId;
578      this.totalFlushableSize = totalFlushableSize;
579    }
580
581    public FlushResult getResult() {
582      return this.result;
583    }
584  }
585
586  /**
587   * A class that tracks exceptions that have been observed in one batch. Not thread safe.
588   */
589  static class ObservedExceptionsInBatch {
590    private boolean wrongRegion = false;
591    private boolean failedSanityCheck = false;
592    private boolean wrongFamily = false;
593
594    /**
595     * @return If a {@link WrongRegionException} has been observed.
596     */
597    boolean hasSeenWrongRegion() {
598      return wrongRegion;
599    }
600
601    /**
602     * Records that a {@link WrongRegionException} has been observed.
603     */
604    void sawWrongRegion() {
605      wrongRegion = true;
606    }
607
608    /**
609     * @return If a {@link FailedSanityCheckException} has been observed.
610     */
611    boolean hasSeenFailedSanityCheck() {
612      return failedSanityCheck;
613    }
614
615    /**
616     * Records that a {@link FailedSanityCheckException} has been observed.
617     */
618    void sawFailedSanityCheck() {
619      failedSanityCheck = true;
620    }
621
622    /**
623     * @return If a {@link NoSuchColumnFamilyException} has been observed.
624     */
625    boolean hasSeenNoSuchFamily() {
626      return wrongFamily;
627    }
628
629    /**
630     * Records that a {@link NoSuchColumnFamilyException} has been observed.
631     */
632    void sawNoSuchFamily() {
633      wrongFamily = true;
634    }
635  }
636
637  final WriteState writestate = new WriteState();
638
639  long memstoreFlushSize;
640  final long timestampSlop;
641  final long rowProcessorTimeout;
642
643  // Last flush time for each Store. Useful when we are flushing for each column
644  private final ConcurrentMap<HStore, Long> lastStoreFlushTimeMap = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
645
646  final RegionServerServices rsServices;
647  private RegionServerAccounting rsAccounting;
648  private long flushCheckInterval;
649  // flushPerChanges is to prevent too many changes in memstore
650  private long flushPerChanges;
651  private long blockingMemStoreSize;
652  // Used to guard closes
653  final ReentrantReadWriteLock lock = new ReentrantReadWriteLock();
654
655  // Stop updates lock
656  private final ReentrantReadWriteLock updatesLock = new ReentrantReadWriteLock();
657  private boolean splitRequest;
658  private byte[] explicitSplitPoint = null;
659
660  private final MultiVersionConcurrencyControl mvcc = new MultiVersionConcurrencyControl();
661
662  // Coprocessor host
663  private RegionCoprocessorHost coprocessorHost;

665  private TableDescriptor htableDescriptor = null;
666  private RegionSplitPolicy splitPolicy;
667  private FlushPolicy flushPolicy;
668
669  private final MetricsRegion metricsRegion;
670  private final MetricsRegionWrapperImpl metricsRegionWrapper;
671  private final Durability regionDurability;
672  private final boolean regionStatsEnabled;
673  // Stores the replication scope of the various column families of the table
674  // that has non-default scope
675  private final NavigableMap<byte[], Integer> replicationScope = new TreeMap<>(
676      Bytes.BYTES_COMPARATOR);
677
678  private final StoreHotnessProtector storeHotnessProtector;
679
680  /**
681   * HRegion constructor. This constructor should only be used for testing and
682   * extensions.  Instances of HRegion should be instantiated with the
683   * {@link HRegion#createHRegion} or {@link HRegion#openHRegion} method.
684   *
685   * @param tableDir qualified path of directory where region should be located,
686   * usually the table directory.
687   * @param wal The WAL is the outbound log for any updates to the HRegion
688   * The wal file is a logfile from the previous execution that's
689   * custom-computed for this HRegion. The HRegionServer computes and sorts the
690   * appropriate wal info for this HRegion. If there is a previous wal file
691   * (implying that the HRegion has been written-to before), then read it from
692   * the supplied path.
693   * @param fs is the filesystem.
694   * @param confParam is global configuration settings.
695   * @param regionInfo - RegionInfo that describes the region
696   * is new), then read them from the supplied path.
697   * @param htd the table descriptor
698   * @param rsServices reference to {@link RegionServerServices} or null
699   * @deprecated Use other constructors.
700   */
701  @Deprecated
702  @VisibleForTesting
703  public HRegion(final Path tableDir, final WAL wal, final FileSystem fs,
704      final Configuration confParam, final RegionInfo regionInfo,
705      final TableDescriptor htd, final RegionServerServices rsServices) {
706    this(new HRegionFileSystem(confParam, fs, tableDir, regionInfo),
707      wal, confParam, htd, rsServices);
708  }
709
710  /**
711   * HRegion constructor. This constructor should only be used for testing and
712   * extensions.  Instances of HRegion should be instantiated with the
713   * {@link HRegion#createHRegion} or {@link HRegion#openHRegion} method.
714   *
715   * @param fs is the filesystem.
716   * @param wal The WAL is the outbound log for any updates to the HRegion
717   * The wal file is a logfile from the previous execution that's
718   * custom-computed for this HRegion. The HRegionServer computes and sorts the
719   * appropriate wal info for this HRegion. If there is a previous wal file
720   * (implying that the HRegion has been written-to before), then read it from
721   * the supplied path.
722   * @param confParam is global configuration settings.
723   * @param htd the table descriptor
724   * @param rsServices reference to {@link RegionServerServices} or null
725   */
726  public HRegion(final HRegionFileSystem fs, final WAL wal, final Configuration confParam,
727      final TableDescriptor htd, final RegionServerServices rsServices) {
728    if (htd == null) {
729      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Need table descriptor");
730    }
731
732    if (confParam instanceof CompoundConfiguration) {
733      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Need original base configuration");
734    }
735
736    this.wal = wal;
737    this.fs = fs;
738
739    // 'conf' renamed to 'confParam' b/c we use this.conf in the constructor
740    this.baseConf = confParam;
741    this.conf = new CompoundConfiguration()
742      .add(confParam)
743      .addBytesMap(htd.getValues());
744    this.flushCheckInterval = conf.getInt(MEMSTORE_PERIODIC_FLUSH_INTERVAL,
745        DEFAULT_CACHE_FLUSH_INTERVAL);
746    this.flushPerChanges = conf.getLong(MEMSTORE_FLUSH_PER_CHANGES, DEFAULT_FLUSH_PER_CHANGES);
747    if (this.flushPerChanges > MAX_FLUSH_PER_CHANGES) {
748      throw new IllegalArgumentException(MEMSTORE_FLUSH_PER_CHANGES + " can not exceed "
749          + MAX_FLUSH_PER_CHANGES);
750    }
751    this.rowLockWaitDuration = conf.getInt("hbase.rowlock.wait.duration",
752                    DEFAULT_ROWLOCK_WAIT_DURATION);
753
754    this.isLoadingCfsOnDemandDefault = conf.getBoolean(LOAD_CFS_ON_DEMAND_CONFIG_KEY, true);
755    this.htableDescriptor = htd;
756    Set<byte[]> families = this.htableDescriptor.getColumnFamilyNames();
757    for (byte[] family : families) {
758      if (!replicationScope.containsKey(family)) {
759        int scope = htd.getColumnFamily(family).getScope();
760        // Only store those families that has NON-DEFAULT scope
761        if (scope != REPLICATION_SCOPE_LOCAL) {
762          // Do a copy before storing it here.
763          replicationScope.put(Bytes.copy(family), scope);
764        }
765      }
766    }
767    this.rsServices = rsServices;
768    setHTableSpecificConf();
769    this.scannerReadPoints = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
770
771    this.busyWaitDuration = conf.getLong(
772      "hbase.busy.wait.duration", DEFAULT_BUSY_WAIT_DURATION);
773    this.maxBusyWaitMultiplier = conf.getInt("hbase.busy.wait.multiplier.max", 2);
774    if (busyWaitDuration * maxBusyWaitMultiplier <= 0L) {
775      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid hbase.busy.wait.duration ("
776        + busyWaitDuration + ") or hbase.busy.wait.multiplier.max ("
777        + maxBusyWaitMultiplier + "). Their product should be positive");
778    }
779    this.maxBusyWaitDuration = conf.getLong("hbase.ipc.client.call.purge.timeout",
780      2 * HConstants.DEFAULT_HBASE_RPC_TIMEOUT);
781
782    /*
783     * timestamp.slop provides a server-side constraint on the timestamp. This
784     * assumes that you base your TS around currentTimeMillis(). In this case,
785     * throw an error to the user if the user-specified TS is newer than now +
786     * slop. LATEST_TIMESTAMP == don't use this functionality
787     */
788    this.timestampSlop = conf.getLong(
789        "hbase.hregion.keyvalue.timestamp.slop.millisecs",
790        HConstants.LATEST_TIMESTAMP);
791
792    /**
793     * Timeout for the process time in processRowsWithLocks().
794     * Use -1 to switch off time bound.
795     */
796    this.rowProcessorTimeout = conf.getLong(
797        "hbase.hregion.row.processor.timeout", DEFAULT_ROW_PROCESSOR_TIMEOUT);
798    this.regionDurability = htd.getDurability() == Durability.USE_DEFAULT ?
799        DEFAULT_DURABILITY : htd.getDurability();
800
801    this.storeHotnessProtector = new StoreHotnessProtector(this, conf);
802
803    if (rsServices != null) {
804      this.rsAccounting = this.rsServices.getRegionServerAccounting();
805      // don't initialize coprocessors if not running within a regionserver
806      // TODO: revisit if coprocessors should load in other cases
807      this.coprocessorHost = new RegionCoprocessorHost(this, rsServices, conf);
808      this.metricsRegionWrapper = new MetricsRegionWrapperImpl(this);
809      this.metricsRegion = new MetricsRegion(this.metricsRegionWrapper);
810    } else {
811      this.metricsRegionWrapper = null;
812      this.metricsRegion = null;
813    }
814    if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
815      // Write out region name, its encoded name and storeHotnessProtector as string.
816      LOG.debug("Instantiated " + this +"; "+ storeHotnessProtector.toString());
817    }
818
819    configurationManager = Optional.empty();
820
821    // disable stats tracking system tables, but check the config for everything else
822    this.regionStatsEnabled = htd.getTableName().getNamespaceAsString().equals(
823        NamespaceDescriptor.SYSTEM_NAMESPACE_NAME_STR) ?
824          false :
825          conf.getBoolean(HConstants.ENABLE_CLIENT_BACKPRESSURE,
826              HConstants.DEFAULT_ENABLE_CLIENT_BACKPRESSURE);
827
828    this.maxCellSize = conf.getLong(HBASE_MAX_CELL_SIZE_KEY, DEFAULT_MAX_CELL_SIZE);
829    this.miniBatchSize = conf.getInt(HBASE_REGIONSERVER_MINIBATCH_SIZE,
830        DEFAULT_HBASE_REGIONSERVER_MINIBATCH_SIZE);
831  }
832
833  void setHTableSpecificConf() {
834    if (this.htableDescriptor == null) return;
835    long flushSize = this.htableDescriptor.getMemStoreFlushSize();
836
837    if (flushSize <= 0) {
838      flushSize = conf.getLong(HConstants.HREGION_MEMSTORE_FLUSH_SIZE,
839          TableDescriptorBuilder.DEFAULT_MEMSTORE_FLUSH_SIZE);
840    }
841    this.memstoreFlushSize = flushSize;
842    long mult = conf.getLong(HConstants.HREGION_MEMSTORE_BLOCK_MULTIPLIER,
843        HConstants.DEFAULT_HREGION_MEMSTORE_BLOCK_MULTIPLIER);
844    this.blockingMemStoreSize = this.memstoreFlushSize * mult;
845  }
846
847  /**
848   * Initialize this region.
849   * Used only by tests and SplitTransaction to reopen the region.
850   * You should use createHRegion() or openHRegion()
851   * @return What the next sequence (edit) id should be.
852   * @throws IOException e
853   * @deprecated use HRegion.createHRegion() or HRegion.openHRegion()
854   */
855  @Deprecated
856  public long initialize() throws IOException {
857    return initialize(null);
858  }
859
860  /**
861   * Initialize this region.
862   *
863   * @param reporter Tickle every so often if initialize is taking a while.
864   * @return What the next sequence (edit) id should be.
865   * @throws IOException e
866   */
867  private long initialize(final CancelableProgressable reporter) throws IOException {
868
869    //Refuse to open the region if there is no column family in the table
870    if (htableDescriptor.getColumnFamilyCount() == 0) {
871      throw new DoNotRetryIOException("Table " + htableDescriptor.getTableName().getNameAsString()+
872          " should have at least one column family.");
873    }
874
875    MonitoredTask status = TaskMonitor.get().createStatus("Initializing region " + this);
876    long nextSeqId = -1;
877    try {
878      nextSeqId = initializeRegionInternals(reporter, status);
879      return nextSeqId;
880    } finally {
881      // nextSeqid will be -1 if the initialization fails.
882      // At least it will be 0 otherwise.
883      if (nextSeqId == -1) {
884        status.abort("Exception during region " + getRegionInfo().getRegionNameAsString() +
885          " initialization.");
886      }
887    }
888  }
889
890  private long initializeRegionInternals(final CancelableProgressable reporter,
891      final MonitoredTask status) throws IOException {
892    if (coprocessorHost != null) {
893      status.setStatus("Running coprocessor pre-open hook");
894      coprocessorHost.preOpen();
895    }
896
897    // Write HRI to a file in case we need to recover hbase:meta
898    // Only the primary replica should write .regioninfo
899    if (this.getRegionInfo().getReplicaId() == RegionInfo.DEFAULT_REPLICA_ID) {
900      status.setStatus("Writing region info on filesystem");
901      fs.checkRegionInfoOnFilesystem();
902    }
903
904    // Initialize all the HStores
905    status.setStatus("Initializing all the Stores");
906    long maxSeqId = initializeStores(reporter, status);
907    this.mvcc.advanceTo(maxSeqId);
908    if (ServerRegionReplicaUtil.shouldReplayRecoveredEdits(this)) {
909      Collection<HStore> stores = this.stores.values();
910      try {
911        // update the stores that we are replaying
912        stores.forEach(HStore::startReplayingFromWAL);
913        // Recover any edits if available.
914        maxSeqId = Math.max(maxSeqId,
915          replayRecoveredEditsIfAny(this.fs.getRegionDir(), maxSeqIdInStores, reporter, status));
916        // Make sure mvcc is up to max.
917        this.mvcc.advanceTo(maxSeqId);
918      } finally {
919        // update the stores that we are done replaying
920        stores.forEach(HStore::stopReplayingFromWAL);
921      }
922    }
923    this.lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId = maxSeqId;
924
925    this.writestate.setReadOnly(ServerRegionReplicaUtil.isReadOnly(this));
926    this.writestate.flushRequested = false;
927    this.writestate.compacting.set(0);
928
929    if (this.writestate.writesEnabled) {
930      // Remove temporary data left over from old regions
931      status.setStatus("Cleaning up temporary data from old regions");
932      fs.cleanupTempDir();
933    }
934
935    if (this.writestate.writesEnabled) {
936      status.setStatus("Cleaning up detritus from prior splits");
937      // Get rid of any splits or merges that were lost in-progress.  Clean out
938      // these directories here on open.  We may be opening a region that was
939      // being split but we crashed in the middle of it all.
940      fs.cleanupAnySplitDetritus();
941      fs.cleanupMergesDir();
942    }
943
944    // Initialize split policy
945    this.splitPolicy = RegionSplitPolicy.create(this, conf);
946
947    // Initialize flush policy
948    this.flushPolicy = FlushPolicyFactory.create(this, conf);
949
950    long lastFlushTime = EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime();
951    for (HStore store: stores.values()) {
952      this.lastStoreFlushTimeMap.put(store, lastFlushTime);
953    }
954
955    // Use maximum of log sequenceid or that which was found in stores
956    // (particularly if no recovered edits, seqid will be -1).
957    long maxSeqIdFromFile =
958      WALSplitter.getMaxRegionSequenceId(fs.getFileSystem(), fs.getRegionDir());
959    long nextSeqId = Math.max(maxSeqId, maxSeqIdFromFile) + 1;
960    if (writestate.writesEnabled) {
961      WALSplitter.writeRegionSequenceIdFile(fs.getFileSystem(), fs.getRegionDir(), nextSeqId);
962    }
963
964    LOG.info("Opened {}; next sequenceid={}", this.getRegionInfo().getShortNameToLog(), nextSeqId);
965
966    // A region can be reopened if failed a split; reset flags
967    this.closing.set(false);
968    this.closed.set(false);
969
970    if (coprocessorHost != null) {
971      status.setStatus("Running coprocessor post-open hooks");
972      coprocessorHost.postOpen();
973    }
974
975    status.markComplete("Region opened successfully");
976    return nextSeqId;
977  }
978
979  /**
980   * Open all Stores.
981   * @param reporter
982   * @param status
983   * @return Highest sequenceId found out in a Store.
984   * @throws IOException
985   */
986  private long initializeStores(CancelableProgressable reporter, MonitoredTask status)
987      throws IOException {
988    // Load in all the HStores.
989    long maxSeqId = -1;
990    // initialized to -1 so that we pick up MemstoreTS from column families
991    long maxMemstoreTS = -1;
992
993    if (htableDescriptor.getColumnFamilyCount() != 0) {
994      // initialize the thread pool for opening stores in parallel.
995      ThreadPoolExecutor storeOpenerThreadPool =
996        getStoreOpenAndCloseThreadPool("StoreOpener-" + this.getRegionInfo().getShortNameToLog());
997      CompletionService<HStore> completionService = new ExecutorCompletionService<>(storeOpenerThreadPool);
998
999      // initialize each store in parallel
1000      for (final ColumnFamilyDescriptor family : htableDescriptor.getColumnFamilies()) {
1001        status.setStatus("Instantiating store for column family " + family);
1002        completionService.submit(new Callable<HStore>() {
1003          @Override
1004          public HStore call() throws IOException {
1005            return instantiateHStore(family);
1006          }
1007        });
1008      }
1009      boolean allStoresOpened = false;
1010      boolean hasSloppyStores = false;
1011      try {
1012        for (int i = 0; i < htableDescriptor.getColumnFamilyCount(); i++) {
1013          Future<HStore> future = completionService.take();
1014          HStore store = future.get();
1015          this.stores.put(store.getColumnFamilyDescriptor().getName(), store);
1016          if (store.isSloppyMemStore()) {
1017            hasSloppyStores = true;
1018          }
1019
1020          long storeMaxSequenceId = store.getMaxSequenceId().orElse(0L);
1021          maxSeqIdInStores.put(Bytes.toBytes(store.getColumnFamilyName()),
1022              storeMaxSequenceId);
1023          if (maxSeqId == -1 || storeMaxSequenceId > maxSeqId) {
1024            maxSeqId = storeMaxSequenceId;
1025          }
1026          long maxStoreMemstoreTS = store.getMaxMemStoreTS().orElse(0L);
1027          if (maxStoreMemstoreTS > maxMemstoreTS) {
1028            maxMemstoreTS = maxStoreMemstoreTS;
1029          }
1030        }
1031        allStoresOpened = true;
1032        if(hasSloppyStores) {
1033          htableDescriptor = TableDescriptorBuilder.newBuilder(htableDescriptor)
1034                  .setFlushPolicyClassName(FlushNonSloppyStoresFirstPolicy.class.getName())
1035                  .build();
1036          LOG.info("Setting FlushNonSloppyStoresFirstPolicy for the region=" + this);
1037        }
1038      } catch (InterruptedException e) {
1039        throw (InterruptedIOException)new InterruptedIOException().initCause(e);
1040      } catch (ExecutionException e) {
1041        throw new IOException(e.getCause());
1042      } finally {
1043        storeOpenerThreadPool.shutdownNow();
1044        if (!allStoresOpened) {
1045          // something went wrong, close all opened stores
1046          LOG.error("Could not initialize all stores for the region=" + this);
1047          for (HStore store : this.stores.values()) {
1048            try {
1049              store.close();
1050            } catch (IOException e) {
1051              LOG.warn("close store failed", e);
1052            }
1053          }
1054        }
1055      }
1056    }
1057    return Math.max(maxSeqId, maxMemstoreTS + 1);
1058  }
1059
1060  private void initializeWarmup(final CancelableProgressable reporter) throws IOException {
1061    MonitoredTask status = TaskMonitor.get().createStatus("Initializing region " + this);
1062    // Initialize all the HStores
1063    status.setStatus("Warming up all the Stores");
1064    try {
1065      initializeStores(reporter, status);
1066    } finally {
1067      status.markComplete("Done warming up.");
1068    }
1069  }
1070
1071  /**
1072   * @return Map of StoreFiles by column family
1073   */
1074  private NavigableMap<byte[], List<Path>> getStoreFiles() {
1075    NavigableMap<byte[], List<Path>> allStoreFiles = new TreeMap<>(Bytes.BYTES_COMPARATOR);
1076    for (HStore store : stores.values()) {
1077      Collection<HStoreFile> storeFiles = store.getStorefiles();
1078      if (storeFiles == null) {
1079        continue;
1080      }
1081      List<Path> storeFileNames = new ArrayList<>();
1082      for (HStoreFile storeFile : storeFiles) {
1083        storeFileNames.add(storeFile.getPath());
1084      }
1085      allStoreFiles.put(store.getColumnFamilyDescriptor().getName(), storeFileNames);
1086    }
1087    return allStoreFiles;
1088  }
1089
1090  private void writeRegionOpenMarker(WAL wal, long openSeqId) throws IOException {
1091    Map<byte[], List<Path>> storeFiles = getStoreFiles();
1092    RegionEventDescriptor regionOpenDesc = ProtobufUtil.toRegionEventDescriptor(
1093      RegionEventDescriptor.EventType.REGION_OPEN, getRegionInfo(), openSeqId,
1094      getRegionServerServices().getServerName(), storeFiles);
1095    WALUtil.writeRegionEventMarker(wal, getReplicationScope(), getRegionInfo(), regionOpenDesc,
1096        mvcc);
1097  }
1098
1099  private void writeRegionCloseMarker(WAL wal) throws IOException {
1100    Map<byte[], List<Path>> storeFiles = getStoreFiles();
1101    RegionEventDescriptor regionEventDesc = ProtobufUtil.toRegionEventDescriptor(
1102      RegionEventDescriptor.EventType.REGION_CLOSE, getRegionInfo(), mvcc.getReadPoint(),
1103      getRegionServerServices().getServerName(), storeFiles);
1104    WALUtil.writeRegionEventMarker(wal, getReplicationScope(), getRegionInfo(), regionEventDesc,
1105        mvcc);
1106
1107    // Store SeqId in HDFS when a region closes
1108    // checking region folder exists is due to many tests which delete the table folder while a
1109    // table is still online
1110    if (this.fs.getFileSystem().exists(this.fs.getRegionDir())) {
1111      WALSplitter.writeRegionSequenceIdFile(this.fs.getFileSystem(), this.fs.getRegionDir(),
1112        mvcc.getReadPoint());
1113    }
1114  }
1115
1116  /**
1117   * @return True if this region has references.
1118   */
1119  public boolean hasReferences() {
1120    return stores.values().stream().anyMatch(HStore::hasReferences);
1121  }
1122
1123  public void blockUpdates() {
1124    this.updatesLock.writeLock().lock();
1125  }
1126
1127  public void unblockUpdates() {
1128    this.updatesLock.writeLock().unlock();
1129  }
1130
1131  public HDFSBlocksDistribution getHDFSBlocksDistribution() {
1132    HDFSBlocksDistribution hdfsBlocksDistribution = new HDFSBlocksDistribution();
1133    stores.values().stream().filter(s -> s.getStorefiles() != null)
1134        .flatMap(s -> s.getStorefiles().stream()).map(HStoreFile::getHDFSBlockDistribution)
1135        .forEachOrdered(hdfsBlocksDistribution::add);
1136    return hdfsBlocksDistribution;
1137  }

1139  /**
1140   * This is a helper function to compute HDFS block distribution on demand
1141   * @param conf configuration
1142   * @param tableDescriptor TableDescriptor of the table
1143   * @param regionInfo encoded name of the region
1144   * @return The HDFS blocks distribution for the given region.
1145   * @throws IOException
1146   */
1147  public static HDFSBlocksDistribution computeHDFSBlocksDistribution(Configuration conf,
1148      TableDescriptor tableDescriptor, RegionInfo regionInfo) throws IOException {
1149    Path tablePath = FSUtils.getTableDir(FSUtils.getRootDir(conf), tableDescriptor.getTableName());
1150    return computeHDFSBlocksDistribution(conf, tableDescriptor, regionInfo, tablePath);
1151  }
1152
1153  /**
1154   * This is a helper function to compute HDFS block distribution on demand
1155   * @param conf configuration
1156   * @param tableDescriptor TableDescriptor of the table
1157   * @param regionInfo encoded name of the region
1158   * @param tablePath the table directory
1159   * @return The HDFS blocks distribution for the given region.
1160   * @throws IOException
1161   */
1162  public static HDFSBlocksDistribution computeHDFSBlocksDistribution(Configuration conf,
1163      TableDescriptor tableDescriptor, RegionInfo regionInfo, Path tablePath) throws IOException {
1164    HDFSBlocksDistribution hdfsBlocksDistribution = new HDFSBlocksDistribution();
1165    FileSystem fs = tablePath.getFileSystem(conf);
1166
1167    HRegionFileSystem regionFs = new HRegionFileSystem(conf, fs, tablePath, regionInfo);
1168    for (ColumnFamilyDescriptor family : tableDescriptor.getColumnFamilies()) {
1169      List<LocatedFileStatus> locatedFileStatusList = HRegionFileSystem
1170          .getStoreFilesLocatedStatus(regionFs, family.getNameAsString(), true);
1171      if (locatedFileStatusList == null) {
1172        continue;
1173      }
1174
1175      for (LocatedFileStatus status : locatedFileStatusList) {
1176        Path p = status.getPath();
1177        if (StoreFileInfo.isReference(p) || HFileLink.isHFileLink(p)) {
1178          // Only construct StoreFileInfo object if its not a hfile, save obj
1179          // creation
1180          StoreFileInfo storeFileInfo = new StoreFileInfo(conf, fs, status);
1181          hdfsBlocksDistribution.add(storeFileInfo
1182              .computeHDFSBlocksDistribution(fs));
1183        } else if (StoreFileInfo.isHFile(p)) {
1184          // If its a HFile, then lets just add to the block distribution
1185          // lets not create more objects here, not even another HDFSBlocksDistribution
1186          FSUtils.addToHDFSBlocksDistribution(hdfsBlocksDistribution,
1187              status.getBlockLocations());
1188        } else {
1189          throw new IOException("path=" + p
1190              + " doesn't look like a valid StoreFile");
1191        }
1192      }
1193    }
1194    return hdfsBlocksDistribution;
1195  }
1196
1197  /**
1198   * Increase the size of mem store in this region and the size of global mem
1199   * store
1200   */
1201  public void incMemStoreSize(MemStoreSize memStoreSize) {
1202    if (this.rsAccounting != null) {
1203      rsAccounting.incGlobalMemStoreSize(memStoreSize);
1204    }
1205    long dataSize;
1206    synchronized (this.memStoreSize) {
1207      this.memStoreSize.incMemStoreSize(memStoreSize);
1208      dataSize = this.memStoreSize.getDataSize();
1209    }
1210    checkNegativeMemStoreDataSize(dataSize, memStoreSize.getDataSize());
1211  }
1212
1213  public void decrMemStoreSize(MemStoreSize memStoreSize) {
1214    if (this.rsAccounting != null) {
1215      rsAccounting.decGlobalMemStoreSize(memStoreSize);
1216    }
1217    long size;
1218    synchronized (this.memStoreSize) {
1219      this.memStoreSize.decMemStoreSize(memStoreSize);
1220      size = this.memStoreSize.getDataSize();
1221    }
1222    checkNegativeMemStoreDataSize(size, -memStoreSize.getDataSize());
1223  }
1224
1225  private void checkNegativeMemStoreDataSize(long memStoreDataSize, long delta) {
1226    // This is extremely bad if we make memStoreSize negative. Log as much info on the offending
1227    // caller as possible. (memStoreSize might be a negative value already -- freeing memory)
1228    if (memStoreDataSize < 0) {
1229      LOG.error("Asked to modify this region's (" + this.toString()
1230          + ") memStoreSize to a negative value which is incorrect. Current memStoreSize="
1231          + (memStoreDataSize - delta) + ", delta=" + delta, new Exception());
1232    }
1233  }

1340  @Override
1341  public boolean isMergeable() {
1342    if (!isAvailable()) {
1343      LOG.debug("Region " + this
1344          + " is not mergeable because it is closing or closed");
1345      return false;
1346    }
1347    if (hasReferences()) {
1348      LOG.debug("Region " + this
1349          + " is not mergeable because it has references");
1350      return false;
1351    }
1352
1353    return true;
1354  }

1387  /**
1388   * Close down this HRegion.  Flush the cache, shut down each HStore, don't
1389   * service any more calls.
1390   *
1391   * <p>This method could take some time to execute, so don't call it from a
1392   * time-sensitive thread.
1393   *
1394   * @return Vector of all the storage files that the HRegion's component
1395   * HStores make use of.  It's a list of all StoreFile objects. Returns empty
1396   * vector if already closed and null if judged that it should not close.
1397   *
1398   * @throws IOException e
1399   * @throws DroppedSnapshotException Thrown when replay of wal is required
1400   * because a Snapshot was not properly persisted. The region is put in closing mode, and the
1401   * caller MUST abort after this.
1402   */
1403  public Map<byte[], List<HStoreFile>> close() throws IOException {
1404    return close(false);
1405  }
1406
1407  private final Object closeLock = new Object();
1408
1409  /** Conf key for the periodic flush interval */
1410  public static final String MEMSTORE_PERIODIC_FLUSH_INTERVAL =
1411      "hbase.regionserver.optionalcacheflushinterval";
1412  /** Default interval for the memstore flush */
1413  public static final int DEFAULT_CACHE_FLUSH_INTERVAL = 3600000;
1414  /** Default interval for System tables memstore flush */
1415  public static final int SYSTEM_CACHE_FLUSH_INTERVAL = 300000; // 5 minutes
1416
1417  /** Conf key to force a flush if there are already enough changes for one region in memstore */
1418  public static final String MEMSTORE_FLUSH_PER_CHANGES =
1419      "hbase.regionserver.flush.per.changes";
1420  public static final long DEFAULT_FLUSH_PER_CHANGES = 30000000; // 30 millions
1421  /**
1422   * The following MAX_FLUSH_PER_CHANGES is large enough because each KeyValue has 20+ bytes
1423   * overhead. Therefore, even 1G empty KVs occupy at least 20GB memstore size for a single region
1424   */
1425  public static final long MAX_FLUSH_PER_CHANGES = 1000000000; // 1G
1426
1427  /**
1428   * Close down this HRegion.  Flush the cache unless abort parameter is true,
1429   * Shut down each HStore, don't service any more calls.
1430   *
1431   * This method could take some time to execute, so don't call it from a
1432   * time-sensitive thread.
1433   *
1434   * @param abort true if server is aborting (only during testing)
1435   * @return Vector of all the storage files that the HRegion's component
1436   * HStores make use of.  It's a list of StoreFile objects.  Can be null if
1437   * we are not to close at this time or we are already closed.
1438   *
1439   * @throws IOException e
1440   * @throws DroppedSnapshotException Thrown when replay of wal is required
1441   * because a Snapshot was not properly persisted. The region is put in closing mode, and the
1442   * caller MUST abort after this.
1443   */
1444  public Map<byte[], List<HStoreFile>> close(boolean abort) throws IOException {
1445    // Only allow one thread to close at a time. Serialize them so dual
1446    // threads attempting to close will run up against each other.
1447    MonitoredTask status = TaskMonitor.get().createStatus(
1448        "Closing region " + this +
1449        (abort ? " due to abort" : ""));
1450
1451    status.setStatus("Waiting for close lock");
1452    try {
1453      synchronized (closeLock) {
1454        return doClose(abort, status);
1455      }
1456    } finally {
1457      status.cleanup();
1458    }
1459  }
1460
1461  /**
1462   * Exposed for some very specific unit tests.
1463   */
1464  @VisibleForTesting
1465  public void setClosing(boolean closing) {
1466    this.closing.set(closing);
1467  }
1468
1469  /**
1470   * The {@link HRegion#doClose} will block forever if someone tries proving the dead lock via the unit test.
1471   * Instead of blocking, the {@link HRegion#doClose} will throw exception if you set the timeout.
1472   * @param timeoutForWriteLock the second time to wait for the write lock in {@link HRegion#doClose}
1473   */
1474  @VisibleForTesting
1475  public void setTimeoutForWriteLock(long timeoutForWriteLock) {
1476    assert timeoutForWriteLock >= 0;
1477    this.timeoutForWriteLock = timeoutForWriteLock;
1478  }
1479
1480  @edu.umd.cs.findbugs.annotations.SuppressWarnings(value="UL_UNRELEASED_LOCK_EXCEPTION_PATH",
1481      justification="I think FindBugs is confused")
1482  private Map<byte[], List<HStoreFile>> doClose(boolean abort, MonitoredTask status)
1483      throws IOException {
1484    if (isClosed()) {
1485      LOG.warn("Region " + this + " already closed");
1486      return null;
1487    }
1488
1489    if (coprocessorHost != null) {
1490      status.setStatus("Running coprocessor pre-close hooks");
1491      this.coprocessorHost.preClose(abort);
1492    }
1493    status.setStatus("Disabling compacts and flushes for region");
1494    boolean canFlush = true;
1495    synchronized (writestate) {
1496      // Disable compacting and flushing by background threads for this
1497      // region.
1498      canFlush = !writestate.readOnly;
1499      writestate.writesEnabled = false;
1500      LOG.debug("Closing " + this + ": disabling compactions & flushes");
1501      waitForFlushesAndCompactions();
1502    }
1503    // If we were not just flushing, is it worth doing a preflush...one
1504    // that will clear out of the bulk of the memstore before we put up
1505    // the close flag?
1506    if (!abort && worthPreFlushing() && canFlush) {
1507      status.setStatus("Pre-flushing region before close");
1508      LOG.info("Running close preflush of " + this);
1509      try {
1510        internalFlushcache(status);
1511      } catch (IOException ioe) {
1512        // Failed to flush the region. Keep going.
1513        status.setStatus("Failed pre-flush " + this + "; " + ioe.getMessage());
1514      }
1515    }
1516
1517    if (timeoutForWriteLock == null
1518        || timeoutForWriteLock == Long.MAX_VALUE) {
1519      // block waiting for the lock for closing
1520      lock.writeLock().lock(); // FindBugs: Complains UL_UNRELEASED_LOCK_EXCEPTION_PATH but seems fine
1521    } else {
1522      try {
1523        boolean succeed = lock.writeLock().tryLock(timeoutForWriteLock, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
1524        if (!succeed) {
1525          throw new IOException("Failed to get write lock when closing region");
1526        }
1527      } catch (InterruptedException e) {
1528        throw (InterruptedIOException) new InterruptedIOException().initCause(e);
1529      }
1530    }
1531    this.closing.set(true);
1532    status.setStatus("Disabling writes for close");
1533    try {
1534      if (this.isClosed()) {
1535        status.abort("Already got closed by another process");
1536        // SplitTransaction handles the null
1537        return null;
1538      }
1539      LOG.debug("Updates disabled for region " + this);
1540      // Don't flush the cache if we are aborting
1541      if (!abort && canFlush) {
1542        int failedfFlushCount = 0;
1543        int flushCount = 0;
1544        long tmp = 0;
1545        long remainingSize = this.memStoreSize.getDataSize();
1546        while (remainingSize > 0) {
1547          try {
1548            internalFlushcache(status);
1549            if(flushCount >0) {
1550              LOG.info("Running extra flush, " + flushCount +
1551                  " (carrying snapshot?) " + this);
1552            }
1553            flushCount++;
1554            tmp = this.memStoreSize.getDataSize();
1555            if (tmp >= remainingSize) {
1556              failedfFlushCount++;
1557            }
1558            remainingSize = tmp;
1559            if (failedfFlushCount > 5) {
1560              // If we failed 5 times and are unable to clear memory, abort
1561              // so we do not lose data
1562              throw new DroppedSnapshotException("Failed clearing memory after " +
1563                  flushCount + " attempts on region: " +
1564                  Bytes.toStringBinary(getRegionInfo().getRegionName()));
1565            }
1566          } catch (IOException ioe) {
1567            status.setStatus("Failed flush " + this + ", putting online again");
1568            synchronized (writestate) {
1569              writestate.writesEnabled = true;
1570            }
1571            // Have to throw to upper layers.  I can't abort server from here.
1572            throw ioe;
1573          }
1574        }
1575      }
1576
1577      Map<byte[], List<HStoreFile>> result = new TreeMap<>(Bytes.BYTES_COMPARATOR);
1578      if (!stores.isEmpty()) {
1579        // initialize the thread pool for closing stores in parallel.
1580        ThreadPoolExecutor storeCloserThreadPool =
1581          getStoreOpenAndCloseThreadPool("StoreCloserThread-" +
1582            getRegionInfo().getRegionNameAsString());
1583        CompletionService<Pair<byte[], Collection<HStoreFile>>> completionService =
1584          new ExecutorCompletionService<>(storeCloserThreadPool);
1585
1586        // close each store in parallel
1587        for (HStore store : stores.values()) {
1588          MemStoreSize flushableSize = store.getFlushableSize();
1589          if (!(abort || flushableSize.getDataSize() == 0 || writestate.readOnly)) {
1590            if (getRegionServerServices() != null) {
1591              getRegionServerServices().abort("Assertion failed while closing store "
1592                + getRegionInfo().getRegionNameAsString() + " " + store
1593                + ". flushableSize expected=0, actual= " + flushableSize
1594                + ". Current memStoreSize=" + getMemStoreDataSize() + ". Maybe a coprocessor "
1595                + "operation failed and left the memstore in a partially updated state.", null);
1596            }
1597          }
1598          completionService
1599              .submit(new Callable<Pair<byte[], Collection<HStoreFile>>>() {
1600                @Override
1601                public Pair<byte[], Collection<HStoreFile>> call() throws IOException {
1602                  return new Pair<>(store.getColumnFamilyDescriptor().getName(), store.close());
1603                }
1604              });
1605        }
1606        try {
1607          for (int i = 0; i < stores.size(); i++) {
1608            Future<Pair<byte[], Collection<HStoreFile>>> future = completionService.take();
1609            Pair<byte[], Collection<HStoreFile>> storeFiles = future.get();
1610            List<HStoreFile> familyFiles = result.get(storeFiles.getFirst());
1611            if (familyFiles == null) {
1612              familyFiles = new ArrayList<>();
1613              result.put(storeFiles.getFirst(), familyFiles);
1614            }
1615            familyFiles.addAll(storeFiles.getSecond());
1616          }
1617        } catch (InterruptedException e) {
1618          throw (InterruptedIOException)new InterruptedIOException().initCause(e);
1619        } catch (ExecutionException e) {
1620          Throwable cause = e.getCause();
1621          if (cause instanceof IOException) {
1622            throw (IOException) cause;
1623          }
1624          throw new IOException(cause);
1625        } finally {
1626          storeCloserThreadPool.shutdownNow();
1627        }
1628      }
1629
1630      status.setStatus("Writing region close event to WAL");
1631      if (!abort && wal != null && getRegionServerServices() != null && !writestate.readOnly) {
1632        writeRegionCloseMarker(wal);
1633      }
1634
1635      this.closed.set(true);
1636      if (!canFlush) {
1637        this.decrMemStoreSize(new MemStoreSize(memStoreSize));
1638      } else if (memStoreSize.getDataSize() != 0) {
1639        LOG.error("Memstore data size is " + memStoreSize.getDataSize());
1640      }
1641      if (coprocessorHost != null) {
1642        status.setStatus("Running coprocessor post-close hooks");
1643        this.coprocessorHost.postClose(abort);
1644      }
1645      if (this.metricsRegion != null) {
1646        this.metricsRegion.close();
1647      }
1648      if (this.metricsRegionWrapper != null) {
1649        Closeables.close(this.metricsRegionWrapper, true);
1650      }
1651      status.markComplete("Closed");
1652      LOG.info("Closed " + this);
1653      return result;
1654    } finally {
1655      lock.writeLock().unlock();
1656    }
1657  }
1658
1659  /** Wait for all current flushes and compactions of the region to complete */
1660  // TODO HBASE-18906. Check the usage (if any) in Phoenix and expose this or give alternate way for
1661  // Phoenix needs.
1662  public void waitForFlushesAndCompactions() {
1663    synchronized (writestate) {
1664      if (this.writestate.readOnly) {
1665        // we should not wait for replayed flushed if we are read only (for example in case the
1666        // region is a secondary replica).
1667        return;
1668      }
1669      boolean interrupted = false;
1670      try {
1671        while (writestate.compacting.get() > 0 || writestate.flushing) {
1672          LOG.debug("waiting for " + writestate.compacting + " compactions"
1673            + (writestate.flushing ? " & cache flush" : "") + " to complete for region " + this);
1674          try {
1675            writestate.wait();
1676          } catch (InterruptedException iex) {
1677            // essentially ignore and propagate the interrupt back up
1678            LOG.warn("Interrupted while waiting");
1679            interrupted = true;
1680            break;
1681          }
1682        }
1683      } finally {
1684        if (interrupted) {
1685          Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
1686        }
1687      }
1688    }
1689  }
1690
1691  /**
1692   * Wait for all current flushes of the region to complete
1693   */
1694  public void waitForFlushes() {
1695    waitForFlushes(0);// Unbound wait
1696  }
1697
1698  @Override
1699  public boolean waitForFlushes(long timeout) {
1700    synchronized (writestate) {
1701      if (this.writestate.readOnly) {
1702        // we should not wait for replayed flushed if we are read only (for example in case the
1703        // region is a secondary replica).
1704        return true;
1705      }
1706      if (!writestate.flushing) return true;
1707      long start = System.currentTimeMillis();
1708      long duration = 0;
1709      boolean interrupted = false;
1710      LOG.debug("waiting for cache flush to complete for region " + this);
1711      try {
1712        while (writestate.flushing) {
1713          if (timeout > 0 && duration >= timeout) break;
1714          try {
1715            long toWait = timeout == 0 ? 0 : (timeout - duration);
1716            writestate.wait(toWait);
1717          } catch (InterruptedException iex) {
1718            // essentially ignore and propagate the interrupt back up
1719            LOG.warn("Interrupted while waiting");
1720            interrupted = true;
1721            break;
1722          } finally {
1723            duration = System.currentTimeMillis() - start;
1724          }
1725        }
1726      } finally {
1727        if (interrupted) {
1728          Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
1729        }
1730      }
1731      LOG.debug("Waited " + duration + " ms for flush to complete");
1732      return !(writestate.flushing);
1733    }
1734  }
1735
1736  protected ThreadPoolExecutor getStoreOpenAndCloseThreadPool(
1737      final String threadNamePrefix) {
1738    int numStores = Math.max(1, this.htableDescriptor.getColumnFamilyCount());
1739    int maxThreads = Math.min(numStores,
1740        conf.getInt(HConstants.HSTORE_OPEN_AND_CLOSE_THREADS_MAX,
1741            HConstants.DEFAULT_HSTORE_OPEN_AND_CLOSE_THREADS_MAX));
1742    return getOpenAndCloseThreadPool(maxThreads, threadNamePrefix);
1743  }
1744
1745  protected ThreadPoolExecutor getStoreFileOpenAndCloseThreadPool(
1746      final String threadNamePrefix) {
1747    int numStores = Math.max(1, this.htableDescriptor.getColumnFamilyCount());
1748    int maxThreads = Math.max(1,
1749        conf.getInt(HConstants.HSTORE_OPEN_AND_CLOSE_THREADS_MAX,
1750            HConstants.DEFAULT_HSTORE_OPEN_AND_CLOSE_THREADS_MAX)
1751            / numStores);
1752    return getOpenAndCloseThreadPool(maxThreads, threadNamePrefix);
1753  }
1754
1755  static ThreadPoolExecutor getOpenAndCloseThreadPool(int maxThreads,
1756      final String threadNamePrefix) {
1757    return Threads.getBoundedCachedThreadPool(maxThreads, 30L, TimeUnit.SECONDS,
1758      new ThreadFactory() {
1759        private int count = 1;
1760
1761        @Override
1762        public Thread newThread(Runnable r) {
1763          return new Thread(r, threadNamePrefix + "-" + count++);
1764        }
1765      });
1766  }
1767
1768   /**
1769    * @return True if its worth doing a flush before we put up the close flag.
1770    */
1771  private boolean worthPreFlushing() {
1772    return this.memStoreSize.getDataSize() >
1773      this.conf.getLong("hbase.hregion.preclose.flush.size", 1024 * 1024 * 5);
1774  }

1802  /**
1803   * A split takes the config from the parent region & passes it to the daughter
1804   * region's constructor. If 'conf' was passed, you would end up using the HTD
1805   * of the parent region in addition to the new daughter HTD. Pass 'baseConf'
1806   * to the daughter regions to avoid this tricky dedupe problem.
1807   * @return Configuration object
1808   */
1809  Configuration getBaseConf() {
1810    return this.baseConf;
1811  }
1812
1813  /** @return {@link FileSystem} being used by this region */
1814  public FileSystem getFilesystem() {
1815    return fs.getFileSystem();
1816  }
1817
1818  /** @return the {@link HRegionFileSystem} used by this region */
1819  public HRegionFileSystem getRegionFileSystem() {
1820    return this.fs;
1821  }
1822
1823  @Override
1824  public long getEarliestFlushTimeForAllStores() {
1825    return Collections.min(lastStoreFlushTimeMap.values());
1826  }
1827
1828  @Override
1829  public long getOldestHfileTs(boolean majorCompactionOnly) throws IOException {
1830    long result = Long.MAX_VALUE;
1831    for (HStore store : stores.values()) {
1832      Collection<HStoreFile> storeFiles = store.getStorefiles();
1833      if (storeFiles == null) {
1834        continue;
1835      }
1836      for (HStoreFile file : storeFiles) {
1837        StoreFileReader sfReader = file.getReader();
1838        if (sfReader == null) {
1839          continue;
1840        }
1841        HFile.Reader reader = sfReader.getHFileReader();
1842        if (reader == null) {
1843          continue;
1844        }
1845        if (majorCompactionOnly) {
1846          byte[] val = reader.loadFileInfo().get(MAJOR_COMPACTION_KEY);
1847          if (val == null || !Bytes.toBoolean(val)) {
1848            continue;
1849          }
1850        }
1851        result = Math.min(result, reader.getFileContext().getFileCreateTime());
1852      }
1853    }
1854    return result == Long.MAX_VALUE ? 0 : result;
1855  }
1856
1857  RegionLoad.Builder setCompleteSequenceId(RegionLoad.Builder regionLoadBldr) {
1858    long lastFlushOpSeqIdLocal = this.lastFlushOpSeqId;
1859    byte[] encodedRegionName = this.getRegionInfo().getEncodedNameAsBytes();
1860    regionLoadBldr.clearStoreCompleteSequenceId();
1861    for (byte[] familyName : this.stores.keySet()) {
1862      long earliest = this.wal.getEarliestMemStoreSeqNum(encodedRegionName, familyName);
1863      // Subtract - 1 to go earlier than the current oldest, unflushed edit in memstore; this will
1864      // give us a sequence id that is for sure flushed. We want edit replay to start after this
1865      // sequence id in this region. If NO_SEQNUM, use the regions maximum flush id.
1866      long csid = (earliest == HConstants.NO_SEQNUM)? lastFlushOpSeqIdLocal: earliest - 1;
1867      regionLoadBldr.addStoreCompleteSequenceId(StoreSequenceId.newBuilder()
1868          .setFamilyName(UnsafeByteOperations.unsafeWrap(familyName)).setSequenceId(csid).build());
1869    }
1870    return regionLoadBldr.setCompleteSequenceId(getMaxFlushedSeqId());
1871  }
