1873  //////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
1874  // HRegion maintenance.
1875  //
1876  // These methods are meant to be called periodically by the HRegionServer for
1877  // upkeep.
1878  //////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
1879  /**
1880   * Do preparation for pending compaction.
1881   * @throws IOException
1882   */
1883  protected void doRegionCompactionPrep() throws IOException {
1884  }
1885
1886  /**
1887   * Synchronously compact all stores in the region.
1888   * <p>This operation could block for a long time, so don't call it from a
1889   * time-sensitive thread.
1890   * <p>Note that no locks are taken to prevent possible conflicts between
1891   * compaction and splitting activities. The regionserver does not normally compact
1892   * and split in parallel. However by calling this method you may introduce
1893   * unexpected and unhandled concurrency. Don't do this unless you know what
1894   * you are doing.
1895   *
1896   * @param majorCompaction True to force a major compaction regardless of thresholds
1897   * @throws IOException
1898   */
1899  public void compact(boolean majorCompaction) throws IOException {
1900    if (majorCompaction) {
1901      stores.values().forEach(HStore::triggerMajorCompaction);
1902    }
1903    for (HStore s : stores.values()) {
1904      Optional<CompactionContext> compaction = s.requestCompaction();
1905      if (compaction.isPresent()) {
1906        ThroughputController controller = null;
1907        if (rsServices != null) {
1908          controller = CompactionThroughputControllerFactory.create(rsServices, conf);
1909        }
1910        if (controller == null) {
1911          controller = NoLimitThroughputController.INSTANCE;
1912        }
1913        compact(compaction.get(), s, controller, null);
1914      }
1915    }
1916  }
1917
1918  /**
1919   * This is a helper function that compact all the stores synchronously.
1920   * <p>
1921   * It is used by utilities and testing
1922   */
1923  @VisibleForTesting
1924  public void compactStores() throws IOException {
1925    for (HStore s : stores.values()) {
1926      Optional<CompactionContext> compaction = s.requestCompaction();
1927      if (compaction.isPresent()) {
1928        compact(compaction.get(), s, NoLimitThroughputController.INSTANCE, null);
1929      }
1930    }
1931  }
1932
1933  /**
1934   * This is a helper function that compact the given store.
1935   * <p>
1936   * It is used by utilities and testing
1937   */
1938  @VisibleForTesting
1939  void compactStore(byte[] family, ThroughputController throughputController) throws IOException {
1940    HStore s = getStore(family);
1941    Optional<CompactionContext> compaction = s.requestCompaction();
1942    if (compaction.isPresent()) {
1943      compact(compaction.get(), s, throughputController, null);
1944    }
1945  }
1946
1947  /**
1948   * Called by compaction thread and after region is opened to compact the
1949   * HStores if necessary.
1950   *
1951   * <p>This operation could block for a long time, so don't call it from a
1952   * time-sensitive thread.
1953   *
1954   * Note that no locking is necessary at this level because compaction only
1955   * conflicts with a region split, and that cannot happen because the region
1956   * server does them sequentially and not in parallel.
1957   *
1958   * @param compaction Compaction details, obtained by requestCompaction()
1959   * @param throughputController
1960   * @return whether the compaction completed
1961   */
1962  public boolean compact(CompactionContext compaction, HStore store,
1963      ThroughputController throughputController) throws IOException {
1964    return compact(compaction, store, throughputController, null);
1965  }
1966
1967  public boolean compact(CompactionContext compaction, HStore store,
1968      ThroughputController throughputController, User user) throws IOException {
1969    assert compaction != null && compaction.hasSelection();
1970    assert !compaction.getRequest().getFiles().isEmpty();
1971    if (this.closing.get() || this.closed.get()) {
1972      LOG.debug("Skipping compaction on " + this + " because closing/closed");
1973      store.cancelRequestedCompaction(compaction);
1974      return false;
1975    }
1976    MonitoredTask status = null;
1977    boolean requestNeedsCancellation = true;
1978    /*
1979     * We are trying to remove / relax the region read lock for compaction.
1980     * Let's see what are the potential race conditions among the operations (user scan,
1981     * region split, region close and region bulk load).
1982     *
1983     *  user scan ---> region read lock
1984     *  region split --> region close first --> region write lock
1985     *  region close --> region write lock
1986     *  region bulk load --> region write lock
1987     *
1988     * read lock is compatible with read lock. ---> no problem with user scan/read
1989     * region bulk load does not cause problem for compaction (no consistency problem, store lock
1990     *  will help the store file accounting).
1991     * They can run almost concurrently at the region level.
1992     *
1993     * The only remaining race condition is between the region close and compaction.
1994     * So we will evaluate, below, how region close intervenes with compaction if compaction does
1995     * not acquire region read lock.
1996     *
1997     * Here are the steps for compaction:
1998     * 1. obtain list of StoreFile's
1999     * 2. create StoreFileScanner's based on list from #1
2000     * 3. perform compaction and save resulting files under tmp dir
2001     * 4. swap in compacted files
2002     *
2003     * #1 is guarded by store lock. This patch does not change this --> no worse or better
2004     * For #2, we obtain smallest read point (for region) across all the Scanners (for both default
2005     * compactor and stripe compactor).
2006     * The read points are for user scans. Region keeps the read points for all currently open
2007     * user scanners.
2008     * Compaction needs to know the smallest read point so that during re-write of the hfiles,
2009     * it can remove the mvcc points for the cells if their mvccs are older than the smallest
2010     * since they are not needed anymore.
2011     * This will not conflict with compaction.
2012     * For #3, it can be performed in parallel to other operations.
2013     * For #4 bulk load and compaction don't conflict with each other on the region level
2014     *   (for multi-family atomicy).
2015     * Region close and compaction are guarded pretty well by the 'writestate'.
2016     * In HRegion#doClose(), we have :
2017     * synchronized (writestate) {
2018     *   // Disable compacting and flushing by background threads for this
2019     *   // region.
2020     *   canFlush = !writestate.readOnly;
2021     *   writestate.writesEnabled = false;
2022     *   LOG.debug("Closing " + this + ": disabling compactions & flushes");
2023     *   waitForFlushesAndCompactions();
2024     * }
2025     * waitForFlushesAndCompactions() would wait for writestate.compacting to come down to 0.
2026     * and in HRegion.compact()
2027     *  try {
2028     *    synchronized (writestate) {
2029     *    if (writestate.writesEnabled) {
2030     *      wasStateSet = true;
2031     *      ++writestate.compacting;
2032     *    } else {
2033     *      String msg = "NOT compacting region " + this + ". Writes disabled.";
2034     *      LOG.info(msg);
2035     *      status.abort(msg);
2036     *      return false;
2037     *    }
2038     *  }
2039     * Also in compactor.performCompaction():
2040     * check periodically to see if a system stop is requested
2041     * if (closeCheckInterval > 0) {
2042     *   bytesWritten += len;
2043     *   if (bytesWritten > closeCheckInterval) {
2044     *     bytesWritten = 0;
2045     *     if (!store.areWritesEnabled()) {
2046     *       progress.cancel();
2047     *       return false;
2048     *     }
2049     *   }
2050     * }
2051     */
2052    try {
2053      byte[] cf = Bytes.toBytes(store.getColumnFamilyName());
2054      if (stores.get(cf) != store) {
2055        LOG.warn("Store " + store.getColumnFamilyName() + " on region " + this
2056            + " has been re-instantiated, cancel this compaction request. "
2057            + " It may be caused by the roll back of split transaction");
2058        return false;
2059      }
2060
2061      status = TaskMonitor.get().createStatus("Compacting " + store + " in " + this);
2062      if (this.closed.get()) {
2063        String msg = "Skipping compaction on " + this + " because closed";
2064        LOG.debug(msg);
2065        status.abort(msg);
2066        return false;
2067      }
2068      boolean wasStateSet = false;
2069      try {
2070        synchronized (writestate) {
2071          if (writestate.writesEnabled) {
2072            wasStateSet = true;
2073            writestate.compacting.incrementAndGet();
2074          } else {
2075            String msg = "NOT compacting region " + this + ". Writes disabled.";
2076            LOG.info(msg);
2077            status.abort(msg);
2078            return false;
2079          }
2080        }
2081        LOG.info("Starting compaction on " + store + " in region " + this
2082            + (compaction.getRequest().isOffPeak()?" as an off-peak compaction":""));
2083        doRegionCompactionPrep();
2084        try {
2085          status.setStatus("Compacting store " + store);
2086          // We no longer need to cancel the request on the way out of this
2087          // method because Store#compact will clean up unconditionally
2088          requestNeedsCancellation = false;
2089          store.compact(compaction, throughputController, user);
2090        } catch (InterruptedIOException iioe) {
2091          String msg = "compaction interrupted";
2092          LOG.info(msg, iioe);
2093          status.abort(msg);
2094          return false;
2095        }
2096      } finally {
2097        if (wasStateSet) {
2098          synchronized (writestate) {
2099            writestate.compacting.decrementAndGet();
2100            if (writestate.compacting.get() <= 0) {
2101              writestate.notifyAll();
2102            }
2103          }
2104        }
2105      }
2106      status.markComplete("Compaction complete");
2107      return true;
2108    } finally {
2109      if (requestNeedsCancellation) store.cancelRequestedCompaction(compaction);
2110      if (status != null) status.cleanup();
2111    }
2112  }
2113
2114  /**
2115   * Flush the cache.
2116   *
2117   * <p>When this method is called the cache will be flushed unless:
2118   * <ol>
2119   *   <li>the cache is empty</li>
2120   *   <li>the region is closed.</li>
2121   *   <li>a flush is already in progress</li>
2122   *   <li>writes are disabled</li>
2123   * </ol>
2124   *
2125   * <p>This method may block for some time, so it should not be called from a
2126   * time-sensitive thread.
2127   * @param force whether we want to force a flush of all stores
2128   * @return FlushResult indicating whether the flush was successful or not and if
2129   * the region needs compacting
2130   *
2131   * @throws IOException general io exceptions
2132   * because a snapshot was not properly persisted.
2133   */
2134  // TODO HBASE-18905. We might have to expose a requestFlush API for CPs
2135  public FlushResult flush(boolean force) throws IOException {
2136    return flushcache(force, false, FlushLifeCycleTracker.DUMMY);
2137  }
2138
2139  public interface FlushResult {
2140    enum Result {
2141      FLUSHED_NO_COMPACTION_NEEDED,
2142      FLUSHED_COMPACTION_NEEDED,
2143      // Special case where a flush didn't run because there's nothing in the memstores. Used when
2144      // bulk loading to know when we can still load even if a flush didn't happen.
2145      CANNOT_FLUSH_MEMSTORE_EMPTY,
2146      CANNOT_FLUSH
2147    }
2148
2149    /** @return the detailed result code */
2150    Result getResult();
2151
2152    /** @return true if the memstores were flushed, else false */
2153    boolean isFlushSucceeded();
2154
2155    /** @return True if the flush requested a compaction, else false */
2156    boolean isCompactionNeeded();
2157  }
2158
2159  /**
2160   * Flush the cache.
2161   *
2162   * When this method is called the cache will be flushed unless:
2163   * <ol>
2164   *   <li>the cache is empty</li>
2165   *   <li>the region is closed.</li>
2166   *   <li>a flush is already in progress</li>
2167   *   <li>writes are disabled</li>
2168   * </ol>
2169   *
2170   * <p>This method may block for some time, so it should not be called from a
2171   * time-sensitive thread.
2172   * @param forceFlushAllStores whether we want to flush all stores
2173   * @param writeFlushRequestWalMarker whether to write the flush request marker to WAL
2174   * @param tracker used to track the life cycle of this flush
2175   * @return whether the flush is success and whether the region needs compacting
2176   *
2177   * @throws IOException general io exceptions
2178   * @throws DroppedSnapshotException Thrown when replay of wal is required
2179   * because a Snapshot was not properly persisted. The region is put in closing mode, and the
2180   * caller MUST abort after this.
2181   */
2182  public FlushResultImpl flushcache(boolean forceFlushAllStores, boolean writeFlushRequestWalMarker,
2183      FlushLifeCycleTracker tracker) throws IOException {
2184    // fail-fast instead of waiting on the lock
2185    if (this.closing.get()) {
2186      String msg = "Skipping flush on " + this + " because closing";
2187      LOG.debug(msg);
2188      return new FlushResultImpl(FlushResult.Result.CANNOT_FLUSH, msg, false);
2189    }
2190    MonitoredTask status = TaskMonitor.get().createStatus("Flushing " + this);
2191    status.setStatus("Acquiring readlock on region");
2192    // block waiting for the lock for flushing cache
2193    lock.readLock().lock();
2194    try {
2195      if (this.closed.get()) {
2196        String msg = "Skipping flush on " + this + " because closed";
2197        LOG.debug(msg);
2198        status.abort(msg);
2199        return new FlushResultImpl(FlushResult.Result.CANNOT_FLUSH, msg, false);
2200      }
2201      if (coprocessorHost != null) {
2202        status.setStatus("Running coprocessor pre-flush hooks");
2203        coprocessorHost.preFlush(tracker);
2204      }
2205      // TODO: this should be managed within memstore with the snapshot, updated only after flush
2206      // successful
2207      if (numMutationsWithoutWAL.sum() > 0) {
2208        numMutationsWithoutWAL.reset();
2209        dataInMemoryWithoutWAL.reset();
2210      }
2211      synchronized (writestate) {
2212        if (!writestate.flushing && writestate.writesEnabled) {
2213          this.writestate.flushing = true;
2214        } else {
2215          if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
2216            LOG.debug("NOT flushing memstore for region " + this
2217                + ", flushing=" + writestate.flushing + ", writesEnabled="
2218                + writestate.writesEnabled);
2219          }
2220          String msg = "Not flushing since "
2221              + (writestate.flushing ? "already flushing"
2222              : "writes not enabled");
2223          status.abort(msg);
2224          return new FlushResultImpl(FlushResult.Result.CANNOT_FLUSH, msg, false);
2225        }
2226      }
2227
2228      try {
2229        Collection<HStore> specificStoresToFlush =
2230            forceFlushAllStores ? stores.values() : flushPolicy.selectStoresToFlush();
2231        FlushResultImpl fs =
2232            internalFlushcache(specificStoresToFlush, status, writeFlushRequestWalMarker, tracker);
2233
2234        if (coprocessorHost != null) {
2235          status.setStatus("Running post-flush coprocessor hooks");
2236          coprocessorHost.postFlush(tracker);
2237        }
2238
2239        if(fs.isFlushSucceeded()) {
2240          flushesQueued.reset();
2241        }
2242
2243        status.markComplete("Flush successful");
2244        return fs;
2245      } finally {
2246        synchronized (writestate) {
2247          writestate.flushing = false;
2248          this.writestate.flushRequested = false;
2249          writestate.notifyAll();
2250        }
2251      }
2252    } finally {
2253      lock.readLock().unlock();
2254      status.cleanup();
2255    }
2256  }
2257
2258  /**
2259   * Should the store be flushed because it is old enough.
2260   * <p>
2261   * Every FlushPolicy should call this to determine whether a store is old enough to flush (except
2262   * that you always flush all stores). Otherwise the method will always
2263   * returns true which will make a lot of flush requests.
2264   */
2265  boolean shouldFlushStore(HStore store) {
2266    long earliest = this.wal.getEarliestMemStoreSeqNum(getRegionInfo().getEncodedNameAsBytes(),
2267      store.getColumnFamilyDescriptor().getName()) - 1;
2268    if (earliest > 0 && earliest + flushPerChanges < mvcc.getReadPoint()) {
2269      if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
2270        LOG.debug("Flush column family " + store.getColumnFamilyName() + " of " +
2271          getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " because unflushed sequenceid=" + earliest +
2272          " is > " + this.flushPerChanges + " from current=" + mvcc.getReadPoint());
2273      }
2274      return true;
2275    }
2276    if (this.flushCheckInterval <= 0) {
2277      return false;
2278    }
2279    long now = EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime();
2280    if (store.timeOfOldestEdit() < now - this.flushCheckInterval) {
2281      if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
2282        LOG.debug("Flush column family: " + store.getColumnFamilyName() + " of " +
2283          getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " because time of oldest edit=" +
2284            store.timeOfOldestEdit() + " is > " + this.flushCheckInterval + " from now =" + now);
2285      }
2286      return true;
2287    }
2288    return false;
2289  }
2290
2291  /**
2292   * Should the memstore be flushed now
2293   */
2294  boolean shouldFlush(final StringBuilder whyFlush) {
2295    whyFlush.setLength(0);
2296    // This is a rough measure.
2297    if (this.maxFlushedSeqId > 0
2298          && (this.maxFlushedSeqId + this.flushPerChanges < this.mvcc.getReadPoint())) {
2299      whyFlush.append("more than max edits, " + this.flushPerChanges + ", since last flush");
2300      return true;
2301    }
2302    long modifiedFlushCheckInterval = flushCheckInterval;
2303    if (getRegionInfo().getTable().isSystemTable() &&
2304        getRegionInfo().getReplicaId() == RegionInfo.DEFAULT_REPLICA_ID) {
2305      modifiedFlushCheckInterval = SYSTEM_CACHE_FLUSH_INTERVAL;
2306    }
2307    if (modifiedFlushCheckInterval <= 0) { //disabled
2308      return false;
2309    }
2310    long now = EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime();
2311    //if we flushed in the recent past, we don't need to do again now
2312    if ((now - getEarliestFlushTimeForAllStores() < modifiedFlushCheckInterval)) {
2313      return false;
2314    }
2315    //since we didn't flush in the recent past, flush now if certain conditions
2316    //are met. Return true on first such memstore hit.
2317    for (HStore s : stores.values()) {
2318      if (s.timeOfOldestEdit() < now - modifiedFlushCheckInterval) {
2319        // we have an old enough edit in the memstore, flush
2320        whyFlush.append(s.toString() + " has an old edit so flush to free WALs");
2321        return true;
2322      }
2323    }
2324    return false;
2325  }
2326
2327  /**
2328   * Flushing all stores.
2329   * @see #internalFlushcache(Collection, MonitoredTask, boolean, FlushLifeCycleTracker)
2330   */
2331  private FlushResult internalFlushcache(MonitoredTask status) throws IOException {
2332    return internalFlushcache(stores.values(), status, false, FlushLifeCycleTracker.DUMMY);
2333  }
2334
2335  /**
2336   * Flushing given stores.
2337   * @see #internalFlushcache(WAL, long, Collection, MonitoredTask, boolean, FlushLifeCycleTracker)
2338   */
2339  private FlushResultImpl internalFlushcache(Collection<HStore> storesToFlush, MonitoredTask status,
2340      boolean writeFlushWalMarker, FlushLifeCycleTracker tracker) throws IOException {
2341    return internalFlushcache(this.wal, HConstants.NO_SEQNUM, storesToFlush, status,
2342      writeFlushWalMarker, tracker);
2343  }
2344
2345  /**
2346   * Flush the memstore. Flushing the memstore is a little tricky. We have a lot of updates in the
2347   * memstore, all of which have also been written to the wal. We need to write those updates in the
2348   * memstore out to disk, while being able to process reads/writes as much as possible during the
2349   * flush operation.
2350   * <p>
2351   * This method may block for some time. Every time you call it, we up the regions sequence id even
2352   * if we don't flush; i.e. the returned region id will be at least one larger than the last edit
2353   * applied to this region. The returned id does not refer to an actual edit. The returned id can
2354   * be used for say installing a bulk loaded file just ahead of the last hfile that was the result
2355   * of this flush, etc.
2356   * @param wal Null if we're NOT to go via wal.
2357   * @param myseqid The seqid to use if <code>wal</code> is null writing out flush file.
2358   * @param storesToFlush The list of stores to flush.
2359   * @return object describing the flush's state
2360   * @throws IOException general io exceptions
2361   * @throws DroppedSnapshotException Thrown when replay of WAL is required.
2362   */
2363  protected FlushResultImpl internalFlushcache(WAL wal, long myseqid,
2364      Collection<HStore> storesToFlush, MonitoredTask status, boolean writeFlushWalMarker,
2365      FlushLifeCycleTracker tracker) throws IOException {
2366    PrepareFlushResult result =
2367        internalPrepareFlushCache(wal, myseqid, storesToFlush, status, writeFlushWalMarker, tracker);
2368    if (result.result == null) {
2369      return internalFlushCacheAndCommit(wal, status, result, storesToFlush);
2370    } else {
2371      return result.result; // early exit due to failure from prepare stage
2372    }
2373  }
2374
2375  @edu.umd.cs.findbugs.annotations.SuppressWarnings(value="DLS_DEAD_LOCAL_STORE",
2376      justification="FindBugs seems confused about trxId")
2377  protected PrepareFlushResult internalPrepareFlushCache(WAL wal, long myseqid,
2378      Collection<HStore> storesToFlush, MonitoredTask status, boolean writeFlushWalMarker,
2379      FlushLifeCycleTracker tracker) throws IOException {
2380    if (this.rsServices != null && this.rsServices.isAborted()) {
2381      // Don't flush when server aborting, it's unsafe
2382      throw new IOException("Aborting flush because server is aborted...");
2383    }
2384    final long startTime = EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime();
2385    // If nothing to flush, return, but return with a valid unused sequenceId.
2386    // Its needed by bulk upload IIRC. It flushes until no edits in memory so it can insert a
2387    // bulk loaded file between memory and existing hfiles. It wants a good seqeunceId that belongs
2388    // to no other that it can use to associate with the bulk load. Hence this little dance below
2389    // to go get one.
2390    if (this.memStoreSize.getDataSize() <= 0) {
2391      // Take an update lock so no edits can come into memory just yet.
2392      this.updatesLock.writeLock().lock();
2393      WriteEntry writeEntry = null;
2394      try {
2395        if (this.memStoreSize.getDataSize() <= 0) {
2396          // Presume that if there are still no edits in the memstore, then there are no edits for
2397          // this region out in the WAL subsystem so no need to do any trickery clearing out
2398          // edits in the WAL sub-system. Up the sequence number so the resulting flush id is for
2399          // sure just beyond the last appended region edit and not associated with any edit
2400          // (useful as marker when bulk loading, etc.).
2401          if (wal != null) {
2402            writeEntry = mvcc.begin();
2403            long flushOpSeqId = writeEntry.getWriteNumber();
2404            FlushResultImpl flushResult =
2405                new FlushResultImpl(FlushResult.Result.CANNOT_FLUSH_MEMSTORE_EMPTY, flushOpSeqId,
2406                    "Nothing to flush", writeFlushRequestMarkerToWAL(wal, writeFlushWalMarker));
2407            mvcc.completeAndWait(writeEntry);
2408            // Set to null so we don't complete it again down in finally block.
2409            writeEntry = null;
2410            return new PrepareFlushResult(flushResult, myseqid);
2411          } else {
2412            return new PrepareFlushResult(new FlushResultImpl(
2413              FlushResult.Result.CANNOT_FLUSH_MEMSTORE_EMPTY, "Nothing to flush", false), myseqid);
2414          }
2415        }
2416      } finally {
2417        if (writeEntry != null) {
2418          // If writeEntry is non-null, this operation failed; the mvcc transaction failed...
2419          // but complete it anyways so it doesn't block the mvcc queue.
2420          mvcc.complete(writeEntry);
2421        }
2422        this.updatesLock.writeLock().unlock();
2423      }
2424    }
2425    logFatLineOnFlush(storesToFlush, myseqid);
2426    // Stop updates while we snapshot the memstore of all of these regions' stores. We only have
2427    // to do this for a moment.  It is quick. We also set the memstore size to zero here before we
2428    // allow updates again so its value will represent the size of the updates received
2429    // during flush
2430
2431    // We have to take an update lock during snapshot, or else a write could end up in both snapshot
2432    // and memstore (makes it difficult to do atomic rows then)
2433    status.setStatus("Obtaining lock to block concurrent updates");
2434    // block waiting for the lock for internal flush
2435    this.updatesLock.writeLock().lock();
2436    status.setStatus("Preparing flush snapshotting stores in " + getRegionInfo().getEncodedName());
2437    MemStoreSizing totalSizeOfFlushableStores = new MemStoreSizing();
2438
2439    Map<byte[], Long> flushedFamilyNamesToSeq = new HashMap<>();
2440    for (HStore store : storesToFlush) {
2441      flushedFamilyNamesToSeq.put(store.getColumnFamilyDescriptor().getName(),
2442        store.preFlushSeqIDEstimation());
2443    }
2444
2445    TreeMap<byte[], StoreFlushContext> storeFlushCtxs = new TreeMap<>(Bytes.BYTES_COMPARATOR);
2446    TreeMap<byte[], List<Path>> committedFiles = new TreeMap<>(Bytes.BYTES_COMPARATOR);
2447    TreeMap<byte[], MemStoreSize> storeFlushableSize = new TreeMap<>(Bytes.BYTES_COMPARATOR);
2448    // The sequence id of this flush operation which is used to log FlushMarker and pass to
2449    // createFlushContext to use as the store file's sequence id. It can be in advance of edits
2450    // still in the memstore, edits that are in other column families yet to be flushed.
2451    long flushOpSeqId = HConstants.NO_SEQNUM;
2452    // The max flushed sequence id after this flush operation completes. All edits in memstore
2453    // will be in advance of this sequence id.
2454    long flushedSeqId = HConstants.NO_SEQNUM;
2455    byte[] encodedRegionName = getRegionInfo().getEncodedNameAsBytes();
2456    try {
2457      if (wal != null) {
2458        Long earliestUnflushedSequenceIdForTheRegion =
2459            wal.startCacheFlush(encodedRegionName, flushedFamilyNamesToSeq);
2460        if (earliestUnflushedSequenceIdForTheRegion == null) {
2461          // This should never happen. This is how startCacheFlush signals flush cannot proceed.
2462          String msg = this.getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " flush aborted; WAL closing.";
2463          status.setStatus(msg);
2464          return new PrepareFlushResult(
2465              new FlushResultImpl(FlushResult.Result.CANNOT_FLUSH, msg, false),
2466              myseqid);
2467        }
2468        flushOpSeqId = getNextSequenceId(wal);
2469        // Back up 1, minus 1 from oldest sequence id in memstore to get last 'flushed' edit
2470        flushedSeqId =
2471            earliestUnflushedSequenceIdForTheRegion.longValue() == HConstants.NO_SEQNUM?
2472                flushOpSeqId: earliestUnflushedSequenceIdForTheRegion.longValue() - 1;
2473      } else {
2474        // use the provided sequence Id as WAL is not being used for this flush.
2475        flushedSeqId = flushOpSeqId = myseqid;
2476      }
2477
2478      for (HStore s : storesToFlush) {
2479        storeFlushCtxs.put(s.getColumnFamilyDescriptor().getName(),
2480          s.createFlushContext(flushOpSeqId, tracker));
2481        // for writing stores to WAL
2482        committedFiles.put(s.getColumnFamilyDescriptor().getName(), null);
2483      }
2484
2485      // write the snapshot start to WAL
2486      if (wal != null && !writestate.readOnly) {
2487        FlushDescriptor desc = ProtobufUtil.toFlushDescriptor(FlushAction.START_FLUSH,
2488            getRegionInfo(), flushOpSeqId, committedFiles);
2489        // No sync. Sync is below where no updates lock and we do FlushAction.COMMIT_FLUSH
2490        WALUtil.writeFlushMarker(wal, this.getReplicationScope(), getRegionInfo(), desc, false,
2491            mvcc);
2492      }
2493
2494      // Prepare flush (take a snapshot)
2495      storeFlushCtxs.forEach((name, flush) -> {
2496        MemStoreSize snapshotSize = flush.prepare();
2497        totalSizeOfFlushableStores.incMemStoreSize(snapshotSize);
2498        storeFlushableSize.put(name, snapshotSize);
2499      });
2500    } catch (IOException ex) {
2501      doAbortFlushToWAL(wal, flushOpSeqId, committedFiles);
2502      throw ex;
2503    } finally {
2504      this.updatesLock.writeLock().unlock();
2505    }
2506    String s = "Finished memstore snapshotting " + this + ", syncing WAL and waiting on mvcc, " +
2507        "flushsize=" + totalSizeOfFlushableStores;
2508    status.setStatus(s);
2509    doSyncOfUnflushedWALChanges(wal, getRegionInfo());
2510    return new PrepareFlushResult(storeFlushCtxs, committedFiles, storeFlushableSize, startTime,
2511        flushOpSeqId, flushedSeqId, totalSizeOfFlushableStores);
2512  }
2513
2514  /**
2515   * Utility method broken out of internalPrepareFlushCache so that method is smaller.
2516   */
2517  private void logFatLineOnFlush(Collection<HStore> storesToFlush, long sequenceId) {
2518    if (!LOG.isInfoEnabled()) {
2519      return;
2520    }
2521    // Log a fat line detailing what is being flushed.
2522    StringBuilder perCfExtras = null;
2523    if (!isAllFamilies(storesToFlush)) {
2524      perCfExtras = new StringBuilder();
2525      for (HStore store: storesToFlush) {
2526        perCfExtras.append("; ").append(store.getColumnFamilyName());
2527        perCfExtras.append("=")
2528            .append(StringUtils.byteDesc(store.getFlushableSize().getDataSize()));
2529      }
2530    }
2531    LOG.info("Flushing " + + storesToFlush.size() + "/" + stores.size() + " column families," +
2532        " memstore data size=" + StringUtils.byteDesc(this.memStoreSize.getDataSize()) +
2533        " memstore heap size=" + StringUtils.byteDesc(this.memStoreSize.getHeapSize()) +
2534        ((perCfExtras != null && perCfExtras.length() > 0)? perCfExtras.toString(): "") +
2535        ((wal != null) ? "" : "; WAL is null, using passed sequenceid=" + sequenceId));
2536  }
2537
2538  private void doAbortFlushToWAL(final WAL wal, final long flushOpSeqId,
2539      final Map<byte[], List<Path>> committedFiles) {
2540    if (wal == null) return;
2541    try {
2542      FlushDescriptor desc = ProtobufUtil.toFlushDescriptor(FlushAction.ABORT_FLUSH,
2543          getRegionInfo(), flushOpSeqId, committedFiles);
2544      WALUtil.writeFlushMarker(wal, this.getReplicationScope(), getRegionInfo(), desc, false,
2545          mvcc);
2546    } catch (Throwable t) {
2547      LOG.warn("Received unexpected exception trying to write ABORT_FLUSH marker to WAL:" +
2548          StringUtils.stringifyException(t));
2549      // ignore this since we will be aborting the RS with DSE.
2550    }
2551    // we have called wal.startCacheFlush(), now we have to abort it
2552    wal.abortCacheFlush(this.getRegionInfo().getEncodedNameAsBytes());
2553  }
2554
2555  /**
2556   * Sync unflushed WAL changes. See HBASE-8208 for details
2557   */
2558  private static void doSyncOfUnflushedWALChanges(final WAL wal, final RegionInfo hri)
2559  throws IOException {
2560    if (wal == null) {
2561      return;
2562    }
2563    try {
2564      wal.sync(); // ensure that flush marker is sync'ed
2565    } catch (IOException ioe) {
2566      wal.abortCacheFlush(hri.getEncodedNameAsBytes());
2567      throw ioe;
2568    }
2569  }
2570
2571  /**
2572   * @return True if passed Set is all families in the region.
2573   */
2574  private boolean isAllFamilies(Collection<HStore> families) {
2575    return families == null || this.stores.size() == families.size();
2576  }
2577
2578  /**
2579   * Writes a marker to WAL indicating a flush is requested but cannot be complete due to various
2580   * reasons. Ignores exceptions from WAL. Returns whether the write succeeded.
2581   * @param wal
2582   * @return whether WAL write was successful
2583   */
2584  private boolean writeFlushRequestMarkerToWAL(WAL wal, boolean writeFlushWalMarker) {
2585    if (writeFlushWalMarker && wal != null && !writestate.readOnly) {
2586      FlushDescriptor desc = ProtobufUtil.toFlushDescriptor(FlushAction.CANNOT_FLUSH,
2587        getRegionInfo(), -1, new TreeMap<>(Bytes.BYTES_COMPARATOR));
2588      try {
2589        WALUtil.writeFlushMarker(wal, this.getReplicationScope(), getRegionInfo(), desc, true,
2590            mvcc);
2591        return true;
2592      } catch (IOException e) {
2593        LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
2594            + "Received exception while trying to write the flush request to wal", e);
2595      }
2596    }
2597    return false;
2598  }
2599
2600  @edu.umd.cs.findbugs.annotations.SuppressWarnings(value="NN_NAKED_NOTIFY",
2601      justification="Intentional; notify is about completed flush")
2602  protected FlushResultImpl internalFlushCacheAndCommit(WAL wal, MonitoredTask status,
2603      PrepareFlushResult prepareResult, Collection<HStore> storesToFlush) throws IOException {
2604    // prepare flush context is carried via PrepareFlushResult
2605    TreeMap<byte[], StoreFlushContext> storeFlushCtxs = prepareResult.storeFlushCtxs;
2606    TreeMap<byte[], List<Path>> committedFiles = prepareResult.committedFiles;
2607    long startTime = prepareResult.startTime;
2608    long flushOpSeqId = prepareResult.flushOpSeqId;
2609    long flushedSeqId = prepareResult.flushedSeqId;
2610
2611    String s = "Flushing stores of " + this;
2612    status.setStatus(s);
2613    if (LOG.isTraceEnabled()) LOG.trace(s);
2614
2615    // Any failure from here on out will be catastrophic requiring server
2616    // restart so wal content can be replayed and put back into the memstore.
2617    // Otherwise, the snapshot content while backed up in the wal, it will not
2618    // be part of the current running servers state.
2619    boolean compactionRequested = false;
2620    long flushedOutputFileSize = 0;
2621    try {
2622      // A.  Flush memstore to all the HStores.
2623      // Keep running vector of all store files that includes both old and the
2624      // just-made new flush store file. The new flushed file is still in the
2625      // tmp directory.
2626
2627      for (StoreFlushContext flush : storeFlushCtxs.values()) {
2628        flush.flushCache(status);
2629      }
2630
2631      // Switch snapshot (in memstore) -> new hfile (thus causing
2632      // all the store scanners to reset/reseek).
2633      Iterator<HStore> it = storesToFlush.iterator();
2634      // stores.values() and storeFlushCtxs have same order
2635      for (StoreFlushContext flush : storeFlushCtxs.values()) {
2636        boolean needsCompaction = flush.commit(status);
2637        if (needsCompaction) {
2638          compactionRequested = true;
2639        }
2640        byte[] storeName = it.next().getColumnFamilyDescriptor().getName();
2641        List<Path> storeCommittedFiles = flush.getCommittedFiles();
2642        committedFiles.put(storeName, storeCommittedFiles);
2643        // Flush committed no files, indicating flush is empty or flush was canceled
2644        if (storeCommittedFiles == null || storeCommittedFiles.isEmpty()) {
2645          MemStoreSize storeFlushableSize = prepareResult.storeFlushableSize.get(storeName);
2646          prepareResult.totalFlushableSize.decMemStoreSize(storeFlushableSize);
2647        }
2648        flushedOutputFileSize += flush.getOutputFileSize();
2649      }
2650      storeFlushCtxs.clear();
2651
2652      // Set down the memstore size by amount of flush.
2653      this.decrMemStoreSize(prepareResult.totalFlushableSize);
2654
2655      // Increase the size of this Region for the purposes of quota. Noop if quotas are disabled.
2656      // During startup, quota manager may not be initialized yet.
2657      if (rsServices != null) {
2658        RegionServerSpaceQuotaManager quotaManager = rsServices.getRegionServerSpaceQuotaManager();
2659        if (quotaManager != null) {
2660          quotaManager.getRegionSizeStore().incrementRegionSize(
2661              this.getRegionInfo(), flushedOutputFileSize);
2662        }
2663      }
2664
2665      if (wal != null) {
2666        // write flush marker to WAL. If fail, we should throw DroppedSnapshotException
2667        FlushDescriptor desc = ProtobufUtil.toFlushDescriptor(FlushAction.COMMIT_FLUSH,
2668          getRegionInfo(), flushOpSeqId, committedFiles);
2669        WALUtil.writeFlushMarker(wal, this.getReplicationScope(), getRegionInfo(), desc, true,
2670            mvcc);
2671      }
2672    } catch (Throwable t) {
2673      // An exception here means that the snapshot was not persisted.
2674      // The wal needs to be replayed so its content is restored to memstore.
2675      // Currently, only a server restart will do this.
2676      // We used to only catch IOEs but its possible that we'd get other
2677      // exceptions -- e.g. HBASE-659 was about an NPE -- so now we catch
2678      // all and sundry.
2679      if (wal != null) {
2680        try {
2681          FlushDescriptor desc = ProtobufUtil.toFlushDescriptor(FlushAction.ABORT_FLUSH,
2682            getRegionInfo(), flushOpSeqId, committedFiles);
2683          WALUtil.writeFlushMarker(wal, this.replicationScope, getRegionInfo(), desc, false, mvcc);
2684        } catch (Throwable ex) {
2685          LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
2686              + "failed writing ABORT_FLUSH marker to WAL", ex);
2687          // ignore this since we will be aborting the RS with DSE.
2688        }
2689        wal.abortCacheFlush(this.getRegionInfo().getEncodedNameAsBytes());
2690      }
2691      DroppedSnapshotException dse = new DroppedSnapshotException("region: " +
2692          Bytes.toStringBinary(getRegionInfo().getRegionName()));
2693      dse.initCause(t);
2694      status.abort("Flush failed: " + StringUtils.stringifyException(t));
2695
2696      // Callers for flushcache() should catch DroppedSnapshotException and abort the region server.
2697      // However, since we may have the region read lock, we cannot call close(true) here since
2698      // we cannot promote to a write lock. Instead we are setting closing so that all other region
2699      // operations except for close will be rejected.
2700      this.closing.set(true);
2701
2702      if (rsServices != null) {
2703        // This is a safeguard against the case where the caller fails to explicitly handle aborting
2704        rsServices.abort("Replay of WAL required. Forcing server shutdown", dse);
2705      }
2706
2707      throw dse;
2708    }
2709
2710    // If we get to here, the HStores have been written.
2711    if (wal != null) {
2712      wal.completeCacheFlush(this.getRegionInfo().getEncodedNameAsBytes());
2713    }
2714
2715    // Record latest flush time
2716    for (HStore store: storesToFlush) {
2717      this.lastStoreFlushTimeMap.put(store, startTime);
2718    }
2719
2720    this.maxFlushedSeqId = flushedSeqId;
2721    this.lastFlushOpSeqId = flushOpSeqId;
2722
2723    // C. Finally notify anyone waiting on memstore to clear:
2724    // e.g. checkResources().
2725    synchronized (this) {
2726      notifyAll(); // FindBugs NN_NAKED_NOTIFY
2727    }
2728
2729    long time = EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime() - startTime;
2730    long flushableDataSize = prepareResult.totalFlushableSize.getDataSize();
2731    long flushableHeapSize = prepareResult.totalFlushableSize.getHeapSize();
2732    long memstoresize = this.memStoreSize.getDataSize();
2733    String msg = "Finished memstore flush."
2734        + " Flushed data size ~" + StringUtils.byteDesc(flushableDataSize) + "/" + flushableDataSize
2735        + " Flushed Heap size ~" + StringUtils.byteDesc(flushableHeapSize) + "/" + flushableHeapSize
2736        + ", currentsize=" + StringUtils.byteDesc(memstoresize) + "/" + memstoresize
2737        + " for region " + this + " in " + time + "ms, sequenceid="
2738        + flushOpSeqId +  ", compaction requested=" + compactionRequested
2739        + ((wal == null) ? "; wal=null" : "");
2740    LOG.info(msg);
2741    status.setStatus(msg);
2742
2743    if (rsServices != null && rsServices.getMetrics() != null) {
2744      rsServices.getMetrics().updateFlush(time - startTime,
2745          prepareResult.totalFlushableSize.getDataSize(), flushedOutputFileSize);
2746    }
2747
2748    return new FlushResultImpl(compactionRequested ?
2749        FlushResult.Result.FLUSHED_COMPACTION_NEEDED :
2750          FlushResult.Result.FLUSHED_NO_COMPACTION_NEEDED, flushOpSeqId);
2751  }
2752
2753  /**
2754   * Method to safely get the next sequence number.
2755   * @return Next sequence number unassociated with any actual edit.
2756   * @throws IOException
2757   */
2758  @VisibleForTesting
2759  protected long getNextSequenceId(final WAL wal) throws IOException {
2760    WriteEntry we = mvcc.begin();
2761    mvcc.completeAndWait(we);
2762    return we.getWriteNumber();
2763  }
