2769  @Override
2770  public RegionScannerImpl getScanner(Scan scan) throws IOException {
2771   return getScanner(scan, null);
2772  }
2773
2774  @Override
2775  public RegionScannerImpl getScanner(Scan scan, List<KeyValueScanner> additionalScanners)
2776      throws IOException {
2777    return getScanner(scan, additionalScanners, HConstants.NO_NONCE, HConstants.NO_NONCE);
2778  }
2779
2780  private RegionScannerImpl getScanner(Scan scan, List<KeyValueScanner> additionalScanners,
2781      long nonceGroup, long nonce) throws IOException {
2782    startRegionOperation(Operation.SCAN);
2783    try {
2784      // Verify families are all valid
2785      if (!scan.hasFamilies()) {
2786        // Adding all families to scanner
2787        for (byte[] family : this.htableDescriptor.getColumnFamilyNames()) {
2788          scan.addFamily(family);
2789        }
2790      } else {
2791        for (byte[] family : scan.getFamilyMap().keySet()) {
2792          checkFamily(family);
2793        }
2794      }
2795      return instantiateRegionScanner(scan, additionalScanners, nonceGroup, nonce);
2796    } finally {
2797      closeRegionOperation(Operation.SCAN);
2798    }
2799  }
2800
2801  protected RegionScanner instantiateRegionScanner(Scan scan,
2802      List<KeyValueScanner> additionalScanners) throws IOException {
2803    return instantiateRegionScanner(scan, additionalScanners, HConstants.NO_NONCE,
2804      HConstants.NO_NONCE);
2805  }
2806
2807  protected RegionScannerImpl instantiateRegionScanner(Scan scan,
2808      List<KeyValueScanner> additionalScanners, long nonceGroup, long nonce) throws IOException {
2809    if (scan.isReversed()) {
2810      if (scan.getFilter() != null) {
2811        scan.getFilter().setReversed(true);
2812      }
2813      return new ReversedRegionScannerImpl(scan, additionalScanners, this);
2814    }
2815    return new RegionScannerImpl(scan, additionalScanners, this, nonceGroup, nonce);
2816  }
2817
2818  /**
2819   * Prepare a delete for a row mutation processor
2820   * @param delete The passed delete is modified by this method. WARNING!
2821   * @throws IOException
2822   */
2823  public void prepareDelete(Delete delete) throws IOException {
2824    // Check to see if this is a deleteRow insert
2825    if(delete.getFamilyCellMap().isEmpty()){
2826      for(byte [] family : this.htableDescriptor.getColumnFamilyNames()){
2827        // Don't eat the timestamp
2828        delete.addFamily(family, delete.getTimeStamp());
2829      }
2830    } else {
2831      for(byte [] family : delete.getFamilyCellMap().keySet()) {
2832        if(family == null) {
2833          throw new NoSuchColumnFamilyException("Empty family is invalid");
2834        }
2835        checkFamily(family);
2836      }
2837    }
2838  }
2839
2840  @Override
2841  public void delete(Delete delete) throws IOException {
2842    checkReadOnly();
2843    checkResources();
2844    startRegionOperation(Operation.DELETE);
2845    try {
2846      // All edits for the given row (across all column families) must happen atomically.
2847      doBatchMutate(delete);
2848    } finally {
2849      closeRegionOperation(Operation.DELETE);
2850    }
2851  }
2852
2853  /**
2854   * Row needed by below method.
2855   */
2856  private static final byte [] FOR_UNIT_TESTS_ONLY = Bytes.toBytes("ForUnitTestsOnly");
2857
2858  /**
2859   * This is used only by unit tests. Not required to be a public API.
2860   * @param familyMap map of family to edits for the given family.
2861   * @throws IOException
2862   */
2863  void delete(NavigableMap<byte[], List<Cell>> familyMap,
2864      Durability durability) throws IOException {
2865    Delete delete = new Delete(FOR_UNIT_TESTS_ONLY);
2866    delete.setFamilyCellMap(familyMap);
2867    delete.setDurability(durability);
2868    doBatchMutate(delete);
2869  }
2870
2871  /**
2872   * Set up correct timestamps in the KVs in Delete object.
2873   * <p>Caller should have the row and region locks.
2874   * @param mutation
2875   * @param familyMap
2876   * @param byteNow
2877   * @throws IOException
2878   */
2879  public void prepareDeleteTimestamps(Mutation mutation, Map<byte[], List<Cell>> familyMap,
2880      byte[] byteNow) throws IOException {
2881    for (Map.Entry<byte[], List<Cell>> e : familyMap.entrySet()) {
2882
2883      byte[] family = e.getKey();
2884      List<Cell> cells = e.getValue();
2885      assert cells instanceof RandomAccess;
2886
2887      Map<byte[], Integer> kvCount = new TreeMap<>(Bytes.BYTES_COMPARATOR);
2888      int listSize = cells.size();
2889      for (int i=0; i < listSize; i++) {
2890        Cell cell = cells.get(i);
2891        //  Check if time is LATEST, change to time of most recent addition if so
2892        //  This is expensive.
2893        if (cell.getTimestamp() == HConstants.LATEST_TIMESTAMP
2894            && PrivateCellUtil.isDeleteType(cell)) {
2895          byte[] qual = CellUtil.cloneQualifier(cell);
2896
2897          Integer count = kvCount.get(qual);
2898          if (count == null) {
2899            kvCount.put(qual, 1);
2900          } else {
2901            kvCount.put(qual, count + 1);
2902          }
2903          count = kvCount.get(qual);
2904
2905          Get get = new Get(CellUtil.cloneRow(cell));
2906          get.setMaxVersions(count);
2907          get.addColumn(family, qual);
2908          if (coprocessorHost != null) {
2909            if (!coprocessorHost.prePrepareTimeStampForDeleteVersion(mutation, cell,
2910                byteNow, get)) {
2911              updateDeleteLatestVersionTimeStamp(cell, get, count, byteNow);
2912            }
2913          } else {
2914            updateDeleteLatestVersionTimeStamp(cell, get, count, byteNow);
2915          }
2916        } else {
2917          PrivateCellUtil.updateLatestStamp(cell, byteNow);
2918        }
2919      }
2920    }
2921  }
2922
2923  void updateDeleteLatestVersionTimeStamp(Cell cell, Get get, int count, byte[] byteNow)
2924      throws IOException {
2925    List<Cell> result = get(get, false);
2926
2927    if (result.size() < count) {
2928      // Nothing to delete
2929      PrivateCellUtil.updateLatestStamp(cell, byteNow);
2930      return;
2931    }
2932    if (result.size() > count) {
2933      throw new RuntimeException("Unexpected size: " + result.size());
2934    }
2935    Cell getCell = result.get(count - 1);
2936    PrivateCellUtil.setTimestamp(cell, getCell.getTimestamp());
2937  }
2938
2939  @Override
2940  public void put(Put put) throws IOException {
2941    checkReadOnly();
2942
2943    // Do a rough check that we have resources to accept a write.  The check is
2944    // 'rough' in that between the resource check and the call to obtain a
2945    // read lock, resources may run out.  For now, the thought is that this
2946    // will be extremely rare; we'll deal with it when it happens.
2947    checkResources();
2948    startRegionOperation(Operation.PUT);
2949    try {
2950      // All edits for the given row (across all column families) must happen atomically.
2951      doBatchMutate(put);
2952    } finally {
2953      closeRegionOperation(Operation.PUT);
2954    }
2955  }
2956
2957  /**
2958   * Class that tracks the progress of a batch operations, accumulating status codes and tracking
2959   * the index at which processing is proceeding. These batch operations may get split into
2960   * mini-batches for processing.
2961   */
2962  private abstract static class BatchOperation<T> {
2963    protected final T[] operations;
2964    protected final OperationStatus[] retCodeDetails;
2965    protected final WALEdit[] walEditsFromCoprocessors;
2966    // reference family cell maps directly so coprocessors can mutate them if desired
2967    protected final Map<byte[], List<Cell>>[] familyCellMaps;
2968
2969    protected final HRegion region;
2970    protected int nextIndexToProcess = 0;
2971    protected final ObservedExceptionsInBatch observedExceptions;
2972    //Durability of the batch (highest durability of all operations)
2973    protected Durability durability;
2974    protected boolean atomic = false;
2975
2976    public BatchOperation(final HRegion region, T[] operations) {
2977      this.operations = operations;
2978      this.retCodeDetails = new OperationStatus[operations.length];
2979      Arrays.fill(this.retCodeDetails, OperationStatus.NOT_RUN);
2980      this.walEditsFromCoprocessors = new WALEdit[operations.length];
2981      familyCellMaps = new Map[operations.length];
2982
2983      this.region = region;
2984      observedExceptions = new ObservedExceptionsInBatch();
2985      durability = Durability.USE_DEFAULT;
2986    }
2987
2988    /**
2989     * Visitor interface for batch operations
2990     */
2991    @FunctionalInterface
2992    public interface Visitor {
2993      /**
2994       * @param index operation index
2995       * @return If true continue visiting remaining entries, break otherwise
2996       */
2997      boolean visit(int index) throws IOException;
2998    }
2999
3000    /**
3001     * Helper method for visiting pending/ all batch operations
3002     */
3003    public void visitBatchOperations(boolean pendingOnly, int lastIndexExclusive, Visitor visitor)
3004        throws IOException {
3005      assert lastIndexExclusive <= this.size();
3006      for (int i = nextIndexToProcess; i < lastIndexExclusive; i++) {
3007        if (!pendingOnly || isOperationPending(i)) {
3008          if (!visitor.visit(i)) {
3009            break;
3010          }
3011        }
3012      }
3013    }
3014
3015    public abstract Mutation getMutation(int index);
3016    public abstract long getNonceGroup(int index);
3017    public abstract long getNonce(int index);
3018    /** This method is potentially expensive and useful mostly for non-replay CP path. */
3019    public abstract Mutation[] getMutationsForCoprocs();
3020    public abstract boolean isInReplay();
3021    public abstract long getOrigLogSeqNum();
3022    public abstract void startRegionOperation() throws IOException;
3023    public abstract void closeRegionOperation() throws IOException;
3024
3025    /**
3026     * Validates each mutation and prepares a batch for write. If necessary (non-replay case), runs
3027     * CP prePut()/ preDelete() hooks for all mutations in a batch. This is intended to operate on
3028     * entire batch and will be called from outside of class to check and prepare batch. This can
3029     * be implemented by calling helper method {@link #checkAndPrepareMutation(int, long)} in a
3030     * 'for' loop over mutations.
3031     */
3032    public abstract void checkAndPrepare() throws IOException;
3033
3034    /**
3035     * Implement any Put request specific check and prepare logic here. Please refer to
3036     * {@link #checkAndPrepareMutation(Mutation, long)} for how its used.
3037     */
3038    protected abstract void checkAndPreparePut(final Put p) throws IOException;
3039
3040    /**
3041     *  If necessary, calls preBatchMutate() CP hook for a mini-batch and updates metrics, cell
3042     *  count, tags and timestamp for all cells of all operations in a mini-batch.
3043     */
3044    public abstract void prepareMiniBatchOperations(MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation>
3045        miniBatchOp, long timestamp, final List<RowLock> acquiredRowLocks) throws IOException;
3046
3047    /**
3048     * Write mini-batch operations to MemStore
3049     */
3050    public abstract WriteEntry writeMiniBatchOperationsToMemStore(
3051        final MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> miniBatchOp, final WriteEntry writeEntry)
3052        throws IOException;
3053
3054    protected void writeMiniBatchOperationsToMemStore(
3055        final MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> miniBatchOp, final long writeNumber)
3056        throws IOException {
3057      MemStoreSizing memStoreAccounting = new MemStoreSizing();
3058      visitBatchOperations(true, miniBatchOp.getLastIndexExclusive(), (int index) -> {
3059        // We need to update the sequence id for following reasons.
3060        // 1) If the op is in replay mode, FSWALEntry#stampRegionSequenceId won't stamp sequence id.
3061        // 2) If no WAL, FSWALEntry won't be used
3062        // we use durability of the original mutation for the mutation passed by CP.
3063        if (isInReplay() || getMutation(index).getDurability() == Durability.SKIP_WAL) {
3064          region.updateSequenceId(familyCellMaps[index].values(), writeNumber);
3065        }
3066        applyFamilyMapToMemStore(familyCellMaps[index], memStoreAccounting);
3067        return true;
3068      });
3069      // update memStore size
3070      region.incMemStoreSize(memStoreAccounting);
3071    }
3072
3073    public boolean isDone() {
3074      return nextIndexToProcess == operations.length;
3075    }
3076
3077    public int size() {
3078      return operations.length;
3079    }
3080
3081    public boolean isOperationPending(int index) {
3082      return retCodeDetails[index].getOperationStatusCode() == OperationStatusCode.NOT_RUN;
3083    }
3084
3085    public List<UUID> getClusterIds() {
3086      assert size() != 0;
3087      return getMutation(0).getClusterIds();
3088    }
3089
3090    boolean isAtomic() {
3091      return atomic;
3092    }
3093
3094    /**
3095     * Helper method that checks and prepares only one mutation. This can be used to implement
3096     * {@link #checkAndPrepare()} for entire Batch.
3097     * NOTE: As CP prePut()/ preDelete() hooks may modify mutations, this method should be called
3098     * after prePut()/ preDelete() CP hooks are run for the mutation
3099     */
3100    protected void checkAndPrepareMutation(Mutation mutation, final long timestamp)
3101        throws IOException {
3102      region.checkRow(mutation.getRow(), "batchMutate");
3103      if (mutation instanceof Put) {
3104        // Check the families in the put. If bad, skip this one.
3105        checkAndPreparePut((Put) mutation);
3106        region.checkTimestamps(mutation.getFamilyCellMap(), timestamp);
3107      } else {
3108        region.prepareDelete((Delete) mutation);
3109      }
3110    }
3111
3112    protected void checkAndPrepareMutation(int index, long timestamp) throws IOException {
3113      Mutation mutation = getMutation(index);
3114      try {
3115        this.checkAndPrepareMutation(mutation, timestamp);
3116
3117        // store the family map reference to allow for mutations
3118        familyCellMaps[index] = mutation.getFamilyCellMap();
3119        // store durability for the batch (highest durability of all operations in the batch)
3120        Durability tmpDur = region.getEffectiveDurability(mutation.getDurability());
3121        if (tmpDur.ordinal() > durability.ordinal()) {
3122          durability = tmpDur;
3123        }
3124      } catch (NoSuchColumnFamilyException nscfe) {
3125        final String msg = "No such column family in batch mutation. ";
3126        if (observedExceptions.hasSeenNoSuchFamily()) {
3127          LOG.warn(msg + nscfe.getMessage());
3128        } else {
3129          LOG.warn(msg, nscfe);
3130          observedExceptions.sawNoSuchFamily();
3131        }
3132        retCodeDetails[index] = new OperationStatus(
3133            OperationStatusCode.BAD_FAMILY, nscfe.getMessage());
3134        if (isAtomic()) { // fail, atomic means all or none
3135          throw nscfe;
3136        }
3137      } catch (FailedSanityCheckException fsce) {
3138        final String msg = "Batch Mutation did not pass sanity check. ";
3139        if (observedExceptions.hasSeenFailedSanityCheck()) {
3140          LOG.warn(msg + fsce.getMessage());
3141        } else {
3142          LOG.warn(msg, fsce);
3143          observedExceptions.sawFailedSanityCheck();
3144        }
3145        retCodeDetails[index] = new OperationStatus(
3146            OperationStatusCode.SANITY_CHECK_FAILURE, fsce.getMessage());
3147        if (isAtomic()) {
3148          throw fsce;
3149        }
3150      } catch (WrongRegionException we) {
3151        final String msg = "Batch mutation had a row that does not belong to this region. ";
3152        if (observedExceptions.hasSeenWrongRegion()) {
3153          LOG.warn(msg + we.getMessage());
3154        } else {
3155          LOG.warn(msg, we);
3156          observedExceptions.sawWrongRegion();
3157        }
3158        retCodeDetails[index] = new OperationStatus(
3159            OperationStatusCode.SANITY_CHECK_FAILURE, we.getMessage());
3160        if (isAtomic()) {
3161          throw we;
3162        }
3163      }
3164    }
3165
3166    /**
3167     * Creates Mini-batch of all operations [nextIndexToProcess, lastIndexExclusive) for which
3168     * a row lock can be acquired. All mutations with locked rows are considered to be
3169     * In-progress operations and hence the name {@link MiniBatchOperationInProgress}. Mini batch
3170     * is window over {@link BatchOperation} and contains contiguous pending operations.
3171     *
3172     * @param acquiredRowLocks keeps track of rowLocks acquired.
3173     */
3174    public MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> lockRowsAndBuildMiniBatch(
3175        List<RowLock> acquiredRowLocks) throws IOException {
3176      int readyToWriteCount = 0;
3177      int lastIndexExclusive = 0;
3178      RowLock prevRowLock = null;
3179      for (; lastIndexExclusive < size(); lastIndexExclusive++) {
3180        // It reaches the miniBatchSize, stop here and process the miniBatch
3181        // This only applies to non-atomic batch operations.
3182        if (!isAtomic() && (readyToWriteCount == region.miniBatchSize)) {
3183          break;
3184        }
3185
3186        if (!isOperationPending(lastIndexExclusive)) {
3187          continue;
3188        }
3189
3190        // HBASE-19389 Limit concurrency of put with dense (hundreds) columns to avoid exhausting
3191        // RS handlers, covering both MutationBatchOperation and ReplayBatchOperation
3192        // The BAD_FAMILY/SANITY_CHECK_FAILURE cases are handled in checkAndPrepare phase and won't
3193        // pass the isOperationPending check
3194        Map<byte[], List<Cell>> curFamilyCellMap =
3195            getMutation(lastIndexExclusive).getFamilyCellMap();
3196        try {
3197          // start the protector before acquiring row lock considering performance, and will finish
3198          // it when encountering exception
3199          region.storeHotnessProtector.start(curFamilyCellMap);
3200        } catch (RegionTooBusyException rtbe) {
3201          region.storeHotnessProtector.finish(curFamilyCellMap);
3202          if (isAtomic()) {
3203            throw rtbe;
3204          }
3205          retCodeDetails[lastIndexExclusive] =
3206              new OperationStatus(OperationStatusCode.STORE_TOO_BUSY, rtbe.getMessage());
3207          continue;
3208        }
3209
3210        Mutation mutation = getMutation(lastIndexExclusive);
3211        // If we haven't got any rows in our batch, we should block to get the next one.
3212        RowLock rowLock = null;
3213        boolean throwException = false;
3214        try {
3215          // if atomic then get exclusive lock, else shared lock
3216          rowLock = region.getRowLockInternal(mutation.getRow(), !isAtomic(), prevRowLock);
3217        } catch (TimeoutIOException|InterruptedIOException e) {
3218          // NOTE: We will retry when other exceptions, but we should stop if we receive
3219          // TimeoutIOException or InterruptedIOException as operation has timed out or
3220          // interrupted respectively.
3221          throwException = true;
3222          throw e;
3223        } catch (IOException ioe) {
3224          LOG.warn("Failed getting lock, row=" + Bytes.toStringBinary(mutation.getRow()), ioe);
3225          if (isAtomic()) { // fail, atomic means all or none
3226            throwException = true;
3227            throw ioe;
3228          }
3229        } catch (Throwable throwable) {
3230          throwException = true;
3231          throw throwable;
3232        } finally {
3233          if (throwException) {
3234            region.storeHotnessProtector.finish(curFamilyCellMap);
3235          }
3236        }
3237        if (rowLock == null) {
3238          // We failed to grab another lock
3239          if (isAtomic()) {
3240            region.storeHotnessProtector.finish(curFamilyCellMap);
3241            throw new IOException("Can't apply all operations atomically!");
3242          }
3243          break; // Stop acquiring more rows for this batch
3244        } else {
3245          if (rowLock != prevRowLock) {
3246            // It is a different row now, add this to the acquiredRowLocks and
3247            // set prevRowLock to the new returned rowLock
3248            acquiredRowLocks.add(rowLock);
3249            prevRowLock = rowLock;
3250          }
3251        }
3252
3253        readyToWriteCount++;
3254      }
3255      return createMiniBatch(lastIndexExclusive, readyToWriteCount);
3256    }
3257
3258    protected MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> createMiniBatch(final int lastIndexExclusive,
3259        final int readyToWriteCount) {
3260      return new MiniBatchOperationInProgress<>(getMutationsForCoprocs(), retCodeDetails,
3261          walEditsFromCoprocessors, nextIndexToProcess, lastIndexExclusive, readyToWriteCount);
3262    }
3263
3264    /**
3265     * Builds separate WALEdit per nonce by applying input mutations. If WALEdits from CP are
3266     * present, they are merged to result WALEdit.
3267     */
3268    public List<Pair<NonceKey, WALEdit>> buildWALEdits(
3269        final MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> miniBatchOp) throws IOException {
3270      List<Pair<NonceKey, WALEdit>> walEdits = new ArrayList<>();
3271
3272      visitBatchOperations(true, nextIndexToProcess + miniBatchOp.size(), new Visitor() {
3273        private Pair<NonceKey, WALEdit> curWALEditForNonce;
3274        @Override
3275        public boolean visit(int index) throws IOException {
3276          Mutation m = getMutation(index);
3277          // we use durability of the original mutation for the mutation passed by CP.
3278          if (region.getEffectiveDurability(m.getDurability()) == Durability.SKIP_WAL) {
3279            region.recordMutationWithoutWal(m.getFamilyCellMap());
3280            return true;
3281          }
3282
3283          // the batch may contain multiple nonce keys (replay case). If so, write WALEdit for each.
3284          // Given how nonce keys are originally written, these should be contiguous.
3285          // They don't have to be, it will still work, just write more WALEdits than needed.
3286          long nonceGroup = getNonceGroup(index);
3287          long nonce = getNonce(index);
3288          if (curWALEditForNonce == null ||
3289              curWALEditForNonce.getFirst().getNonceGroup() != nonceGroup ||
3290              curWALEditForNonce.getFirst().getNonce() != nonce) {
3291            curWALEditForNonce = new Pair<>(new NonceKey(nonceGroup, nonce),
3292                new WALEdit(miniBatchOp.getCellCount(), isInReplay()));
3293            walEdits.add(curWALEditForNonce);
3294          }
3295          WALEdit walEdit = curWALEditForNonce.getSecond();
3296
3297          // Add WAL edits by CP
3298          WALEdit fromCP = walEditsFromCoprocessors[index];
3299          if (fromCP != null) {
3300            for (Cell cell : fromCP.getCells()) {
3301              walEdit.add(cell);
3302            }
3303          }
3304          addFamilyMapToWALEdit(familyCellMaps[index], walEdit);
3305
3306          return true;
3307        }
3308      });
3309      return walEdits;
3310    }
3311
3312    /**
3313     * This method completes mini-batch operations by calling postBatchMutate() CP hook (if
3314     * required) and completing mvcc.
3315     */
3316    public void completeMiniBatchOperations(
3317        final MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> miniBatchOp, final WriteEntry writeEntry)
3318        throws IOException {
3319      if (writeEntry != null) {
3320        region.mvcc.completeAndWait(writeEntry);
3321      }
3322    }
3323
3324    public void doPostOpCleanupForMiniBatch(
3325        final MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> miniBatchOp, final WALEdit walEdit,
3326        boolean success) throws IOException {
3327      doFinishHotnessProtector(miniBatchOp);
3328    }
3329
3330    private void doFinishHotnessProtector(
3331        final MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> miniBatchOp) {
3332      // check and return if the protector is not enabled
3333      if (!region.storeHotnessProtector.isEnable()) {
3334        return;
3335      }
3336      // miniBatchOp is null, if and only if lockRowsAndBuildMiniBatch throwing exception.
3337      // This case was handled.
3338      if (miniBatchOp == null) {
3339        return;
3340      }
3341
3342      final int finalLastIndexExclusive = miniBatchOp.getLastIndexExclusive();
3343
3344      for (int i = nextIndexToProcess; i < finalLastIndexExclusive; i++) {
3345        switch (retCodeDetails[i].getOperationStatusCode()) {
3346          case SUCCESS:
3347          case FAILURE:
3348            region.storeHotnessProtector.finish(getMutation(i).getFamilyCellMap());
3349            break;
3350          default:
3351            // do nothing
3352            // We won't start the protector for NOT_RUN/BAD_FAMILY/SANITY_CHECK_FAILURE and the
3353            // STORE_TOO_BUSY case is handled in StoreHotnessProtector#start
3354            break;
3355        }
3356      }
3357    }
3358
3359    /**
3360     * Atomically apply the given map of family->edits to the memstore.
3361     * This handles the consistency control on its own, but the caller
3362     * should already have locked updatesLock.readLock(). This also does
3363     * <b>not</b> check the families for validity.
3364     *
3365     * @param familyMap Map of Cells by family
3366     */
3367    protected void applyFamilyMapToMemStore(Map<byte[], List<Cell>> familyMap,
3368        MemStoreSizing memstoreAccounting) throws IOException {
3369      for (Map.Entry<byte[], List<Cell>> e : familyMap.entrySet()) {
3370        byte[] family = e.getKey();
3371        List<Cell> cells = e.getValue();
3372        assert cells instanceof RandomAccess;
3373        region.applyToMemStore(region.getStore(family), cells, false, memstoreAccounting);
3374      }
3375    }
3376
3377    /**
3378     * Append the given map of family->edits to a WALEdit data structure.
3379     * This does not write to the WAL itself.
3380     * @param familyMap map of family->edits
3381     * @param walEdit the destination entry to append into
3382     */
3383    private void addFamilyMapToWALEdit(Map<byte[], List<Cell>> familyMap,
3384        WALEdit walEdit) {
3385      for (List<Cell> edits : familyMap.values()) {
3386        // Optimization: 'foreach' loop is not used. See:
3387        // HBASE-12023 HRegion.applyFamilyMapToMemstore creates too many iterator objects
3388        assert edits instanceof RandomAccess;
3389        int listSize = edits.size();
3390        for (int i=0; i < listSize; i++) {
3391          Cell cell = edits.get(i);
3392          walEdit.add(cell);
3393        }
3394      }
3395    }
3396  }
3397
3398  /**
3399   * Batch of mutation operations. Base class is shared with {@link ReplayBatchOperation} as most
3400   * of the logic is same.
3401   */
3402  static class MutationBatchOperation extends BatchOperation<Mutation> {
3403    private long nonceGroup;
3404    private long nonce;
3405    public MutationBatchOperation(final HRegion region, Mutation[] operations, boolean atomic,
3406        long nonceGroup, long nonce) {
3407      super(region, operations);
3408      this.atomic = atomic;
3409      this.nonceGroup = nonceGroup;
3410      this.nonce = nonce;
3411    }
3412
3413    @Override
3414    public Mutation getMutation(int index) {
3415      return this.operations[index];
3416    }
3417
3418    @Override
3419    public long getNonceGroup(int index) {
3420      return nonceGroup;
3421    }
3422
3423    @Override
3424    public long getNonce(int index) {
3425      return nonce;
3426    }
3427
3428    @Override
3429    public Mutation[] getMutationsForCoprocs() {
3430      return this.operations;
3431    }
3432
3433    @Override
3434    public boolean isInReplay() {
3435      return false;
3436    }
3437
3438    @Override
3439    public long getOrigLogSeqNum() {
3440      return SequenceId.NO_SEQUENCE_ID;
3441    }
3442
3443    @Override
3444    public void startRegionOperation() throws IOException {
3445      region.startRegionOperation(Operation.BATCH_MUTATE);
3446    }
3447
3448    @Override
3449    public void closeRegionOperation() throws IOException {
3450      region.closeRegionOperation(Operation.BATCH_MUTATE);
3451    }
3452
3453    @Override
3454    public void checkAndPreparePut(Put p) throws IOException {
3455      region.checkFamilies(p.getFamilyCellMap().keySet());
3456    }
3457
3458    @Override
3459    public void checkAndPrepare() throws IOException {
3460      final int[] metrics = {0, 0}; // index 0: puts, index 1: deletes
3461      visitBatchOperations(true, this.size(), new Visitor() {
3462        private long now = EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime();
3463        private WALEdit walEdit;
3464        @Override
3465        public boolean visit(int index) throws IOException {
3466          // Run coprocessor pre hook outside of locks to avoid deadlock
3467          if (region.coprocessorHost != null) {
3468            if (walEdit == null) {
3469              walEdit = new WALEdit();
3470            }
3471            callPreMutateCPHook(index, walEdit, metrics);
3472            if (!walEdit.isEmpty()) {
3473              walEditsFromCoprocessors[index] = walEdit;
3474              walEdit = null;
3475            }
3476          }
3477          if (isOperationPending(index)) {
3478            // TODO: Currently validation is done with current time before acquiring locks and
3479            // updates are done with different timestamps after acquiring locks. This behavior is
3480            // inherited from the code prior to this change. Can this be changed?
3481            checkAndPrepareMutation(index, now);
3482          }
3483          return true;
3484        }
3485      });
3486
3487      // FIXME: we may update metrics twice! here for all operations bypassed by CP and later in
3488      // normal processing.
3489      // Update metrics in same way as it is done when we go the normal processing route (we now
3490      // update general metrics though a Coprocessor did the work).
3491      if (region.metricsRegion != null) {
3492        if (metrics[0] > 0) {
3493          // There were some Puts in the batch.
3494          region.metricsRegion.updatePut();
3495        }
3496        if (metrics[1] > 0) {
3497          // There were some Deletes in the batch.
3498          region.metricsRegion.updateDelete();
3499        }
3500      }
3501    }
3502
3503    @Override
3504    public void prepareMiniBatchOperations(MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> miniBatchOp,
3505        long timestamp, final List<RowLock> acquiredRowLocks) throws IOException {
3506      byte[] byteTS = Bytes.toBytes(timestamp);
3507      visitBatchOperations(true, miniBatchOp.getLastIndexExclusive(), (int index) -> {
3508        Mutation mutation = getMutation(index);
3509        if (mutation instanceof Put) {
3510          region.updateCellTimestamps(familyCellMaps[index].values(), byteTS);
3511          miniBatchOp.incrementNumOfPuts();
3512        } else {
3513          region.prepareDeleteTimestamps(mutation, familyCellMaps[index], byteTS);
3514          miniBatchOp.incrementNumOfDeletes();
3515        }
3516        region.rewriteCellTags(familyCellMaps[index], mutation);
3517
3518        // update cell count
3519        if (region.getEffectiveDurability(mutation.getDurability()) != Durability.SKIP_WAL) {
3520          for (List<Cell> cells : mutation.getFamilyCellMap().values()) {
3521            miniBatchOp.addCellCount(cells.size());
3522          }
3523        }
3524
3525        WALEdit fromCP = walEditsFromCoprocessors[index];
3526        if (fromCP != null) {
3527          miniBatchOp.addCellCount(fromCP.size());
3528        }
3529        return true;
3530      });
3531
3532      if (region.coprocessorHost != null) {
3533        // calling the pre CP hook for batch mutation
3534        region.coprocessorHost.preBatchMutate(miniBatchOp);
3535        checkAndMergeCPMutations(miniBatchOp, acquiredRowLocks, timestamp);
3536      }
3537    }
3538
3539    @Override
3540    public List<Pair<NonceKey, WALEdit>> buildWALEdits(final MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation>
3541        miniBatchOp) throws IOException {
3542      List<Pair<NonceKey, WALEdit>> walEdits = super.buildWALEdits(miniBatchOp);
3543      // for MutationBatchOperation, more than one nonce is not allowed
3544      if (walEdits.size() > 1) {
3545        throw new IOException("Found multiple nonce keys per batch!");
3546      }
3547      return walEdits;
3548    }
3549
3550    @Override
3551    public WriteEntry writeMiniBatchOperationsToMemStore(
3552        final MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> miniBatchOp, @Nullable WriteEntry writeEntry)
3553        throws IOException {
3554      if (writeEntry == null) {
3555        writeEntry = region.mvcc.begin();
3556      }
3557      super.writeMiniBatchOperationsToMemStore(miniBatchOp, writeEntry.getWriteNumber());
3558      return writeEntry;
3559    }
3560
3561    @Override
3562    public void completeMiniBatchOperations(
3563        final MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> miniBatchOp, final WriteEntry writeEntry)
3564        throws IOException {
3565      // TODO: can it be done after completing mvcc?
3566      // calling the post CP hook for batch mutation
3567      if (region.coprocessorHost != null) {
3568        region.coprocessorHost.postBatchMutate(miniBatchOp);
3569      }
3570      super.completeMiniBatchOperations(miniBatchOp, writeEntry);
3571    }
3572
3573    @Override
3574    public void doPostOpCleanupForMiniBatch(MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> miniBatchOp,
3575        final WALEdit walEdit, boolean success) throws IOException {
3576
3577      super.doPostOpCleanupForMiniBatch(miniBatchOp, walEdit, success);
3578      if (miniBatchOp != null) {
3579        // synced so that the coprocessor contract is adhered to.
3580        if (region.coprocessorHost != null) {
3581          visitBatchOperations(false, miniBatchOp.getLastIndexExclusive(), (int i) -> {
3582            // only for successful puts
3583            if (retCodeDetails[i].getOperationStatusCode() == OperationStatusCode.SUCCESS) {
3584              Mutation m = getMutation(i);
3585              if (m instanceof Put) {
3586                region.coprocessorHost.postPut((Put) m, walEdit, m.getDurability());
3587              } else {
3588                region.coprocessorHost.postDelete((Delete) m, walEdit, m.getDurability());
3589              }
3590            }
3591            return true;
3592          });
3593        }
3594
3595        // See if the column families were consistent through the whole thing.
3596        // if they were then keep them. If they were not then pass a null.
3597        // null will be treated as unknown.
3598        // Total time taken might be involving Puts and Deletes.
3599        // Split the time for puts and deletes based on the total number of Puts and Deletes.
3600        if (region.metricsRegion != null) {
3601          if (miniBatchOp.getNumOfPuts() > 0) {
3602            // There were some Puts in the batch.
3603            region.metricsRegion.updatePut();
3604          }
3605          if (miniBatchOp.getNumOfDeletes() > 0) {
3606            // There were some Deletes in the batch.
3607            region.metricsRegion.updateDelete();
3608          }
3609        }
3610      }
3611
3612      if (region.coprocessorHost != null) {
3613        // call the coprocessor hook to do any finalization steps after the put is done
3614        region.coprocessorHost.postBatchMutateIndispensably(
3615            miniBatchOp != null ? miniBatchOp : createMiniBatch(size(), 0), success);
3616      }
3617    }
3618
3619    /**
3620     * Runs prePut/ preDelete coprocessor hook for input mutation in a batch
3621     * @param metrics Array of 2 ints. index 0: count of puts and index 1: count of deletes
3622     */
3623    private void callPreMutateCPHook(int index, final WALEdit walEdit, final int[] metrics)
3624        throws IOException {
3625      Mutation m = getMutation(index);
3626      if (m instanceof Put) {
3627        if (region.coprocessorHost.prePut((Put) m, walEdit, m.getDurability())) {
3628          // pre hook says skip this Put
3629          // mark as success and skip in doMiniBatchMutation
3630          metrics[0]++;
3631          retCodeDetails[index] = OperationStatus.SUCCESS;
3632        }
3633      } else if (m instanceof Delete) {
3634        Delete curDel = (Delete) m;
3635        if (curDel.getFamilyCellMap().isEmpty()) {
3636          // handle deleting a row case
3637          // TODO: prepareDelete() has been called twice, before and after preDelete() CP hook.
3638          // Can this be avoided?
3639          region.prepareDelete(curDel);
3640        }
3641        if (region.coprocessorHost.preDelete(curDel, walEdit, m.getDurability())) {
3642          // pre hook says skip this Delete
3643          // mark as success and skip in doMiniBatchMutation
3644          metrics[1]++;
3645          retCodeDetails[index] = OperationStatus.SUCCESS;
3646        }
3647      } else {
3648        String msg = "Put/Delete mutations only supported in a batch";
3649        // In case of passing Append mutations along with the Puts and Deletes in batchMutate
3650        // mark the operation return code as failure so that it will not be considered in
3651        // the doMiniBatchMutation
3652        retCodeDetails[index] = new OperationStatus(OperationStatusCode.FAILURE, msg);
3653
3654        if (isAtomic()) { // fail, atomic means all or none
3655          throw new IOException(msg);
3656        }
3657      }
3658    }
3659
3660    private void checkAndMergeCPMutations(final MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> miniBatchOp,
3661        final List<RowLock> acquiredRowLocks, final long timestamp) throws IOException {
3662      visitBatchOperations(true, nextIndexToProcess + miniBatchOp.size(), (int i) -> {
3663        // we pass (i - firstIndex) below since the call expects a relative index
3664        Mutation[] cpMutations = miniBatchOp.getOperationsFromCoprocessors(i - nextIndexToProcess);
3665        if (cpMutations == null) {
3666          return true;
3667        }
3668        // Else Coprocessor added more Mutations corresponding to the Mutation at this index.
3669        Mutation mutation = getMutation(i);
3670        for (Mutation cpMutation : cpMutations) {
3671          this.checkAndPrepareMutation(cpMutation, timestamp);
3672
3673          // Acquire row locks. If not, the whole batch will fail.
3674          acquiredRowLocks.add(region.getRowLockInternal(cpMutation.getRow(), true, null));
3675
3676          // Returned mutations from coprocessor correspond to the Mutation at index i. We can
3677          // directly add the cells from those mutations to the familyMaps of this mutation.
3678          Map<byte[], List<Cell>> cpFamilyMap = cpMutation.getFamilyCellMap();
3679          // will get added to the memStore later
3680          mergeFamilyMaps(familyCellMaps[i], cpFamilyMap);
3681
3682          // The durability of returned mutation is replaced by the corresponding mutation.
3683          // If the corresponding mutation contains the SKIP_WAL, we shouldn't count the
3684          // cells of returned mutation.
3685          if (region.getEffectiveDurability(mutation.getDurability()) != Durability.SKIP_WAL) {
3686            for (List<Cell> cells : cpFamilyMap.values()) {
3687              miniBatchOp.addCellCount(cells.size());
3688            }
3689          }
3690        }
3691        return true;
3692      });
3693    }
3694
3695    private void mergeFamilyMaps(Map<byte[], List<Cell>> familyMap,
3696        Map<byte[], List<Cell>> toBeMerged) {
3697      for (Map.Entry<byte[], List<Cell>> entry : toBeMerged.entrySet()) {
3698        List<Cell> cells = familyMap.get(entry.getKey());
3699        if (cells == null) {
3700          familyMap.put(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue());
3701        } else {
3702          cells.addAll(entry.getValue());
3703        }
3704      }
3705    }
3706  }
3707
3708  /**
3709   * Batch of mutations for replay. Base class is shared with {@link MutationBatchOperation} as most
3710   * of the logic is same.
3711   */
3712  static class ReplayBatchOperation extends BatchOperation<MutationReplay> {
3713    private long origLogSeqNum = 0;
3714    public ReplayBatchOperation(final HRegion region, MutationReplay[] operations,
3715        long origLogSeqNum) {
3716      super(region, operations);
3717      this.origLogSeqNum = origLogSeqNum;
3718    }
3719
3720    @Override
3721    public Mutation getMutation(int index) {
3722      return this.operations[index].mutation;
3723    }
3724
3725    @Override
3726    public long getNonceGroup(int index) {
3727      return this.operations[index].nonceGroup;
3728    }
3729
3730    @Override
3731    public long getNonce(int index) {
3732      return this.operations[index].nonce;
3733    }
3734
3735    @Override
3736    public Mutation[] getMutationsForCoprocs() {
3737      return null;
3738    }
3739
3740    @Override
3741    public boolean isInReplay() {
3742      return true;
3743    }
3744
3745    @Override
3746    public long getOrigLogSeqNum() {
3747      return this.origLogSeqNum;
3748    }
3749
3750    @Override
3751    public void startRegionOperation() throws IOException {
3752      region.startRegionOperation(Operation.REPLAY_BATCH_MUTATE);
3753    }
3754
3755    @Override
3756    public void closeRegionOperation() throws IOException {
3757      region.closeRegionOperation(Operation.REPLAY_BATCH_MUTATE);
3758    }
3759
3760    /**
3761     * During replay, there could exist column families which are removed between region server
3762     * failure and replay
3763     */
3764    @Override
3765    protected void checkAndPreparePut(Put p) throws IOException {
3766      Map<byte[], List<Cell>> familyCellMap = p.getFamilyCellMap();
3767      List<byte[]> nonExistentList = null;
3768      for (byte[] family : familyCellMap.keySet()) {
3769        if (!region.htableDescriptor.hasColumnFamily(family)) {
3770          if (nonExistentList == null) {
3771            nonExistentList = new ArrayList<>();
3772          }
3773          nonExistentList.add(family);
3774        }
3775      }
3776      if (nonExistentList != null) {
3777        for (byte[] family : nonExistentList) {
3778          // Perhaps schema was changed between crash and replay
3779          LOG.info("No family for " + Bytes.toString(family) + " omit from reply.");
3780          familyCellMap.remove(family);
3781        }
3782      }
3783    }
3784
3785    @Override
3786    public void checkAndPrepare() throws IOException {
3787      long now = EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime();
3788      visitBatchOperations(true, this.size(), (int index) -> {
3789        checkAndPrepareMutation(index, now);
3790        return true;
3791      });
3792    }
3793
3794    @Override
3795    public void prepareMiniBatchOperations(MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> miniBatchOp,
3796        long timestamp, final List<RowLock> acquiredRowLocks) throws IOException {
3797      visitBatchOperations(true, miniBatchOp.getLastIndexExclusive(), (int index) -> {
3798        // update cell count
3799        for (List<Cell> cells : getMutation(index).getFamilyCellMap().values()) {
3800          miniBatchOp.addCellCount(cells.size());
3801        }
3802        return true;
3803      });
3804    }
3805
3806    @Override
3807    public WriteEntry writeMiniBatchOperationsToMemStore(
3808        final MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> miniBatchOp, final WriteEntry writeEntry)
3809        throws IOException {
3810      super.writeMiniBatchOperationsToMemStore(miniBatchOp, getOrigLogSeqNum());
3811      return writeEntry;
3812    }
3813
3814    @Override
3815    public void completeMiniBatchOperations(
3816        final MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> miniBatchOp, final WriteEntry writeEntry)
3817        throws IOException {
3818      super.completeMiniBatchOperations(miniBatchOp, writeEntry);
3819      region.mvcc.advanceTo(getOrigLogSeqNum());
3820    }
3821  }

3823  public OperationStatus[] batchMutate(Mutation[] mutations, long nonceGroup, long nonce)
3824      throws IOException {
3825    return batchMutate(mutations, false, nonceGroup, nonce);
3826  }
3827
3828  public OperationStatus[] batchMutate(Mutation[] mutations, boolean atomic, long nonceGroup,
3829      long nonce) throws IOException {
3830    // As it stands, this is used for 3 things
3831    //  * batchMutate with single mutation - put/delete, separate or from checkAndMutate.
3832    //  * coprocessor calls (see ex. BulkDeleteEndpoint).
3833    // So nonces are not really ever used by HBase. They could be by coprocs, and checkAnd...
3834    return batchMutate(new MutationBatchOperation(this, mutations, atomic, nonceGroup, nonce));
3835  }
3836
3837  @Override
3838  public OperationStatus[] batchMutate(Mutation[] mutations) throws IOException {
3839    return batchMutate(mutations, HConstants.NO_NONCE, HConstants.NO_NONCE);
3840  }
3841
3842  public OperationStatus[] batchReplay(MutationReplay[] mutations, long replaySeqId)
3843      throws IOException {
3844    if (!RegionReplicaUtil.isDefaultReplica(getRegionInfo())
3845        && replaySeqId < lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId) {
3846      // if it is a secondary replica we should ignore these entries silently
3847      // since they are coming out of order
3848      if (LOG.isTraceEnabled()) {
3849        LOG.trace(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
3850          + "Skipping " + mutations.length + " mutations with replaySeqId=" + replaySeqId
3851          + " which is < than lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId=" + lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId);
3852        for (MutationReplay mut : mutations) {
3853          LOG.trace(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : Skipping : " + mut.mutation);
3854        }
3855      }
3856
3857      OperationStatus[] statuses = new OperationStatus[mutations.length];
3858      for (int i = 0; i < statuses.length; i++) {
3859        statuses[i] = OperationStatus.SUCCESS;
3860      }
3861      return statuses;
3862    }
3863    return batchMutate(new ReplayBatchOperation(this, mutations, replaySeqId));
3864  }
3865
3866  /**
3867   * Perform a batch of mutations.
3868   *
3869   * It supports only Put and Delete mutations and will ignore other types passed. Operations in
3870   * a batch are stored with highest durability specified of for all operations in a batch,
3871   * except for {@link Durability#SKIP_WAL}.
3872   *
3873   * <p>This function is called from {@link #batchReplay(MutationReplay[], long)} with
3874   * {@link ReplayBatchOperation} instance and {@link #batchMutate(Mutation[], long, long)} with
3875   * {@link MutationBatchOperation} instance as an argument. As the processing of replay batch
3876   * and mutation batch is very similar, lot of code is shared by providing generic methods in
3877   * base class {@link BatchOperation}. The logic for this method and
3878   * {@link #doMiniBatchMutate(BatchOperation)} is implemented using methods in base class which
3879   * are overridden by derived classes to implement special behavior.
3880   *
3881   * @param batchOp contains the list of mutations
3882   * @return an array of OperationStatus which internally contains the
3883   *         OperationStatusCode and the exceptionMessage if any.
3884   * @throws IOException
3885   */
3886  OperationStatus[] batchMutate(BatchOperation<?> batchOp) throws IOException {
3887    boolean initialized = false;
3888    batchOp.startRegionOperation();
3889    try {
3890      while (!batchOp.isDone()) {
3891        if (!batchOp.isInReplay()) {
3892          checkReadOnly();
3893        }
3894        checkResources();
3895
3896        if (!initialized) {
3897          this.writeRequestsCount.add(batchOp.size());
3898          // validate and prepare batch for write, for MutationBatchOperation it also calls CP
3899          // prePut()/ preDelete() hooks
3900          batchOp.checkAndPrepare();
3901          initialized = true;
3902        }
3903        doMiniBatchMutate(batchOp);
3904        requestFlushIfNeeded();
3905      }
3906    } finally {
3907      batchOp.closeRegionOperation();
3908    }
3909    return batchOp.retCodeDetails;
3910  }
3911
3912  /**
3913   * Called to do a piece of the batch that came in to {@link #batchMutate(Mutation[], long, long)}
3914   * In here we also handle replay of edits on region recover.
3915   * @return Change in size brought about by applying <code>batchOp</code>
3916   */
3917  private void doMiniBatchMutate(BatchOperation<?> batchOp) throws IOException {
3918    boolean success = false;
3919    WALEdit walEdit = null;
3920    WriteEntry writeEntry = null;
3921    boolean locked = false;
3922    // We try to set up a batch in the range [batchOp.nextIndexToProcess,lastIndexExclusive)
3923    MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> miniBatchOp = null;
3924    /** Keep track of the locks we hold so we can release them in finally clause */
3925    List<RowLock> acquiredRowLocks = Lists.newArrayListWithCapacity(batchOp.size());
3926    try {
3927      // STEP 1. Try to acquire as many locks as we can and build mini-batch of operations with
3928      // locked rows
3929      miniBatchOp = batchOp.lockRowsAndBuildMiniBatch(acquiredRowLocks);
3930
3931      // We've now grabbed as many mutations off the list as we can
3932      // Ensure we acquire at least one.
3933      if (miniBatchOp.getReadyToWriteCount() <= 0) {
3934        // Nothing to put/delete -- an exception in the above such as NoSuchColumnFamily?
3935        return;
3936      }
3937
3938      lock(this.updatesLock.readLock(), miniBatchOp.getReadyToWriteCount());
3939      locked = true;
3940
3941      // STEP 2. Update mini batch of all operations in progress with  LATEST_TIMESTAMP timestamp
3942      // We should record the timestamp only after we have acquired the rowLock,
3943      // otherwise, newer puts/deletes are not guaranteed to have a newer timestamp
3944      long now = EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime();
3945      batchOp.prepareMiniBatchOperations(miniBatchOp, now, acquiredRowLocks);
3946
3947      // STEP 3. Build WAL edit
3948      List<Pair<NonceKey, WALEdit>> walEdits = batchOp.buildWALEdits(miniBatchOp);
3949
3950      // STEP 4. Append the WALEdits to WAL and sync.
3951      for(Iterator<Pair<NonceKey, WALEdit>> it = walEdits.iterator(); it.hasNext();) {
3952        Pair<NonceKey, WALEdit> nonceKeyWALEditPair = it.next();
3953        walEdit = nonceKeyWALEditPair.getSecond();
3954        NonceKey nonceKey = nonceKeyWALEditPair.getFirst();
3955
3956        if (walEdit != null && !walEdit.isEmpty()) {
3957          writeEntry = doWALAppend(walEdit, batchOp.durability, batchOp.getClusterIds(), now,
3958              nonceKey.getNonceGroup(), nonceKey.getNonce(), batchOp.getOrigLogSeqNum());
3959        }
3960
3961        // Complete mvcc for all but last writeEntry (for replay case)
3962        if (it.hasNext() && writeEntry != null) {
3963          mvcc.complete(writeEntry);
3964          writeEntry = null;
3965        }
3966      }
3967
3968      // STEP 5. Write back to memStore
3969      // NOTE: writeEntry can be null here
3970      writeEntry = batchOp.writeMiniBatchOperationsToMemStore(miniBatchOp, writeEntry);
3971
3972      // STEP 6. Complete MiniBatchOperations: If required calls postBatchMutate() CP hook and
3973      // complete mvcc for last writeEntry
3974      batchOp.completeMiniBatchOperations(miniBatchOp, writeEntry);
3975      writeEntry = null;
3976      success = true;
3977    } finally {
3978      // Call complete rather than completeAndWait because we probably had error if walKey != null
3979      if (writeEntry != null) mvcc.complete(writeEntry);
3980
3981      if (locked) {
3982        this.updatesLock.readLock().unlock();
3983      }
3984      releaseRowLocks(acquiredRowLocks);
3985
3986      final int finalLastIndexExclusive =
3987          miniBatchOp != null ? miniBatchOp.getLastIndexExclusive() : batchOp.size();
3988      final boolean finalSuccess = success;
3989      batchOp.visitBatchOperations(true, finalLastIndexExclusive, (int i) -> {
3990        batchOp.retCodeDetails[i] =
3991            finalSuccess ? OperationStatus.SUCCESS : OperationStatus.FAILURE;
3992        return true;
3993      });
3994
3995      batchOp.doPostOpCleanupForMiniBatch(miniBatchOp, walEdit, finalSuccess);
3996
3997      batchOp.nextIndexToProcess = finalLastIndexExclusive;
3998    }
3999  }
4000
4001  /**
4002   * Returns effective durability from the passed durability and
4003   * the table descriptor.
4004   */
4005  protected Durability getEffectiveDurability(Durability d) {
4006    return d == Durability.USE_DEFAULT ? this.regionDurability : d;
4007  }
4008
4009  @Override
4010  public boolean checkAndMutate(byte [] row, byte [] family, byte [] qualifier,
4011                                CompareOperator op, ByteArrayComparable comparator, Mutation mutation, boolean writeToWAL)
4012  throws IOException{
4013    checkMutationType(mutation, row);
4014    return doCheckAndRowMutate(row, family, qualifier, op, comparator, null,
4015      mutation);
4016  }
4017
4018  @Override
4019  public boolean checkAndRowMutate(byte [] row, byte [] family, byte [] qualifier,
4020    CompareOperator op, ByteArrayComparable comparator, RowMutations rm)
4021  throws IOException {
4022    return doCheckAndRowMutate(row, family, qualifier, op, comparator, rm, null);
4023  }
4024
4025  /**
4026   * checkAndMutate and checkAndRowMutate are 90% the same. Rather than copy/paste, below has
4027   * switches in the few places where there is deviation.
4028   */
4029  private boolean doCheckAndRowMutate(byte [] row, byte [] family, byte [] qualifier,
4030                                      CompareOperator op, ByteArrayComparable comparator, RowMutations rowMutations,
4031                                      Mutation mutation)
4032  throws IOException {
4033    // Could do the below checks but seems wacky with two callers only. Just comment out for now.
4034    // One caller passes a Mutation, the other passes RowMutation. Presume all good so we don't
4035    // need these commented out checks.
4036    // if (rowMutations == null && mutation == null) throw new DoNotRetryIOException("Both null");
4037    // if (rowMutations != null && mutation != null) throw new DoNotRetryIOException("Both set");
4038    checkReadOnly();
4039    // TODO, add check for value length also move this check to the client
4040    checkResources();
4041    startRegionOperation();
4042    try {
4043      Get get = new Get(row);
4044      checkFamily(family);
4045      get.addColumn(family, qualifier);
4046      // Lock row - note that doBatchMutate will relock this row if called
4047      checkRow(row, "doCheckAndRowMutate");
4048      RowLock rowLock = getRowLockInternal(get.getRow(), false, null);
4049      try {
4050        if (mutation != null && this.getCoprocessorHost() != null) {
4051          // Call coprocessor.
4052          Boolean processed = null;
4053          if (mutation instanceof Put) {
4054            processed = this.getCoprocessorHost().preCheckAndPutAfterRowLock(row, family,
4055                qualifier, op, comparator, (Put)mutation);
4056          } else if (mutation instanceof Delete) {
4057            processed = this.getCoprocessorHost().preCheckAndDeleteAfterRowLock(row, family,
4058                qualifier, op, comparator, (Delete)mutation);
4059          }
4060          if (processed != null) {
4061            return processed;
4062          }
4063        }
4064        // NOTE: We used to wait here until mvcc caught up:  mvcc.await();
4065        // Supposition is that now all changes are done under row locks, then when we go to read,
4066        // we'll get the latest on this row.
4067        List<Cell> result = get(get, false);
4068        boolean valueIsNull = comparator.getValue() == null || comparator.getValue().length == 0;
4069        boolean matches = false;
4070        long cellTs = 0;
4071        if (result.isEmpty() && valueIsNull) {
4072          matches = true;
4073        } else if (result.size() > 0 && result.get(0).getValueLength() == 0 && valueIsNull) {
4074          matches = true;
4075          cellTs = result.get(0).getTimestamp();
4076        } else if (result.size() == 1 && !valueIsNull) {
4077          Cell kv = result.get(0);
4078          cellTs = kv.getTimestamp();
4079          int compareResult = PrivateCellUtil.compareValue(kv, comparator);
4080          matches = matches(op, compareResult);
4081        }
4082        // If matches put the new put or delete the new delete
4083        if (matches) {
4084          // We have acquired the row lock already. If the system clock is NOT monotonically
4085          // non-decreasing (see HBASE-14070) we should make sure that the mutation has a
4086          // larger timestamp than what was observed via Get. doBatchMutate already does this, but
4087          // there is no way to pass the cellTs. See HBASE-14054.
4088          long now = EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime();
4089          long ts = Math.max(now, cellTs); // ensure write is not eclipsed
4090          byte[] byteTs = Bytes.toBytes(ts);
4091          if (mutation != null) {
4092            if (mutation instanceof Put) {
4093              updateCellTimestamps(mutation.getFamilyCellMap().values(), byteTs);
4094            }
4095            // And else 'delete' is not needed since it already does a second get, and sets the
4096            // timestamp from get (see prepareDeleteTimestamps).
4097          } else {
4098            for (Mutation m: rowMutations.getMutations()) {
4099              if (m instanceof Put) {
4100                updateCellTimestamps(m.getFamilyCellMap().values(), byteTs);
4101              }
4102            }
4103            // And else 'delete' is not needed since it already does a second get, and sets the
4104            // timestamp from get (see prepareDeleteTimestamps).
4105          }
4106          // All edits for the given row (across all column families) must happen atomically.
4107          if (mutation != null) {
4108            doBatchMutate(mutation);
4109          } else {
4110            mutateRow(rowMutations);
4111          }
4112          this.checkAndMutateChecksPassed.increment();
4113          return true;
4114        }
4115        this.checkAndMutateChecksFailed.increment();
4116        return false;
4117      } finally {
4118        rowLock.release();
4119      }
4120    } finally {
4121      closeRegionOperation();
4122    }
4123  }
4124
4125  private void checkMutationType(final Mutation mutation, final byte [] row)
4126  throws DoNotRetryIOException {
4127    boolean isPut = mutation instanceof Put;
4128    if (!isPut && !(mutation instanceof Delete)) {
4129      throw new org.apache.hadoop.hbase.DoNotRetryIOException("Action must be Put or Delete");
4130    }
4131    if (!Bytes.equals(row, mutation.getRow())) {
4132      throw new org.apache.hadoop.hbase.DoNotRetryIOException("Action's getRow must match");
4133    }
4134  }
4135
4136  private boolean matches(final CompareOperator op, final int compareResult) {
4137    boolean matches = false;
4138    switch (op) {
4139      case LESS:
4140        matches = compareResult < 0;
4141        break;
4142      case LESS_OR_EQUAL:
4143        matches = compareResult <= 0;
4144        break;
4145      case EQUAL:
4146        matches = compareResult == 0;
4147        break;
4148      case NOT_EQUAL:
4149        matches = compareResult != 0;
4150        break;
4151      case GREATER_OR_EQUAL:
4152        matches = compareResult >= 0;
4153        break;
4154      case GREATER:
4155        matches = compareResult > 0;
4156        break;
4157      default:
4158        throw new RuntimeException("Unknown Compare op " + op.name());
4159    }
4160    return matches;
4161  }
4162
4163
4164  private void doBatchMutate(Mutation mutation) throws IOException {
4165    // Currently this is only called for puts and deletes, so no nonces.
4166    OperationStatus[] batchMutate = this.batchMutate(new Mutation[]{mutation});
4167    if (batchMutate[0].getOperationStatusCode().equals(OperationStatusCode.SANITY_CHECK_FAILURE)) {
4168      throw new FailedSanityCheckException(batchMutate[0].getExceptionMsg());
4169    } else if (batchMutate[0].getOperationStatusCode().equals(OperationStatusCode.BAD_FAMILY)) {
4170      throw new NoSuchColumnFamilyException(batchMutate[0].getExceptionMsg());
4171    } else if (batchMutate[0].getOperationStatusCode().equals(OperationStatusCode.STORE_TOO_BUSY)) {
4172      throw new RegionTooBusyException(batchMutate[0].getExceptionMsg());
4173    }
4174  }
4175
4176  /**
4177   * Complete taking the snapshot on the region. Writes the region info and adds references to the
4178   * working snapshot directory.
4179   *
4180   * TODO for api consistency, consider adding another version with no {@link ForeignExceptionSnare}
4181   * arg.  (In the future other cancellable HRegion methods could eventually add a
4182   * {@link ForeignExceptionSnare}, or we could do something fancier).
4183   *
4184   * @param desc snapshot description object
4185   * @param exnSnare ForeignExceptionSnare that captures external exceptions in case we need to
4186   *   bail out.  This is allowed to be null and will just be ignored in that case.
4187   * @throws IOException if there is an external or internal error causing the snapshot to fail
4188   */
4189  public void addRegionToSnapshot(SnapshotDescription desc,
4190      ForeignExceptionSnare exnSnare) throws IOException {
4191    Path rootDir = FSUtils.getRootDir(conf);
4192    Path snapshotDir = SnapshotDescriptionUtils.getWorkingSnapshotDir(desc, rootDir);
4193
4194    SnapshotManifest manifest = SnapshotManifest.create(conf, getFilesystem(),
4195            snapshotDir, desc, exnSnare);
4196    manifest.addRegion(this);
4197  }
4198
4199  private void updateSequenceId(final Iterable<List<Cell>> cellItr, final long sequenceId)
4200      throws IOException {
4201    for (List<Cell> cells: cellItr) {
4202      if (cells == null) return;
4203      for (Cell cell : cells) {
4204        PrivateCellUtil.setSequenceId(cell, sequenceId);
4205      }
4206    }
4207  }
4208
4209  /**
4210   * Replace any cell timestamps set to {@link org.apache.hadoop.hbase.HConstants#LATEST_TIMESTAMP}
4211   * provided current timestamp.
4212   * @param cellItr
4213   * @param now
4214   */
4215  public void updateCellTimestamps(final Iterable<List<Cell>> cellItr, final byte[] now)
4216      throws IOException {
4217    for (List<Cell> cells: cellItr) {
4218      if (cells == null) continue;
4219      // Optimization: 'foreach' loop is not used. See:
4220      // HBASE-12023 HRegion.applyFamilyMapToMemstore creates too many iterator objects
4221      assert cells instanceof RandomAccess;
4222      int listSize = cells.size();
4223      for (int i = 0; i < listSize; i++) {
4224        PrivateCellUtil.updateLatestStamp(cells.get(i), now);
4225      }
4226    }
4227  }
4228
4229  /**
4230   * Possibly rewrite incoming cell tags.
4231   */
4232  void rewriteCellTags(Map<byte[], List<Cell>> familyMap, final Mutation m) {
4233    // Check if we have any work to do and early out otherwise
4234    // Update these checks as more logic is added here
4235    if (m.getTTL() == Long.MAX_VALUE) {
4236      return;
4237    }
4238
4239    // From this point we know we have some work to do
4240    for (Map.Entry<byte[], List<Cell>> e: familyMap.entrySet()) {
4241      List<Cell> cells = e.getValue();
4242      assert cells instanceof RandomAccess;
4243      int listSize = cells.size();
4244      for (int i = 0; i < listSize; i++) {
4245        Cell cell = cells.get(i);
4246        List<Tag> newTags = TagUtil.carryForwardTags(null, cell);
4247        newTags = TagUtil.carryForwardTTLTag(newTags, m.getTTL());
4248        // Rewrite the cell with the updated set of tags
4249        cells.set(i, PrivateCellUtil.createCell(cell, newTags));
4250      }
4251    }
4252  }
4253
4254  /*
4255   * Check if resources to support an update.
4256   *
4257   * We throw RegionTooBusyException if above memstore limit
4258   * and expect client to retry using some kind of backoff
4259  */
4260  void checkResources() throws RegionTooBusyException {
4261    // If catalog region, do not impose resource constraints or block updates.
4262    if (this.getRegionInfo().isMetaRegion()) return;
4263
4264    if (this.memStoreSize.getHeapSize()
4265        + this.memStoreSize.getOffHeapSize() > this.blockingMemStoreSize) {
4266      blockedRequestsCount.increment();
4267      requestFlush();
4268      // Don't print current limit because it will vary too much. The message is used as a key
4269      // over in RetriesExhaustedWithDetailsException processing.
4270      throw new RegionTooBusyException("Over memstore limit; regionName=" +
4271          (this.getRegionInfo() == null? "unknown": this.getRegionInfo().getEncodedName()) +
4272          ", server=" + (this.getRegionServerServices() == null ? "unknown":
4273          this.getRegionServerServices().getServerName()) +
4274          ", blockingMemStoreSize=" +
4275          org.apache.hadoop.hbase.procedure2.util.StringUtils.humanSize(blockingMemStoreSize));
4276    }
4277  }
4278
4279  /**
4280   * @throws IOException Throws exception if region is in read-only mode.
4281   */
4282  protected void checkReadOnly() throws IOException {
4283    if (isReadOnly()) {
4284      throw new DoNotRetryIOException("region is read only");
4285    }
4286  }
4287
4288  protected void checkReadsEnabled() throws IOException {
4289    if (!this.writestate.readsEnabled) {
4290      throw new IOException(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName()
4291        + ": The region's reads are disabled. Cannot serve the request");
4292    }
4293  }
4294
4295  public void setReadsEnabled(boolean readsEnabled) {
4296   if (readsEnabled && !this.writestate.readsEnabled) {
4297     LOG.info(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : Enabling reads for region.");
4298    }
4299    this.writestate.setReadsEnabled(readsEnabled);
4300  }
4301
4302  /**
4303   * Add updates first to the wal and then add values to memstore.
4304   * Warning: Assumption is caller has lock on passed in row.
4305   * @param edits Cell updates by column
4306   * @throws IOException
4307   */
4308  void put(final byte [] row, byte [] family, List<Cell> edits)
4309  throws IOException {
4310    NavigableMap<byte[], List<Cell>> familyMap;
4311    familyMap = new TreeMap<>(Bytes.BYTES_COMPARATOR);
4312
4313    familyMap.put(family, edits);
4314    Put p = new Put(row);
4315    p.setFamilyCellMap(familyMap);
4316    doBatchMutate(p);
4317  }
4318
4319  /**
4320   * @param delta If we are doing delta changes -- e.g. increment/append -- then this flag will be
4321   *          set; when set we will run operations that make sense in the increment/append scenario
4322   *          but that do not make sense otherwise.
4323   * @see #applyToMemStore(HStore, Cell, MemStoreSizing)
4324   */
4325  private void applyToMemStore(HStore store, List<Cell> cells, boolean delta,
4326      MemStoreSizing memstoreAccounting) throws IOException {
4327    // Any change in how we update Store/MemStore needs to also be done in other applyToMemStore!!!!
4328    boolean upsert = delta && store.getColumnFamilyDescriptor().getMaxVersions() == 1;
4329    if (upsert) {
4330      store.upsert(cells, getSmallestReadPoint(), memstoreAccounting);
4331    } else {
4332      store.add(cells, memstoreAccounting);
4333    }
4334  }
4335
4336  /**
4337   * @see #applyToMemStore(HStore, List, boolean, MemStoreSizing)
4338   */
4339  private void applyToMemStore(HStore store, Cell cell, MemStoreSizing memstoreAccounting)
4340      throws IOException {
4341    // Any change in how we update Store/MemStore needs to also be done in other applyToMemStore!!!!
4342    if (store == null) {
4343      checkFamily(CellUtil.cloneFamily(cell));
4344      // Unreachable because checkFamily will throw exception
4345    }
4346    store.add(cell, memstoreAccounting);
4347  }
4348
4349  /**
4350   * Check the collection of families for validity.
4351   * @param families
4352   * @throws NoSuchColumnFamilyException
4353   */
4354  public void checkFamilies(Collection<byte[]> families) throws NoSuchColumnFamilyException {
4355    for (byte[] family : families) {
4356      checkFamily(family);
4357    }
4358  }
4359
4360  /**
4361   * Check the collection of families for valid timestamps
4362   * @param familyMap
4363   * @param now current timestamp
4364   * @throws FailedSanityCheckException
4365   */
4366  public void checkTimestamps(final Map<byte[], List<Cell>> familyMap, long now)
4367      throws FailedSanityCheckException {
4368    if (timestampSlop == HConstants.LATEST_TIMESTAMP) {
4369      return;
4370    }
4371    long maxTs = now + timestampSlop;
4372    for (List<Cell> kvs : familyMap.values()) {
4373      // Optimization: 'foreach' loop is not used. See:
4374      // HBASE-12023 HRegion.applyFamilyMapToMemstore creates too many iterator objects
4375      assert kvs instanceof RandomAccess;
4376      int listSize  = kvs.size();
4377      for (int i=0; i < listSize; i++) {
4378        Cell cell = kvs.get(i);
4379        // see if the user-side TS is out of range. latest = server-side
4380        long ts = cell.getTimestamp();
4381        if (ts != HConstants.LATEST_TIMESTAMP && ts > maxTs) {
4382          throw new FailedSanityCheckException("Timestamp for KV out of range "
4383              + cell + " (too.new=" + timestampSlop + ")");
4384        }
4385      }
4386    }
4387  }
4388
4389  /*
4390   * @param size
4391   * @return True if size is over the flush threshold
4392   */
4393  private boolean isFlushSize(MemStoreSize size) {
4394    return size.getHeapSize() + size.getOffHeapSize() > getMemStoreFlushSize();
4395  }
4396
4397  /**
4398   * Read the edits put under this region by wal splitting process.  Put
4399   * the recovered edits back up into this region.
4400   *
4401   * <p>We can ignore any wal message that has a sequence ID that's equal to or
4402   * lower than minSeqId.  (Because we know such messages are already
4403   * reflected in the HFiles.)
4404   *
4405   * <p>While this is running we are putting pressure on memory yet we are
4406   * outside of our usual accounting because we are not yet an onlined region
4407   * (this stuff is being run as part of Region initialization).  This means
4408   * that if we're up against global memory limits, we'll not be flagged to flush
4409   * because we are not online. We can't be flushed by usual mechanisms anyways;
4410   * we're not yet online so our relative sequenceids are not yet aligned with
4411   * WAL sequenceids -- not till we come up online, post processing of split
4412   * edits.
4413   *
4414   * <p>But to help relieve memory pressure, at least manage our own heap size
4415   * flushing if are in excess of per-region limits.  Flushing, though, we have
4416   * to be careful and avoid using the regionserver/wal sequenceid.  Its running
4417   * on a different line to whats going on in here in this region context so if we
4418   * crashed replaying these edits, but in the midst had a flush that used the
4419   * regionserver wal with a sequenceid in excess of whats going on in here
4420   * in this region and with its split editlogs, then we could miss edits the
4421   * next time we go to recover. So, we have to flush inline, using seqids that
4422   * make sense in a this single region context only -- until we online.
4423   *
4424   * @param maxSeqIdInStores Any edit found in split editlogs needs to be in excess of
4425   * the maxSeqId for the store to be applied, else its skipped.
4426   * @return the sequence id of the last edit added to this region out of the
4427   * recovered edits log or <code>minSeqId</code> if nothing added from editlogs.
4428   * @throws IOException
4429   */
4430  protected long replayRecoveredEditsIfAny(final Path regiondir,
4431      Map<byte[], Long> maxSeqIdInStores,
4432      final CancelableProgressable reporter, final MonitoredTask status)
4433      throws IOException {
4434    long minSeqIdForTheRegion = -1;
4435    for (Long maxSeqIdInStore : maxSeqIdInStores.values()) {
4436      if (maxSeqIdInStore < minSeqIdForTheRegion || minSeqIdForTheRegion == -1) {
4437        minSeqIdForTheRegion = maxSeqIdInStore;
4438      }
4439    }
4440    long seqid = minSeqIdForTheRegion;
4441
4442    FileSystem fs = this.fs.getFileSystem();
4443    NavigableSet<Path> files = WALSplitter.getSplitEditFilesSorted(fs, regiondir);
4444    if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
4445      LOG.debug("Found " + (files == null ? 0 : files.size())
4446        + " recovered edits file(s) under " + regiondir);
4447    }
4448
4449    if (files == null || files.isEmpty()) return seqid;
4450
4451    for (Path edits: files) {
4452      if (edits == null || !fs.exists(edits)) {
4453        LOG.warn("Null or non-existent edits file: " + edits);
4454        continue;
4455      }
4456      if (isZeroLengthThenDelete(fs, edits)) continue;
4457
4458      long maxSeqId;
4459      String fileName = edits.getName();
4460      maxSeqId = Math.abs(Long.parseLong(fileName));
4461      if (maxSeqId <= minSeqIdForTheRegion) {
4462        if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
4463          String msg = "Maximum sequenceid for this wal is " + maxSeqId
4464            + " and minimum sequenceid for the region is " + minSeqIdForTheRegion
4465            + ", skipped the whole file, path=" + edits;
4466          LOG.debug(msg);
4467        }
4468        continue;
4469      }
4470
4471      try {
4472        // replay the edits. Replay can return -1 if everything is skipped, only update
4473        // if seqId is greater
4474        seqid = Math.max(seqid, replayRecoveredEdits(edits, maxSeqIdInStores, reporter));
4475      } catch (IOException e) {
4476        boolean skipErrors = conf.getBoolean(
4477            HConstants.HREGION_EDITS_REPLAY_SKIP_ERRORS,
4478            conf.getBoolean(
4479                "hbase.skip.errors",
4480                HConstants.DEFAULT_HREGION_EDITS_REPLAY_SKIP_ERRORS));
4481        if (conf.get("hbase.skip.errors") != null) {
4482          LOG.warn(
4483              "The property 'hbase.skip.errors' has been deprecated. Please use " +
4484              HConstants.HREGION_EDITS_REPLAY_SKIP_ERRORS + " instead.");
4485        }
4486        if (skipErrors) {
4487          Path p = WALSplitter.moveAsideBadEditsFile(fs, edits);
4488          LOG.error(HConstants.HREGION_EDITS_REPLAY_SKIP_ERRORS
4489              + "=true so continuing. Renamed " + edits +
4490              " as " + p, e);
4491        } else {
4492          throw e;
4493        }
4494      }
4495    }
4496    // The edits size added into rsAccounting during this replaying will not
4497    // be required any more. So just clear it.
4498    if (this.rsAccounting != null) {
4499      this.rsAccounting.clearRegionReplayEditsSize(getRegionInfo().getRegionName());
4500    }
4501    if (seqid > minSeqIdForTheRegion) {
4502      // Then we added some edits to memory. Flush and cleanup split edit files.
4503      internalFlushcache(null, seqid, stores.values(), status, false, FlushLifeCycleTracker.DUMMY);
4504    }
4505    // Now delete the content of recovered edits.  We're done w/ them.
4506    if (files.size() > 0 && this.conf.getBoolean("hbase.region.archive.recovered.edits", false)) {
4507      // For debugging data loss issues!
4508      // If this flag is set, make use of the hfile archiving by making recovered.edits a fake
4509      // column family. Have to fake out file type too by casting our recovered.edits as storefiles
4510      String fakeFamilyName = WALSplitter.getRegionDirRecoveredEditsDir(regiondir).getName();
4511      Set<HStoreFile> fakeStoreFiles = new HashSet<>(files.size());
4512      for (Path file: files) {
4513        fakeStoreFiles.add(
4514          new HStoreFile(getRegionFileSystem().getFileSystem(), file, this.conf, null, null, true));
4515      }
4516      getRegionFileSystem().removeStoreFiles(fakeFamilyName, fakeStoreFiles);
4517    } else {
4518      for (Path file: files) {
4519        if (!fs.delete(file, false)) {
4520          LOG.error("Failed delete of " + file);
4521        } else {
4522          LOG.debug("Deleted recovered.edits file=" + file);
4523        }
4524      }
4525    }
4526    return seqid;
4527  }
4528
4529  /*
4530   * @param edits File of recovered edits.
4531   * @param maxSeqIdInStores Maximum sequenceid found in each store.  Edits in wal
4532   * must be larger than this to be replayed for each store.
4533   * @param reporter
4534   * @return the sequence id of the last edit added to this region out of the
4535   * recovered edits log or <code>minSeqId</code> if nothing added from editlogs.
4536   * @throws IOException
4537   */
4538  private long replayRecoveredEdits(final Path edits,
4539      Map<byte[], Long> maxSeqIdInStores, final CancelableProgressable reporter)
4540    throws IOException {
4541    String msg = "Replaying edits from " + edits;
4542    LOG.info(msg);
4543    MonitoredTask status = TaskMonitor.get().createStatus(msg);
4544    FileSystem fs = this.fs.getFileSystem();
4545
4546    status.setStatus("Opening recovered edits");
4547    WAL.Reader reader = null;
4548    try {
4549      reader = WALFactory.createReader(fs, edits, conf);
4550      long currentEditSeqId = -1;
4551      long currentReplaySeqId = -1;
4552      long firstSeqIdInLog = -1;
4553      long skippedEdits = 0;
4554      long editsCount = 0;
4555      long intervalEdits = 0;
4556      WAL.Entry entry;
4557      HStore store = null;
4558      boolean reported_once = false;
4559      ServerNonceManager ng = this.rsServices == null ? null : this.rsServices.getNonceManager();
4560
4561      try {
4562        // How many edits seen before we check elapsed time
4563        int interval = this.conf.getInt("hbase.hstore.report.interval.edits", 2000);
4564        // How often to send a progress report (default 1/2 master timeout)
4565        int period = this.conf.getInt("hbase.hstore.report.period", 300000);
4566        long lastReport = EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime();
4567
4568        if (coprocessorHost != null) {
4569          coprocessorHost.preReplayWALs(this.getRegionInfo(), edits);
4570        }
4571
4572        while ((entry = reader.next()) != null) {
4573          WALKey key = entry.getKey();
4574          WALEdit val = entry.getEdit();
4575
4576          if (ng != null) { // some test, or nonces disabled
4577            ng.reportOperationFromWal(key.getNonceGroup(), key.getNonce(), key.getWriteTime());
4578          }
4579
4580          if (reporter != null) {
4581            intervalEdits += val.size();
4582            if (intervalEdits >= interval) {
4583              // Number of edits interval reached
4584              intervalEdits = 0;
4585              long cur = EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime();
4586              if (lastReport + period <= cur) {
4587                status.setStatus("Replaying edits..." +
4588                    " skipped=" + skippedEdits +
