4589                    " edits=" + editsCount);
4590                // Timeout reached
4591                if(!reporter.progress()) {
4592                  msg = "Progressable reporter failed, stopping replay";
4593                  LOG.warn(msg);
4594                  status.abort(msg);
4595                  throw new IOException(msg);
4596                }
4597                reported_once = true;
4598                lastReport = cur;
4599              }
4600            }
4601          }
4602
4603          if (firstSeqIdInLog == -1) {
4604            firstSeqIdInLog = key.getSequenceId();
4605          }
4606          if (currentEditSeqId > key.getSequenceId()) {
4607            // when this condition is true, it means we have a serious defect because we need to
4608            // maintain increasing SeqId for WAL edits per region
4609            LOG.error(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4610                 + "Found decreasing SeqId. PreId=" + currentEditSeqId + " key=" + key
4611                + "; edit=" + val);
4612          } else {
4613            currentEditSeqId = key.getSequenceId();
4614          }
4615          currentReplaySeqId = (key.getOrigLogSeqNum() > 0) ?
4616            key.getOrigLogSeqNum() : currentEditSeqId;
4617
4618          // Start coprocessor replay here. The coprocessor is for each WALEdit
4619          // instead of a KeyValue.
4620          if (coprocessorHost != null) {
4621            status.setStatus("Running pre-WAL-restore hook in coprocessors");
4622            if (coprocessorHost.preWALRestore(this.getRegionInfo(), key, val)) {
4623              // if bypass this wal entry, ignore it ...
4624              continue;
4625            }
4626          }
4627          boolean checkRowWithinBoundary = false;
4628          // Check this edit is for this region.
4629          if (!Bytes.equals(key.getEncodedRegionName(),
4630              this.getRegionInfo().getEncodedNameAsBytes())) {
4631            checkRowWithinBoundary = true;
4632          }
4633
4634          boolean flush = false;
4635          MemStoreSizing memstoreSize = new MemStoreSizing();
4636          for (Cell cell: val.getCells()) {
4637            // Check this edit is for me. Also, guard against writing the special
4638            // METACOLUMN info such as HBASE::CACHEFLUSH entries
4639            if (CellUtil.matchingFamily(cell, WALEdit.METAFAMILY)) {
4640              // if region names don't match, skipp replaying compaction marker
4641              if (!checkRowWithinBoundary) {
4642                //this is a special edit, we should handle it
4643                CompactionDescriptor compaction = WALEdit.getCompaction(cell);
4644                if (compaction != null) {
4645                  //replay the compaction
4646                  replayWALCompactionMarker(compaction, false, true, Long.MAX_VALUE);
4647                }
4648              }
4649              skippedEdits++;
4650              continue;
4651            }
4652            // Figure which store the edit is meant for.
4653            if (store == null || !CellUtil.matchingFamily(cell,
4654                store.getColumnFamilyDescriptor().getName())) {
4655              store = getStore(cell);
4656            }
4657            if (store == null) {
4658              // This should never happen.  Perhaps schema was changed between
4659              // crash and redeploy?
4660              LOG.warn("No family for " + cell);
4661              skippedEdits++;
4662              continue;
4663            }
4664            if (checkRowWithinBoundary && !rowIsInRange(this.getRegionInfo(),
4665              cell.getRowArray(), cell.getRowOffset(), cell.getRowLength())) {
4666              LOG.warn("Row of " + cell + " is not within region boundary");
4667              skippedEdits++;
4668              continue;
4669            }
4670            // Now, figure if we should skip this edit.
4671            if (key.getSequenceId() <= maxSeqIdInStores.get(store.getColumnFamilyDescriptor()
4672                .getName())) {
4673              skippedEdits++;
4674              continue;
4675            }
4676            PrivateCellUtil.setSequenceId(cell, currentReplaySeqId);
4677
4678            restoreEdit(store, cell, memstoreSize);
4679            editsCount++;
4680          }
4681          if (this.rsAccounting != null) {
4682            rsAccounting.addRegionReplayEditsSize(getRegionInfo().getRegionName(),
4683                memstoreSize);
4684          }
4685          incMemStoreSize(memstoreSize);
4686          flush = isFlushSize(this.memStoreSize);
4687          if (flush) {
4688            internalFlushcache(null, currentEditSeqId, stores.values(), status, false,
4689              FlushLifeCycleTracker.DUMMY);
4690          }
4691
4692          if (coprocessorHost != null) {
4693            coprocessorHost.postWALRestore(this.getRegionInfo(), key, val);
4694          }
4695        }
4696
4697        if (coprocessorHost != null) {
4698          coprocessorHost.postReplayWALs(this.getRegionInfo(), edits);
4699        }
4700      } catch (EOFException eof) {
4701        Path p = WALSplitter.moveAsideBadEditsFile(fs, edits);
4702        msg = "EnLongAddered EOF. Most likely due to Master failure during " +
4703            "wal splitting, so we have this data in another edit.  " +
4704            "Continuing, but renaming " + edits + " as " + p;
4705        LOG.warn(msg, eof);
4706        status.abort(msg);
4707      } catch (IOException ioe) {
4708        // If the IOE resulted from bad file format,
4709        // then this problem is idempotent and retrying won't help
4710        if (ioe.getCause() instanceof ParseException) {
4711          Path p = WALSplitter.moveAsideBadEditsFile(fs, edits);
4712          msg = "File corruption enLongAddered!  " +
4713              "Continuing, but renaming " + edits + " as " + p;
4714          LOG.warn(msg, ioe);
4715          status.setStatus(msg);
4716        } else {
4717          status.abort(StringUtils.stringifyException(ioe));
4718          // other IO errors may be transient (bad network connection,
4719          // checksum exception on one datanode, etc).  throw & retry
4720          throw ioe;
4721        }
4722      }
4723      if (reporter != null && !reported_once) {
4724        reporter.progress();
4725      }
4726      msg = "Applied " + editsCount + ", skipped " + skippedEdits +
4727        ", firstSequenceIdInLog=" + firstSeqIdInLog +
4728        ", maxSequenceIdInLog=" + currentEditSeqId + ", path=" + edits;
4729      status.markComplete(msg);
4730      LOG.debug(msg);
4731      return currentEditSeqId;
4732    } finally {
4733      status.cleanup();
4734      if (reader != null) {
4735         reader.close();
4736      }
4737    }
4738  }
4739
4740  /**
4741   * Call to complete a compaction. Its for the case where we find in the WAL a compaction
4742   * that was not finished.  We could find one recovering a WAL after a regionserver crash.
4743   * See HBASE-2331.
4744   */
4745  void replayWALCompactionMarker(CompactionDescriptor compaction, boolean pickCompactionFiles,
4746      boolean removeFiles, long replaySeqId)
4747      throws IOException {
4748    try {
4749      checkTargetRegion(compaction.getEncodedRegionName().toByteArray(),
4750        "Compaction marker from WAL ", compaction);
4751    } catch (WrongRegionException wre) {
4752      if (RegionReplicaUtil.isDefaultReplica(this.getRegionInfo())) {
4753        // skip the compaction marker since it is not for this region
4754        return;
4755      }
4756      throw wre;
4757    }
4758
4759    synchronized (writestate) {
4760      if (replaySeqId < lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId) {
4761        LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4762            + "Skipping replaying compaction event :" + TextFormat.shortDebugString(compaction)
4763            + " because its sequence id " + replaySeqId + " is smaller than this regions "
4764            + "lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId of " + lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId);
4765        return;
4766      }
4767      if (replaySeqId < lastReplayedCompactionSeqId) {
4768        LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4769            + "Skipping replaying compaction event :" + TextFormat.shortDebugString(compaction)
4770            + " because its sequence id " + replaySeqId + " is smaller than this regions "
4771            + "lastReplayedCompactionSeqId of " + lastReplayedCompactionSeqId);
4772        return;
4773      } else {
4774        lastReplayedCompactionSeqId = replaySeqId;
4775      }
4776
4777      if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
4778        LOG.debug(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4779            + "Replaying compaction marker " + TextFormat.shortDebugString(compaction)
4780            + " with seqId=" + replaySeqId + " and lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId="
4781            + lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId);
4782      }
4783
4784      startRegionOperation(Operation.REPLAY_EVENT);
4785      try {
4786        HStore store = this.getStore(compaction.getFamilyName().toByteArray());
4787        if (store == null) {
4788          LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4789              + "Found Compaction WAL edit for deleted family:"
4790              + Bytes.toString(compaction.getFamilyName().toByteArray()));
4791          return;
4792        }
4793        store.replayCompactionMarker(compaction, pickCompactionFiles, removeFiles);
4794        logRegionFiles();
4795      } catch (FileNotFoundException ex) {
4796        LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4797            + "At least one of the store files in compaction: "
4798            + TextFormat.shortDebugString(compaction)
4799            + " doesn't exist any more. Skip loading the file(s)", ex);
4800      } finally {
4801        closeRegionOperation(Operation.REPLAY_EVENT);
4802      }
4803    }
4804  }
4805
4806  void replayWALFlushMarker(FlushDescriptor flush, long replaySeqId) throws IOException {
4807    checkTargetRegion(flush.getEncodedRegionName().toByteArray(),
4808      "Flush marker from WAL ", flush);
4809
4810    if (ServerRegionReplicaUtil.isDefaultReplica(this.getRegionInfo())) {
4811      return; // if primary nothing to do
4812    }
4813
4814    if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
4815      LOG.debug(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4816          + "Replaying flush marker " + TextFormat.shortDebugString(flush));
4817    }
4818
4819    startRegionOperation(Operation.REPLAY_EVENT); // use region close lock to guard against close
4820    try {
4821      FlushAction action = flush.getAction();
4822      switch (action) {
4823      case START_FLUSH:
4824        replayWALFlushStartMarker(flush);
4825        break;
4826      case COMMIT_FLUSH:
4827        replayWALFlushCommitMarker(flush);
4828        break;
4829      case ABORT_FLUSH:
4830        replayWALFlushAbortMarker(flush);
4831        break;
4832      case CANNOT_FLUSH:
4833        replayWALFlushCannotFlushMarker(flush, replaySeqId);
4834        break;
4835      default:
4836        LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : " +
4837          "Received a flush event with unknown action, ignoring. " +
4838          TextFormat.shortDebugString(flush));
4839        break;
4840      }
4841
4842      logRegionFiles();
4843    } finally {
4844      closeRegionOperation(Operation.REPLAY_EVENT);
4845    }
4846  }
4847
4848  /** Replay the flush marker from primary region by creating a corresponding snapshot of
4849   * the store memstores, only if the memstores do not have a higher seqId from an earlier wal
4850   * edit (because the events may be coming out of order).
4851   */
4852  @VisibleForTesting
4853  PrepareFlushResult replayWALFlushStartMarker(FlushDescriptor flush) throws IOException {
4854    long flushSeqId = flush.getFlushSequenceNumber();
4855
4856    HashSet<HStore> storesToFlush = new HashSet<>();
4857    for (StoreFlushDescriptor storeFlush : flush.getStoreFlushesList()) {
4858      byte[] family = storeFlush.getFamilyName().toByteArray();
4859      HStore store = getStore(family);
4860      if (store == null) {
4861        LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4862          + "Received a flush start marker from primary, but the family is not found. Ignoring"
4863          + " StoreFlushDescriptor:" + TextFormat.shortDebugString(storeFlush));
4864        continue;
4865      }
4866      storesToFlush.add(store);
4867    }
4868
4869    MonitoredTask status = TaskMonitor.get().createStatus("Preparing flush " + this);
4870
4871    // we will use writestate as a coarse-grain lock for all the replay events
4872    // (flush, compaction, region open etc)
4873    synchronized (writestate) {
4874      try {
4875        if (flush.getFlushSequenceNumber() < lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId) {
4876          LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4877              + "Skipping replaying flush event :" + TextFormat.shortDebugString(flush)
4878              + " because its sequence id is smaller than this regions lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId "
4879              + " of " + lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId);
4880          return null;
4881        }
4882        if (numMutationsWithoutWAL.sum() > 0) {
4883          numMutationsWithoutWAL.reset();
4884          dataInMemoryWithoutWAL.reset();
4885        }
4886
4887        if (!writestate.flushing) {
4888          // we do not have an active snapshot and corresponding this.prepareResult. This means
4889          // we can just snapshot our memstores and continue as normal.
4890
4891          // invoke prepareFlushCache. Send null as wal since we do not want the flush events in wal
4892          PrepareFlushResult prepareResult = internalPrepareFlushCache(null, flushSeqId,
4893            storesToFlush, status, false, FlushLifeCycleTracker.DUMMY);
4894          if (prepareResult.result == null) {
4895            // save the PrepareFlushResult so that we can use it later from commit flush
4896            this.writestate.flushing = true;
4897            this.prepareFlushResult = prepareResult;
4898            status.markComplete("Flush prepare successful");
4899            if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
4900              LOG.debug(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4901                  + " Prepared flush with seqId:" + flush.getFlushSequenceNumber());
4902            }
4903          } else {
4904            // special case empty memstore. We will still save the flush result in this case, since
4905            // our memstore ie empty, but the primary is still flushing
4906            if (prepareResult.getResult().getResult() ==
4907                  FlushResult.Result.CANNOT_FLUSH_MEMSTORE_EMPTY) {
4908              this.writestate.flushing = true;
4909              this.prepareFlushResult = prepareResult;
4910              if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
4911                LOG.debug(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4912                  + " Prepared empty flush with seqId:" + flush.getFlushSequenceNumber());
4913              }
4914            }
4915            status.abort("Flush prepare failed with " + prepareResult.result);
4916            // nothing much to do. prepare flush failed because of some reason.
4917          }
4918          return prepareResult;
4919        } else {
4920          // we already have an active snapshot.
4921          if (flush.getFlushSequenceNumber() == this.prepareFlushResult.flushOpSeqId) {
4922            // They define the same flush. Log and continue.
4923            LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4924                + "Received a flush prepare marker with the same seqId: " +
4925                + flush.getFlushSequenceNumber() + " before clearing the previous one with seqId: "
4926                + prepareFlushResult.flushOpSeqId + ". Ignoring");
4927            // ignore
4928          } else if (flush.getFlushSequenceNumber() < this.prepareFlushResult.flushOpSeqId) {
4929            // We received a flush with a smaller seqNum than what we have prepared. We can only
4930            // ignore this prepare flush request.
4931            LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4932                + "Received a flush prepare marker with a smaller seqId: " +
4933                + flush.getFlushSequenceNumber() + " before clearing the previous one with seqId: "
4934                + prepareFlushResult.flushOpSeqId + ". Ignoring");
4935            // ignore
4936          } else {
4937            // We received a flush with a larger seqNum than what we have prepared
4938            LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4939                + "Received a flush prepare marker with a larger seqId: " +
4940                + flush.getFlushSequenceNumber() + " before clearing the previous one with seqId: "
4941                + prepareFlushResult.flushOpSeqId + ". Ignoring");
4942            // We do not have multiple active snapshots in the memstore or a way to merge current
4943            // memstore snapshot with the contents and resnapshot for now. We cannot take
4944            // another snapshot and drop the previous one because that will cause temporary
4945            // data loss in the secondary. So we ignore this for now, deferring the resolution
4946            // to happen when we see the corresponding flush commit marker. If we have a memstore
4947            // snapshot with x, and later received another prepare snapshot with y (where x < y),
4948            // when we see flush commit for y, we will drop snapshot for x, and can also drop all
4949            // the memstore edits if everything in memstore is < y. This is the usual case for
4950            // RS crash + recovery where we might see consequtive prepare flush wal markers.
4951            // Otherwise, this will cause more memory to be used in secondary replica until a
4952            // further prapare + commit flush is seen and replayed.
4953          }
4954        }
4955      } finally {
4956        status.cleanup();
4957        writestate.notifyAll();
4958      }
4959    }
4960    return null;
4961  }
4962
4963  @VisibleForTesting
4964  @edu.umd.cs.findbugs.annotations.SuppressWarnings(value="NN_NAKED_NOTIFY",
4965    justification="Intentional; post memstore flush")
4966  void replayWALFlushCommitMarker(FlushDescriptor flush) throws IOException {
4967    MonitoredTask status = TaskMonitor.get().createStatus("Committing flush " + this);
4968
4969    // check whether we have the memstore snapshot with the corresponding seqId. Replay to
4970    // secondary region replicas are in order, except for when the region moves or then the
4971    // region server crashes. In those cases, we may receive replay requests out of order from
4972    // the original seqIds.
4973    synchronized (writestate) {
4974      try {
4975        if (flush.getFlushSequenceNumber() < lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId) {
4976          LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4977            + "Skipping replaying flush event :" + TextFormat.shortDebugString(flush)
4978            + " because its sequence id is smaller than this regions lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId "
4979            + " of " + lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId);
4980          return;
4981        }
4982
4983        if (writestate.flushing) {
4984          PrepareFlushResult prepareFlushResult = this.prepareFlushResult;
4985          if (flush.getFlushSequenceNumber() == prepareFlushResult.flushOpSeqId) {
4986            if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
4987              LOG.debug(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
4988                  + "Received a flush commit marker with seqId:" + flush.getFlushSequenceNumber()
4989                  + " and a previous prepared snapshot was found");
4990            }
4991            // This is the regular case where we received commit flush after prepare flush
4992            // corresponding to the same seqId.
4993            replayFlushInStores(flush, prepareFlushResult, true);
4994
4995            // Set down the memstore size by amount of flush.
4996            this.decrMemStoreSize(prepareFlushResult.totalFlushableSize);
4997
4998            this.prepareFlushResult = null;
4999            writestate.flushing = false;
5000          } else if (flush.getFlushSequenceNumber() < prepareFlushResult.flushOpSeqId) {
5001            // This should not happen normally. However, lets be safe and guard against these cases
5002            // we received a flush commit with a smaller seqId than what we have prepared
5003            // we will pick the flush file up from this commit (if we have not seen it), but we
5004            // will not drop the memstore
5005            LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5006                + "Received a flush commit marker with smaller seqId: "
5007                + flush.getFlushSequenceNumber() + " than what we have prepared with seqId: "
5008                + prepareFlushResult.flushOpSeqId + ". Picking up new file, but not dropping"
5009                +"  prepared memstore snapshot");
5010            replayFlushInStores(flush, prepareFlushResult, false);
5011
5012            // snapshot is not dropped, so memstore sizes should not be decremented
5013            // we still have the prepared snapshot, flushing should still be true
5014          } else {
5015            // This should not happen normally. However, lets be safe and guard against these cases
5016            // we received a flush commit with a larger seqId than what we have prepared
5017            // we will pick the flush file for this. We will also obtain the updates lock and
5018            // look for contents of the memstore to see whether we have edits after this seqId.
5019            // If not, we will drop all the memstore edits and the snapshot as well.
5020            LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5021                + "Received a flush commit marker with larger seqId: "
5022                + flush.getFlushSequenceNumber() + " than what we have prepared with seqId: " +
5023                prepareFlushResult.flushOpSeqId + ". Picking up new file and dropping prepared"
5024                +" memstore snapshot");
5025
5026            replayFlushInStores(flush, prepareFlushResult, true);
5027
5028            // Set down the memstore size by amount of flush.
5029            this.decrMemStoreSize(prepareFlushResult.totalFlushableSize);
5030
5031            // Inspect the memstore contents to see whether the memstore contains only edits
5032            // with seqId smaller than the flush seqId. If so, we can discard those edits.
5033            dropMemStoreContentsForSeqId(flush.getFlushSequenceNumber(), null);
5034
5035            this.prepareFlushResult = null;
5036            writestate.flushing = false;
5037          }
5038          // If we were waiting for observing a flush or region opening event for not showing
5039          // partial data after a secondary region crash, we can allow reads now. We can only make
5040          // sure that we are not showing partial data (for example skipping some previous edits)
5041          // until we observe a full flush start and flush commit. So if we were not able to find
5042          // a previous flush we will not enable reads now.
5043          this.setReadsEnabled(true);
5044        } else {
5045          LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5046              + "Received a flush commit marker with seqId:" + flush.getFlushSequenceNumber()
5047              + ", but no previous prepared snapshot was found");
5048          // There is no corresponding prepare snapshot from before.
5049          // We will pick up the new flushed file
5050          replayFlushInStores(flush, null, false);
5051
5052          // Inspect the memstore contents to see whether the memstore contains only edits
5053          // with seqId smaller than the flush seqId. If so, we can discard those edits.
5054          dropMemStoreContentsForSeqId(flush.getFlushSequenceNumber(), null);
5055        }
5056
5057        status.markComplete("Flush commit successful");
5058
5059        // Update the last flushed sequence id for region.
5060        this.maxFlushedSeqId = flush.getFlushSequenceNumber();
5061
5062        // advance the mvcc read point so that the new flushed file is visible.
5063        mvcc.advanceTo(flush.getFlushSequenceNumber());
5064
5065      } catch (FileNotFoundException ex) {
5066        LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5067            + "At least one of the store files in flush: " + TextFormat.shortDebugString(flush)
5068            + " doesn't exist any more. Skip loading the file(s)", ex);
5069      }
5070      finally {
5071        status.cleanup();
5072        writestate.notifyAll();
5073      }
5074    }
5075
5076    // C. Finally notify anyone waiting on memstore to clear:
5077    // e.g. checkResources().
5078    synchronized (this) {
5079      notifyAll(); // FindBugs NN_NAKED_NOTIFY
5080    }
5081  }
5082
5083  /**
5084   * Replays the given flush descriptor by opening the flush files in stores and dropping the
5085   * memstore snapshots if requested.
5086   * @param flush
5087   * @param prepareFlushResult
5088   * @param dropMemstoreSnapshot
5089   * @throws IOException
5090   */
5091  private void replayFlushInStores(FlushDescriptor flush, PrepareFlushResult prepareFlushResult,
5092      boolean dropMemstoreSnapshot)
5093      throws IOException {
5094    for (StoreFlushDescriptor storeFlush : flush.getStoreFlushesList()) {
5095      byte[] family = storeFlush.getFamilyName().toByteArray();
5096      HStore store = getStore(family);
5097      if (store == null) {
5098        LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5099            + "Received a flush commit marker from primary, but the family is not found."
5100            + "Ignoring StoreFlushDescriptor:" + storeFlush);
5101        continue;
5102      }
5103      List<String> flushFiles = storeFlush.getFlushOutputList();
5104      StoreFlushContext ctx = null;
5105      long startTime = EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime();
5106      if (prepareFlushResult == null || prepareFlushResult.storeFlushCtxs == null) {
5107        ctx = store.createFlushContext(flush.getFlushSequenceNumber(), FlushLifeCycleTracker.DUMMY);
5108      } else {
5109        ctx = prepareFlushResult.storeFlushCtxs.get(family);
5110        startTime = prepareFlushResult.startTime;
5111      }
5112
5113      if (ctx == null) {
5114        LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5115            + "Unexpected: flush commit marker received from store "
5116            + Bytes.toString(family) + " but no associated flush context. Ignoring");
5117        continue;
5118      }
5119
5120      ctx.replayFlush(flushFiles, dropMemstoreSnapshot); // replay the flush
5121
5122      // Record latest flush time
5123      this.lastStoreFlushTimeMap.put(store, startTime);
5124    }
5125  }
5126
5127  /**
5128   * Drops the memstore contents after replaying a flush descriptor or region open event replay
5129   * if the memstore edits have seqNums smaller than the given seq id
5130   * @throws IOException
5131   */
5132  private MemStoreSize dropMemStoreContentsForSeqId(long seqId, HStore store) throws IOException {
5133    MemStoreSizing totalFreedSize = new MemStoreSizing();
5134    this.updatesLock.writeLock().lock();
5135    try {
5136
5137      long currentSeqId = mvcc.getReadPoint();
5138      if (seqId >= currentSeqId) {
5139        // then we can drop the memstore contents since everything is below this seqId
5140        LOG.info(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5141            + "Dropping memstore contents as well since replayed flush seqId: "
5142            + seqId + " is greater than current seqId:" + currentSeqId);
5143
5144        // Prepare flush (take a snapshot) and then abort (drop the snapshot)
5145        if (store == null) {
5146          for (HStore s : stores.values()) {
5147            totalFreedSize.incMemStoreSize(doDropStoreMemStoreContentsForSeqId(s, currentSeqId));
5148          }
5149        } else {
5150          totalFreedSize.incMemStoreSize(doDropStoreMemStoreContentsForSeqId(store, currentSeqId));
5151        }
5152      } else {
5153        LOG.info(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5154            + "Not dropping memstore contents since replayed flush seqId: "
5155            + seqId + " is smaller than current seqId:" + currentSeqId);
5156      }
5157    } finally {
5158      this.updatesLock.writeLock().unlock();
5159    }
5160    return totalFreedSize;
5161  }
5162
5163  private MemStoreSize doDropStoreMemStoreContentsForSeqId(HStore s, long currentSeqId)
5164      throws IOException {
5165    MemStoreSize flushableSize = s.getFlushableSize();
5166    this.decrMemStoreSize(flushableSize);
5167    StoreFlushContext ctx = s.createFlushContext(currentSeqId, FlushLifeCycleTracker.DUMMY);
5168    ctx.prepare();
5169    ctx.abort();
5170    return flushableSize;
5171  }
5172
5173  private void replayWALFlushAbortMarker(FlushDescriptor flush) {
5174    // nothing to do for now. A flush abort will cause a RS abort which means that the region
5175    // will be opened somewhere else later. We will see the region open event soon, and replaying
5176    // that will drop the snapshot
5177  }
5178
5179  private void replayWALFlushCannotFlushMarker(FlushDescriptor flush, long replaySeqId) {
5180    synchronized (writestate) {
5181      if (this.lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId > replaySeqId) {
5182        LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5183          + "Skipping replaying flush event :" + TextFormat.shortDebugString(flush)
5184          + " because its sequence id " + replaySeqId + " is smaller than this regions "
5185          + "lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId of " + lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId);
5186        return;
5187      }
5188
5189      // If we were waiting for observing a flush or region opening event for not showing partial
5190      // data after a secondary region crash, we can allow reads now. This event means that the
5191      // primary was not able to flush because memstore is empty when we requested flush. By the
5192      // time we observe this, we are guaranteed to have up to date seqId with our previous
5193      // assignment.
5194      this.setReadsEnabled(true);
5195    }
5196  }
5197
5198  @VisibleForTesting
5199  PrepareFlushResult getPrepareFlushResult() {
5200    return prepareFlushResult;
5201  }
5202
5203  @edu.umd.cs.findbugs.annotations.SuppressWarnings(value="NN_NAKED_NOTIFY",
5204      justification="Intentional; cleared the memstore")
5205  void replayWALRegionEventMarker(RegionEventDescriptor regionEvent) throws IOException {
5206    checkTargetRegion(regionEvent.getEncodedRegionName().toByteArray(),
5207      "RegionEvent marker from WAL ", regionEvent);
5208
5209    startRegionOperation(Operation.REPLAY_EVENT);
5210    try {
5211      if (ServerRegionReplicaUtil.isDefaultReplica(this.getRegionInfo())) {
5212        return; // if primary nothing to do
5213      }
5214
5215      if (regionEvent.getEventType() == EventType.REGION_CLOSE) {
5216        // nothing to do on REGION_CLOSE for now.
5217        return;
5218      }
5219      if (regionEvent.getEventType() != EventType.REGION_OPEN) {
5220        LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5221            + "Unknown region event received, ignoring :"
5222            + TextFormat.shortDebugString(regionEvent));
5223        return;
5224      }
5225
5226      if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
5227        LOG.debug(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5228          + "Replaying region open event marker " + TextFormat.shortDebugString(regionEvent));
5229      }
5230
5231      // we will use writestate as a coarse-grain lock for all the replay events
5232      synchronized (writestate) {
5233        // Replication can deliver events out of order when primary region moves or the region
5234        // server crashes, since there is no coordination between replication of different wal files
5235        // belonging to different region servers. We have to safe guard against this case by using
5236        // region open event's seqid. Since this is the first event that the region puts (after
5237        // possibly flushing recovered.edits), after seeing this event, we can ignore every edit
5238        // smaller than this seqId
5239        if (this.lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId <= regionEvent.getLogSequenceNumber()) {
5240          this.lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId = regionEvent.getLogSequenceNumber();
5241        } else {
5242          LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5243            + "Skipping replaying region event :" + TextFormat.shortDebugString(regionEvent)
5244            + " because its sequence id is smaller than this regions lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId "
5245            + " of " + lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId);
5246          return;
5247        }
5248
5249        // region open lists all the files that the region has at the time of the opening. Just pick
5250        // all the files and drop prepared flushes and empty memstores
5251        for (StoreDescriptor storeDescriptor : regionEvent.getStoresList()) {
5252          // stores of primary may be different now
5253          byte[] family = storeDescriptor.getFamilyName().toByteArray();
5254          HStore store = getStore(family);
5255          if (store == null) {
5256            LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5257                + "Received a region open marker from primary, but the family is not found. "
5258                + "Ignoring. StoreDescriptor:" + storeDescriptor);
5259            continue;
5260          }
5261
5262          long storeSeqId = store.getMaxSequenceId().orElse(0L);
5263          List<String> storeFiles = storeDescriptor.getStoreFileList();
5264          try {
5265            store.refreshStoreFiles(storeFiles); // replace the files with the new ones
5266          } catch (FileNotFoundException ex) {
5267            LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5268                    + "At least one of the store files: " + storeFiles
5269                    + " doesn't exist any more. Skip loading the file(s)", ex);
5270            continue;
5271          }
5272          if (store.getMaxSequenceId().orElse(0L) != storeSeqId) {
5273            // Record latest flush time if we picked up new files
5274            lastStoreFlushTimeMap.put(store, EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime());
5275          }
5276
5277          if (writestate.flushing) {
5278            // only drop memstore snapshots if they are smaller than last flush for the store
5279            if (this.prepareFlushResult.flushOpSeqId <= regionEvent.getLogSequenceNumber()) {
5280              StoreFlushContext ctx = this.prepareFlushResult.storeFlushCtxs == null ?
5281                  null : this.prepareFlushResult.storeFlushCtxs.get(family);
5282              if (ctx != null) {
5283                MemStoreSize snapshotSize = store.getFlushableSize();
5284                ctx.abort();
5285                this.decrMemStoreSize(snapshotSize);
5286                this.prepareFlushResult.storeFlushCtxs.remove(family);
5287              }
5288            }
5289          }
5290
5291          // Drop the memstore contents if they are now smaller than the latest seen flushed file
5292          dropMemStoreContentsForSeqId(regionEvent.getLogSequenceNumber(), store);
5293          if (storeSeqId > this.maxFlushedSeqId) {
5294            this.maxFlushedSeqId = storeSeqId;
5295          }
5296        }
5297
5298        // if all stores ended up dropping their snapshots, we can safely drop the
5299        // prepareFlushResult
5300        dropPrepareFlushIfPossible();
5301
5302        // advance the mvcc read point so that the new flushed file is visible.
5303        mvcc.await();
5304
5305        // If we were waiting for observing a flush or region opening event for not showing partial
5306        // data after a secondary region crash, we can allow reads now.
5307        this.setReadsEnabled(true);
5308
5309        // C. Finally notify anyone waiting on memstore to clear:
5310        // e.g. checkResources().
5311        synchronized (this) {
5312          notifyAll(); // FindBugs NN_NAKED_NOTIFY
5313        }
5314      }
5315      logRegionFiles();
5316    } finally {
5317      closeRegionOperation(Operation.REPLAY_EVENT);
5318    }
5319  }
5320
5321  void replayWALBulkLoadEventMarker(WALProtos.BulkLoadDescriptor bulkLoadEvent) throws IOException {
5322    checkTargetRegion(bulkLoadEvent.getEncodedRegionName().toByteArray(),
5323      "BulkLoad marker from WAL ", bulkLoadEvent);
5324
5325    if (ServerRegionReplicaUtil.isDefaultReplica(this.getRegionInfo())) {
5326      return; // if primary nothing to do
5327    }
5328
5329    if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
5330      LOG.debug(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5331              +  "Replaying bulkload event marker " + TextFormat.shortDebugString(bulkLoadEvent));
5332    }
5333    // check if multiple families involved
5334    boolean multipleFamilies = false;
5335    byte[] family = null;
5336    for (StoreDescriptor storeDescriptor : bulkLoadEvent.getStoresList()) {
5337      byte[] fam = storeDescriptor.getFamilyName().toByteArray();
5338      if (family == null) {
5339        family = fam;
5340      } else if (!Bytes.equals(family, fam)) {
5341        multipleFamilies = true;
5342        break;
5343      }
5344    }
5345
5346    startBulkRegionOperation(multipleFamilies);
5347    try {
5348      // we will use writestate as a coarse-grain lock for all the replay events
5349      synchronized (writestate) {
5350        // Replication can deliver events out of order when primary region moves or the region
5351        // server crashes, since there is no coordination between replication of different wal files
5352        // belonging to different region servers. We have to safe guard against this case by using
5353        // region open event's seqid. Since this is the first event that the region puts (after
5354        // possibly flushing recovered.edits), after seeing this event, we can ignore every edit
5355        // smaller than this seqId
5356        if (bulkLoadEvent.getBulkloadSeqNum() >= 0
5357            && this.lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId >= bulkLoadEvent.getBulkloadSeqNum()) {
5358          LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5359              + "Skipping replaying bulkload event :"
5360              + TextFormat.shortDebugString(bulkLoadEvent)
5361              + " because its sequence id is smaller than this region's lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId"
5362              + " =" + lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId);
5363
5364          return;
5365        }
5366
5367        for (StoreDescriptor storeDescriptor : bulkLoadEvent.getStoresList()) {
5368          // stores of primary may be different now
5369          family = storeDescriptor.getFamilyName().toByteArray();
5370          HStore store = getStore(family);
5371          if (store == null) {
5372            LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5373                    + "Received a bulk load marker from primary, but the family is not found. "
5374                    + "Ignoring. StoreDescriptor:" + storeDescriptor);
5375            continue;
5376          }
5377
5378          List<String> storeFiles = storeDescriptor.getStoreFileList();
5379          for (String storeFile : storeFiles) {
5380            StoreFileInfo storeFileInfo = null;
5381            try {
5382              storeFileInfo = fs.getStoreFileInfo(Bytes.toString(family), storeFile);
5383              store.bulkLoadHFile(storeFileInfo);
5384            } catch(FileNotFoundException ex) {
5385              LOG.warn(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5386                      + ((storeFileInfo != null) ? storeFileInfo.toString() :
5387                            (new Path(Bytes.toString(family), storeFile)).toString())
5388                      + " doesn't exist any more. Skip loading the file");
5389            }
5390          }
5391        }
5392      }
5393      if (bulkLoadEvent.getBulkloadSeqNum() > 0) {
5394        mvcc.advanceTo(bulkLoadEvent.getBulkloadSeqNum());
5395      }
5396    } finally {
5397      closeBulkRegionOperation();
5398    }
5399  }
5400
5401  /**
5402   * If all stores ended up dropping their snapshots, we can safely drop the prepareFlushResult
5403   */
5404  private void dropPrepareFlushIfPossible() {
5405    if (writestate.flushing) {
5406      boolean canDrop = true;
5407      if (prepareFlushResult.storeFlushCtxs != null) {
5408        for (Entry<byte[], StoreFlushContext> entry : prepareFlushResult.storeFlushCtxs
5409            .entrySet()) {
5410          HStore store = getStore(entry.getKey());
5411          if (store == null) {
5412            continue;
5413          }
5414          if (store.getSnapshotSize().getDataSize() > 0) {
5415            canDrop = false;
5416            break;
5417          }
5418        }
5419      }
5420
5421      // this means that all the stores in the region has finished flushing, but the WAL marker
5422      // may not have been written or we did not receive it yet.
5423      if (canDrop) {
5424        writestate.flushing = false;
5425        this.prepareFlushResult = null;
5426      }
5427    }
5428  }
5429
5430  @Override
5431  public boolean refreshStoreFiles() throws IOException {
5432    return refreshStoreFiles(false);
5433  }
5434
5435  @edu.umd.cs.findbugs.annotations.SuppressWarnings(value = "NN_NAKED_NOTIFY",
5436      justification = "Notify is about post replay. Intentional")
5437  protected boolean refreshStoreFiles(boolean force) throws IOException {
5438    if (!force && ServerRegionReplicaUtil.isDefaultReplica(this.getRegionInfo())) {
5439      return false; // if primary nothing to do
5440    }
5441
5442    if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
5443      LOG.debug(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : "
5444          + "Refreshing store files to see whether we can free up memstore");
5445    }
5446
5447    long totalFreedDataSize = 0;
5448
5449    long smallestSeqIdInStores = Long.MAX_VALUE;
5450
5451    startRegionOperation(); // obtain region close lock
5452    try {
5453      Map<HStore, Long> map = new HashMap<>();
5454      synchronized (writestate) {
5455        for (HStore store : stores.values()) {
5456          // TODO: some stores might see new data from flush, while others do not which
5457          // MIGHT break atomic edits across column families.
5458          long maxSeqIdBefore = store.getMaxSequenceId().orElse(0L);
5459
5460          // refresh the store files. This is similar to observing a region open wal marker.
5461          store.refreshStoreFiles();
5462
5463          long storeSeqId = store.getMaxSequenceId().orElse(0L);
5464          if (storeSeqId < smallestSeqIdInStores) {
5465            smallestSeqIdInStores = storeSeqId;
5466          }
5467
5468          // see whether we can drop the memstore or the snapshot
5469          if (storeSeqId > maxSeqIdBefore) {
5470            if (writestate.flushing) {
5471              // only drop memstore snapshots if they are smaller than last flush for the store
5472              if (this.prepareFlushResult.flushOpSeqId <= storeSeqId) {
5473                StoreFlushContext ctx = this.prepareFlushResult.storeFlushCtxs == null ?
5474                    null : this.prepareFlushResult.storeFlushCtxs.get(
5475                            store.getColumnFamilyDescriptor().getName());
5476                if (ctx != null) {
5477                  MemStoreSize snapshotSize = store.getFlushableSize();
5478                  ctx.abort();
5479                  this.decrMemStoreSize(snapshotSize);
5480                  this.prepareFlushResult.storeFlushCtxs.remove(
5481                          store.getColumnFamilyDescriptor().getName());
5482                  totalFreedDataSize += snapshotSize.getDataSize();
5483                }
5484              }
5485            }
5486
5487            map.put(store, storeSeqId);
5488          }
5489        }
5490
5491        // if all stores ended up dropping their snapshots, we can safely drop the
5492        // prepareFlushResult
5493        dropPrepareFlushIfPossible();
5494
5495        // advance the mvcc read point so that the new flushed files are visible.
5496        // either greater than flush seq number or they were already picked up via flush.
5497        for (HStore s : stores.values()) {
5498          mvcc.advanceTo(s.getMaxMemStoreTS().orElse(0L));
5499        }
5500
5501
5502        // smallestSeqIdInStores is the seqId that we have a corresponding hfile for. We can safely
5503        // skip all edits that are to be replayed in the future with that has a smaller seqId
5504        // than this. We are updating lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId so that we can skip all edits
5505        // that we have picked the flush files for
5506        if (this.lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId < smallestSeqIdInStores) {
5507          this.lastReplayedOpenRegionSeqId = smallestSeqIdInStores;
5508        }
5509      }
5510      if (!map.isEmpty()) {
5511        for (Map.Entry<HStore, Long> entry : map.entrySet()) {
5512          // Drop the memstore contents if they are now smaller than the latest seen flushed file
5513          totalFreedDataSize += dropMemStoreContentsForSeqId(entry.getValue(), entry.getKey())
5514              .getDataSize();
5515        }
5516      }
5517      // C. Finally notify anyone waiting on memstore to clear:
5518      // e.g. checkResources().
5519      synchronized (this) {
5520        notifyAll(); // FindBugs NN_NAKED_NOTIFY
5521      }
5522      return totalFreedDataSize > 0;
5523    } finally {
5524      closeRegionOperation();
5525    }
5526  }
5527
5528  private void logRegionFiles() {
5529    if (LOG.isTraceEnabled()) {
5530      LOG.trace(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : Store files for region: ");
5531      stores.values().stream().filter(s -> s.getStorefiles() != null)
5532          .flatMap(s -> s.getStorefiles().stream())
5533          .forEachOrdered(sf -> LOG.trace(getRegionInfo().getEncodedName() + " : " + sf));
5534    }
5535  }
5536
5537  /** Checks whether the given regionName is either equal to our region, or that
5538   * the regionName is the primary region to our corresponding range for the secondary replica.
5539   */
5540  private void checkTargetRegion(byte[] encodedRegionName, String exceptionMsg, Object payload)
5541      throws WrongRegionException {
5542    if (Bytes.equals(this.getRegionInfo().getEncodedNameAsBytes(), encodedRegionName)) {
5543      return;
5544    }
5545
5546    if (!RegionReplicaUtil.isDefaultReplica(this.getRegionInfo()) &&
5547        Bytes.equals(encodedRegionName,
5548          this.fs.getRegionInfoForFS().getEncodedNameAsBytes())) {
5549      return;
5550    }
5551
5552    throw new WrongRegionException(exceptionMsg + payload
5553      + " targetted for region " + Bytes.toStringBinary(encodedRegionName)
5554      + " does not match this region: " + this.getRegionInfo());
5555  }

5557  /**
5558   * Used by tests
5559   * @param s Store to add edit too.
5560   * @param cell Cell to add.
5561   */
5562  @VisibleForTesting
5563  protected void restoreEdit(HStore s, Cell cell, MemStoreSizing memstoreAccounting) {
5564    s.add(cell, memstoreAccounting);
5565  }
5566
5567  /**
5568   * @param p File to check.
5569   * @return True if file was zero-length (and if so, we'll delete it in here).
5570   * @throws IOException
5571   */
5572  private static boolean isZeroLengthThenDelete(final FileSystem fs, final Path p)
5573      throws IOException {
5574    FileStatus stat = fs.getFileStatus(p);
5575    if (stat.getLen() > 0) {
5576      return false;
5577    }
5578    LOG.warn("File " + p + " is zero-length, deleting.");
5579    fs.delete(p, false);
5580    return true;
5581  }
5582
5583  protected HStore instantiateHStore(final ColumnFamilyDescriptor family) throws IOException {
5584    if (family.isMobEnabled()) {
5585      if (HFile.getFormatVersion(this.conf) < HFile.MIN_FORMAT_VERSION_WITH_TAGS) {
5586        throw new IOException("A minimum HFile version of "
5587            + HFile.MIN_FORMAT_VERSION_WITH_TAGS
5588            + " is required for MOB feature. Consider setting " + HFile.FORMAT_VERSION_KEY
5589            + " accordingly.");
5590      }
5591      return new HMobStore(this, family, this.conf);
5592    }
5593    return new HStore(this, family, this.conf);
5594  }

5597  public HStore getStore(byte[] column) {
5598    return this.stores.get(column);
5599  }

5601  /**
5602   * Return HStore instance. Does not do any copy: as the number of store is limited, we iterate on
5603   * the list.
5604   */
5605  private HStore getStore(Cell cell) {
5606    return stores.entrySet().stream().filter(e -> CellUtil.matchingFamily(cell, e.getKey()))
5607        .map(e -> e.getValue()).findFirst().orElse(null);
5608  }

5610  @Override
5611  public List<HStore> getStores() {
5612    return new ArrayList<>(stores.values());
5613  }
5614
5615  @Override
5616  public List<String> getStoreFileList(byte[][] columns) throws IllegalArgumentException {
5617    List<String> storeFileNames = new ArrayList<>();
5618    synchronized (closeLock) {
5619      for (byte[] column : columns) {
5620        HStore store = this.stores.get(column);
5621        if (store == null) {
5622          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
5623              "No column family : " + new String(column, StandardCharsets.UTF_8) + " available");
5624        }
5625        Collection<HStoreFile> storeFiles = store.getStorefiles();
5626        if (storeFiles == null) {
5627          continue;
5628        }
5629        for (HStoreFile storeFile : storeFiles) {
5630          storeFileNames.add(storeFile.getPath().toString());
5631        }
5632
5633        logRegionFiles();
5634      }
5635    }
5636    return storeFileNames;
5637  }

5643  /** Make sure this is a valid row for the HRegion */
5644  void checkRow(byte[] row, String op) throws IOException {
5645    if (!rowIsInRange(getRegionInfo(), row)) {
5646      throw new WrongRegionException("Requested row out of range for " +
5647          op + " on HRegion " + this + ", startKey='" +
5648          Bytes.toStringBinary(getRegionInfo().getStartKey()) + "', getEndKey()='" +
5649          Bytes.toStringBinary(getRegionInfo().getEndKey()) + "', row='" +
5650          Bytes.toStringBinary(row) + "'");
5651    }
5652  }
