5654
5655  /**
5656   * Get an exclusive ( write lock ) lock on a given row.
5657   * @param row Which row to lock.
5658   * @return A locked RowLock. The lock is exclusive and already aqquired.
5659   * @throws IOException
5660   */
5661  public RowLock getRowLock(byte[] row) throws IOException {
5662    return getRowLock(row, false);
5663  }
5664
5665  @Override
5666  public RowLock getRowLock(byte[] row, boolean readLock) throws IOException {
5667    checkRow(row, "row lock");
5668    return getRowLockInternal(row, readLock, null);
5669  }
5670
5671  protected RowLock getRowLockInternal(byte[] row, boolean readLock, final RowLock prevRowLock)
5672      throws IOException {
5673    // create an object to use a a key in the row lock map
5674    HashedBytes rowKey = new HashedBytes(row);
5675
5676    RowLockContext rowLockContext = null;
5677    RowLockImpl result = null;
5678
5679    boolean success = false;
5680    try (TraceScope scope = TraceUtil.createTrace("HRegion.getRowLock")) {
5681      TraceUtil.addTimelineAnnotation("Getting a " + (readLock?"readLock":"writeLock"));
5682      // Keep trying until we have a lock or error out.
5683      // TODO: do we need to add a time component here?
5684      while (result == null) {
5685        rowLockContext = computeIfAbsent(lockedRows, rowKey, () -> new RowLockContext(rowKey));
5686        // Now try an get the lock.
5687        // This can fail as
5688        if (readLock) {
5689          // For read lock, if the caller has locked the same row previously, it will not try
5690          // to acquire the same read lock. It simply returns the previous row lock.
5691          RowLockImpl prevRowLockImpl = (RowLockImpl)prevRowLock;
5692          if ((prevRowLockImpl != null) && (prevRowLockImpl.getLock() ==
5693              rowLockContext.readWriteLock.readLock())) {
5694            success = true;
5695            return prevRowLock;
5696          }
5697          result = rowLockContext.newReadLock();
5698        } else {
5699          result = rowLockContext.newWriteLock();
5700        }
5701      }
5702
5703      int timeout = rowLockWaitDuration;
5704      boolean reachDeadlineFirst = false;
5705      Optional<RpcCall> call = RpcServer.getCurrentCall();
5706      if (call.isPresent()) {
5707        long deadline = call.get().getDeadline();
5708        if (deadline < Long.MAX_VALUE) {
5709          int timeToDeadline = (int) (deadline - System.currentTimeMillis());
5710          if (timeToDeadline <= this.rowLockWaitDuration) {
5711            reachDeadlineFirst = true;
5712            timeout = timeToDeadline;
5713          }
5714        }
5715      }
5716
5717      if (timeout <= 0 || !result.getLock().tryLock(timeout, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS)) {
5718        TraceUtil.addTimelineAnnotation("Failed to get row lock");
5719        String message = "Timed out waiting for lock for row: " + rowKey + " in region "
5720            + getRegionInfo().getEncodedName();
5721        if (reachDeadlineFirst) {
5722          throw new TimeoutIOException(message);
5723        } else {
5724          // If timeToDeadline is larger than rowLockWaitDuration, we can not drop the request.
5725          throw new IOException(message);
5726        }
5727      }
5728      rowLockContext.setThreadName(Thread.currentThread().getName());
5729      success = true;
5730      return result;
5731    } catch (InterruptedException ie) {
5732      LOG.warn("Thread interrupted waiting for lock on row: " + rowKey);
5733      InterruptedIOException iie = new InterruptedIOException();
5734      iie.initCause(ie);
5735      TraceUtil.addTimelineAnnotation("Interrupted exception getting row lock");
5736      Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
5737      throw iie;
5738    } catch (Error error) {
5739      // The maximum lock count for read lock is 64K (hardcoded), when this maximum count
5740      // is reached, it will throw out an Error. This Error needs to be caught so it can
5741      // go ahead to process the minibatch with lock acquired.
5742      LOG.warn("Error to get row lock for " + Bytes.toStringBinary(row) + ", cause: " + error);
5743      IOException ioe = new IOException();
5744      ioe.initCause(error);
5745      TraceUtil.addTimelineAnnotation("Error getting row lock");
5746      throw ioe;
5747    } finally {
5748      // Clean up the counts just in case this was the thing keeping the context alive.
5749      if (!success && rowLockContext != null) {
5750        rowLockContext.cleanUp();
5751      }
5752    }
5753  }
5754
5755  private void releaseRowLocks(List<RowLock> rowLocks) {
5756    if (rowLocks != null) {
5757      for (RowLock rowLock : rowLocks) {
5758        rowLock.release();
5759      }
5760      rowLocks.clear();
5761    }
5762  }
5763
5764  @VisibleForTesting
5765  public int getReadLockCount() {
5766    return lock.getReadLockCount();
5767  }
5768
5769  public ConcurrentHashMap<HashedBytes, RowLockContext> getLockedRows() {
5770    return lockedRows;
5771  }
5772
5773  @VisibleForTesting
5774  class RowLockContext {
5775    private final HashedBytes row;
5776    final ReadWriteLock readWriteLock = new ReentrantReadWriteLock(true);
5777    final AtomicBoolean usable = new AtomicBoolean(true);
5778    final AtomicInteger count = new AtomicInteger(0);
5779    final Object lock = new Object();
5780    private String threadName;
5781
5782    RowLockContext(HashedBytes row) {
5783      this.row = row;
5784    }
5785
5786    RowLockImpl newWriteLock() {
5787      Lock l = readWriteLock.writeLock();
5788      return getRowLock(l);
5789    }
5790    RowLockImpl newReadLock() {
5791      Lock l = readWriteLock.readLock();
5792      return getRowLock(l);
5793    }
5794
5795    private RowLockImpl getRowLock(Lock l) {
5796      count.incrementAndGet();
5797      synchronized (lock) {
5798        if (usable.get()) {
5799          return new RowLockImpl(this, l);
5800        } else {
5801          return null;
5802        }
5803      }
5804    }
5805
5806    void cleanUp() {
5807      long c = count.decrementAndGet();
5808      if (c <= 0) {
5809        synchronized (lock) {
5810          if (count.get() <= 0 && usable.get()){ // Don't attempt to remove row if already removed
5811            usable.set(false);
5812            RowLockContext removed = lockedRows.remove(row);
5813            assert removed == this: "we should never remove a different context";
5814          }
5815        }
5816      }
5817    }
5818
5819    public void setThreadName(String threadName) {
5820      this.threadName = threadName;
5821    }
5822
5823    @Override
5824    public String toString() {
5825      return "RowLockContext{" +
5826          "row=" + row +
5827          ", readWriteLock=" + readWriteLock +
5828          ", count=" + count +
5829          ", threadName=" + threadName +
5830          '}';
5831    }
5832  }
5833
5834  /**
5835   * Class used to represent a lock on a row.
5836   */
5837  public static class RowLockImpl implements RowLock {
5838    private final RowLockContext context;
5839    private final Lock lock;
5840
5841    public RowLockImpl(RowLockContext context, Lock lock) {
5842      this.context = context;
5843      this.lock = lock;
5844    }
5845
5846    public Lock getLock() {
5847      return lock;
5848    }
5849
5850    @VisibleForTesting
5851    public RowLockContext getContext() {
5852      return context;
5853    }
5854
5855    @Override
5856    public void release() {
5857      lock.unlock();
5858      context.cleanUp();
5859    }
5860
5861    @Override
5862    public String toString() {
5863      return "RowLockImpl{" +
5864          "context=" + context +
5865          ", lock=" + lock +
5866          '}';
5867    }
5868  }
5869
5870  /**
5871   * Determines whether multiple column families are present
5872   * Precondition: familyPaths is not null
5873   *
5874   * @param familyPaths List of (column family, hfilePath)
5875   */
5876  private static boolean hasMultipleColumnFamilies(Collection<Pair<byte[], String>> familyPaths) {
5877    boolean multipleFamilies = false;
5878    byte[] family = null;
5879    for (Pair<byte[], String> pair : familyPaths) {
5880      byte[] fam = pair.getFirst();
5881      if (family == null) {
5882        family = fam;
5883      } else if (!Bytes.equals(family, fam)) {
5884        multipleFamilies = true;
5885        break;
5886      }
5887    }
5888    return multipleFamilies;
5889  }
5890
5891  /**
5892   * Attempts to atomically load a group of hfiles.  This is critical for loading
5893   * rows with multiple column families atomically.
5894   *
5895   * @param familyPaths List of Pair&lt;byte[] column family, String hfilePath&gt;
5896   * @param bulkLoadListener Internal hooks enabling massaging/preparation of a
5897   * file about to be bulk loaded
5898   * @param assignSeqId
5899   * @return Map from family to List of store file paths if successful, null if failed recoverably
5900   * @throws IOException if failed unrecoverably.
5901   */
5902  public Map<byte[], List<Path>> bulkLoadHFiles(Collection<Pair<byte[], String>> familyPaths, boolean assignSeqId,
5903      BulkLoadListener bulkLoadListener) throws IOException {
5904    return bulkLoadHFiles(familyPaths, assignSeqId, bulkLoadListener, false);
5905  }
5906
5907  /**
5908   * Listener class to enable callers of
5909   * bulkLoadHFile() to perform any necessary
5910   * pre/post processing of a given bulkload call
5911   */
5912  public interface BulkLoadListener {
5913    /**
5914     * Called before an HFile is actually loaded
5915     * @param family family being loaded to
5916     * @param srcPath path of HFile
5917     * @return final path to be used for actual loading
5918     * @throws IOException
5919     */
5920    String prepareBulkLoad(byte[] family, String srcPath, boolean copyFile)
5921        throws IOException;
5922
5923    /**
5924     * Called after a successful HFile load
5925     * @param family family being loaded to
5926     * @param srcPath path of HFile
5927     * @throws IOException
5928     */
5929    void doneBulkLoad(byte[] family, String srcPath) throws IOException;
5930
5931    /**
5932     * Called after a failed HFile load
5933     * @param family family being loaded to
5934     * @param srcPath path of HFile
5935     * @throws IOException
5936     */
5937    void failedBulkLoad(byte[] family, String srcPath) throws IOException;
5938  }
5939
5940  /**
5941   * Attempts to atomically load a group of hfiles.  This is critical for loading
5942   * rows with multiple column families atomically.
5943   *
5944   * @param familyPaths List of Pair&lt;byte[] column family, String hfilePath&gt;
5945   * @param assignSeqId
5946   * @param bulkLoadListener Internal hooks enabling massaging/preparation of a
5947   * file about to be bulk loaded
5948   * @param copyFile always copy hfiles if true
5949   * @return Map from family to List of store file paths if successful, null if failed recoverably
5950   * @throws IOException if failed unrecoverably.
5951   */
5952  public Map<byte[], List<Path>> bulkLoadHFiles(Collection<Pair<byte[], String>> familyPaths,
5953      boolean assignSeqId, BulkLoadListener bulkLoadListener, boolean copyFile) throws IOException {
5954    long seqId = -1;
5955    Map<byte[], List<Path>> storeFiles = new TreeMap<>(Bytes.BYTES_COMPARATOR);
5956    Map<String, Long> storeFilesSizes = new HashMap<>();
5957    Preconditions.checkNotNull(familyPaths);
5958    // we need writeLock for multi-family bulk load
5959    startBulkRegionOperation(hasMultipleColumnFamilies(familyPaths));
5960    boolean isSuccessful = false;
5961    try {
5962      this.writeRequestsCount.increment();
5963
5964      // There possibly was a split that happened between when the split keys
5965      // were gathered and before the HRegion's write lock was taken.  We need
5966      // to validate the HFile region before attempting to bulk load all of them
5967      List<IOException> ioes = new ArrayList<>();
5968      List<Pair<byte[], String>> failures = new ArrayList<>();
5969      for (Pair<byte[], String> p : familyPaths) {
5970        byte[] familyName = p.getFirst();
5971        String path = p.getSecond();
5972
5973        HStore store = getStore(familyName);
5974        if (store == null) {
5975          IOException ioe = new org.apache.hadoop.hbase.DoNotRetryIOException(
5976              "No such column family " + Bytes.toStringBinary(familyName));
5977          ioes.add(ioe);
5978        } else {
5979          try {
5980            store.assertBulkLoadHFileOk(new Path(path));
5981          } catch (WrongRegionException wre) {
5982            // recoverable (file doesn't fit in region)
5983            failures.add(p);
5984          } catch (IOException ioe) {
5985            // unrecoverable (hdfs problem)
5986            ioes.add(ioe);
5987          }
5988        }
5989      }
5990
5991      // validation failed because of some sort of IO problem.
5992      if (ioes.size() != 0) {
5993        IOException e = MultipleIOException.createIOException(ioes);
5994        LOG.error("There were one or more IO errors when checking if the bulk load is ok.", e);
5995        throw e;
5996      }
5997
5998      // validation failed, bail out before doing anything permanent.
5999      if (failures.size() != 0) {
6000        StringBuilder list = new StringBuilder();
6001        for (Pair<byte[], String> p : failures) {
6002          list.append("\n").append(Bytes.toString(p.getFirst())).append(" : ")
6003              .append(p.getSecond());
6004        }
6005        // problem when validating
6006        LOG.warn("There was a recoverable bulk load failure likely due to a" +
6007            " split.  These (family, HFile) pairs were not loaded: " + list);
6008        return null;
6009      }
6010
6011      // We need to assign a sequential ID that's in between two memstores in order to preserve
6012      // the guarantee that all the edits lower than the highest sequential ID from all the
6013      // HFiles are flushed on disk. See HBASE-10958.  The sequence id returned when we flush is
6014      // guaranteed to be one beyond the file made when we flushed (or if nothing to flush, it is
6015      // a sequence id that we can be sure is beyond the last hfile written).
6016      if (assignSeqId) {
6017        FlushResult fs = flushcache(true, false, FlushLifeCycleTracker.DUMMY);
6018        if (fs.isFlushSucceeded()) {
6019          seqId = ((FlushResultImpl)fs).flushSequenceId;
6020        } else if (fs.getResult() == FlushResult.Result.CANNOT_FLUSH_MEMSTORE_EMPTY) {
6021          seqId = ((FlushResultImpl)fs).flushSequenceId;
6022        } else if (fs.getResult() == FlushResult.Result.CANNOT_FLUSH) {
6023          // CANNOT_FLUSH may mean that a flush is already on-going
6024          // we need to wait for that flush to complete
6025          waitForFlushes();
6026        } else {
6027          throw new IOException("Could not bulk load with an assigned sequential ID because the "+
6028            "flush didn't run. Reason for not flushing: " + ((FlushResultImpl)fs).failureReason);
6029        }
6030      }
6031
6032      Map<byte[], List<Pair<Path, Path>>> familyWithFinalPath =
6033          new TreeMap<>(Bytes.BYTES_COMPARATOR);
6034      for (Pair<byte[], String> p : familyPaths) {
6035        byte[] familyName = p.getFirst();
6036        String path = p.getSecond();
6037        HStore store = getStore(familyName);
6038        if (!familyWithFinalPath.containsKey(familyName)) {
6039          familyWithFinalPath.put(familyName, new ArrayList<>());
6040        }
6041        List<Pair<Path, Path>> lst = familyWithFinalPath.get(familyName);
6042        try {
6043          String finalPath = path;
6044          if (bulkLoadListener != null) {
6045            finalPath = bulkLoadListener.prepareBulkLoad(familyName, path, copyFile);
6046          }
6047          Pair<Path, Path> pair = store.preBulkLoadHFile(finalPath, seqId);
6048          lst.add(pair);
6049        } catch (IOException ioe) {
6050          // A failure here can cause an atomicity violation that we currently
6051          // cannot recover from since it is likely a failed HDFS operation.
6052
6053          LOG.error("There was a partial failure due to IO when attempting to" +
6054              " load " + Bytes.toString(p.getFirst()) + " : " + p.getSecond(), ioe);
6055          if (bulkLoadListener != null) {
6056            try {
6057              bulkLoadListener.failedBulkLoad(familyName, path);
6058            } catch (Exception ex) {
6059              LOG.error("Error while calling failedBulkLoad for family " +
6060                  Bytes.toString(familyName) + " with path " + path, ex);
6061            }
6062          }
6063          throw ioe;
6064        }
6065      }
6066
6067      if (this.getCoprocessorHost() != null) {
6068        for (Map.Entry<byte[], List<Pair<Path, Path>>> entry : familyWithFinalPath.entrySet()) {
6069          this.getCoprocessorHost().preCommitStoreFile(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue());
6070        }
6071      }
6072      for (Map.Entry<byte[], List<Pair<Path, Path>>> entry : familyWithFinalPath.entrySet()) {
6073        byte[] familyName = entry.getKey();
6074        for (Pair<Path, Path> p : entry.getValue()) {
6075          String path = p.getFirst().toString();
6076          Path commitedStoreFile = p.getSecond();
6077          HStore store = getStore(familyName);
6078          try {
6079            store.bulkLoadHFile(familyName, path, commitedStoreFile);
6080            // Note the size of the store file
6081            try {
6082              FileSystem fs = commitedStoreFile.getFileSystem(baseConf);
6083              storeFilesSizes.put(commitedStoreFile.getName(), fs.getFileStatus(commitedStoreFile)
6084                  .getLen());
6085            } catch (IOException e) {
6086              LOG.warn("Failed to find the size of hfile " + commitedStoreFile, e);
6087              storeFilesSizes.put(commitedStoreFile.getName(), 0L);
6088            }
6089
6090            if(storeFiles.containsKey(familyName)) {
6091              storeFiles.get(familyName).add(commitedStoreFile);
6092            } else {
6093              List<Path> storeFileNames = new ArrayList<>();
6094              storeFileNames.add(commitedStoreFile);
6095              storeFiles.put(familyName, storeFileNames);
6096            }
6097            if (bulkLoadListener != null) {
6098              bulkLoadListener.doneBulkLoad(familyName, path);
6099            }
6100          } catch (IOException ioe) {
6101            // A failure here can cause an atomicity violation that we currently
6102            // cannot recover from since it is likely a failed HDFS operation.
6103
6104            // TODO Need a better story for reverting partial failures due to HDFS.
6105            LOG.error("There was a partial failure due to IO when attempting to" +
6106                " load " + Bytes.toString(familyName) + " : " + p.getSecond(), ioe);
6107            if (bulkLoadListener != null) {
6108              try {
6109                bulkLoadListener.failedBulkLoad(familyName, path);
6110              } catch (Exception ex) {
6111                LOG.error("Error while calling failedBulkLoad for family " +
6112                    Bytes.toString(familyName) + " with path " + path, ex);
6113              }
6114            }
6115            throw ioe;
6116          }
6117        }
6118      }
6119
6120      isSuccessful = true;
6121    } finally {
6122      if (wal != null && !storeFiles.isEmpty()) {
6123        // Write a bulk load event for hfiles that are loaded
6124        try {
6125          WALProtos.BulkLoadDescriptor loadDescriptor =
6126              ProtobufUtil.toBulkLoadDescriptor(this.getRegionInfo().getTable(),
6127                  UnsafeByteOperations.unsafeWrap(this.getRegionInfo().getEncodedNameAsBytes()),
6128                  storeFiles,
6129                storeFilesSizes, seqId);
6130          WALUtil.writeBulkLoadMarkerAndSync(this.wal, this.getReplicationScope(), getRegionInfo(),
6131              loadDescriptor, mvcc);
6132        } catch (IOException ioe) {
6133          if (this.rsServices != null) {
6134            // Have to abort region server because some hfiles has been loaded but we can't write
6135            // the event into WAL
6136            isSuccessful = false;
6137            this.rsServices.abort("Failed to write bulk load event into WAL.", ioe);
6138          }
6139        }
6140      }
6141
6142      closeBulkRegionOperation();
6143    }
6144    return isSuccessful ? storeFiles : null;
6145  }
6146
6147  @Override
6148  public boolean equals(Object o) {
6149    return o instanceof HRegion && Bytes.equals(getRegionInfo().getRegionName(),
6150                                                ((HRegion) o).getRegionInfo().getRegionName());
6151  }
6152
6153  @Override
6154  public int hashCode() {
6155    return Bytes.hashCode(getRegionInfo().getRegionName());
6156  }
6157
6158  @Override
6159  public String toString() {
6160    return getRegionInfo().getRegionNameAsString();
6161  }
6162
6163  /**
6164   * RegionScannerImpl is used to combine scanners from multiple Stores (aka column families).
6165   */
6166  class RegionScannerImpl
6167      implements RegionScanner, Shipper, org.apache.hadoop.hbase.ipc.RpcCallback {
6168    // Package local for testability
6169    KeyValueHeap storeHeap = null;
6170    /** Heap of key-values that are not essential for the provided filters and are thus read
6171     * on demand, if on-demand column family loading is enabled.*/
6172    KeyValueHeap joinedHeap = null;
6173    /**
6174     * If the joined heap data gathering is interrupted due to scan limits, this will
6175     * contain the row for which we are populating the values.*/
6176    protected Cell joinedContinuationRow = null;
6177    private boolean filterClosed = false;
6178
6179    protected final byte[] stopRow;
6180    protected final boolean includeStopRow;
6181    protected final HRegion region;
6182    protected final CellComparator comparator;
6183
6184    private final long readPt;
6185    private final long maxResultSize;
6186    private final ScannerContext defaultScannerContext;
6187    private final FilterWrapper filter;
6188
6189    @Override
6190    public RegionInfo getRegionInfo() {
6191      return region.getRegionInfo();
6192    }
6193
6194    RegionScannerImpl(Scan scan, List<KeyValueScanner> additionalScanners, HRegion region)
6195        throws IOException {
6196      this(scan, additionalScanners, region, HConstants.NO_NONCE, HConstants.NO_NONCE);
6197    }
6198
6199    RegionScannerImpl(Scan scan, List<KeyValueScanner> additionalScanners, HRegion region,
6200        long nonceGroup, long nonce) throws IOException {
6201      this.region = region;
6202      this.maxResultSize = scan.getMaxResultSize();
6203      if (scan.hasFilter()) {
6204        this.filter = new FilterWrapper(scan.getFilter());
6205      } else {
6206        this.filter = null;
6207      }
6208      this.comparator = region.getCellComparator();
6209      /**
6210       * By default, calls to next/nextRaw must enforce the batch limit. Thus, construct a default
6211       * scanner context that can be used to enforce the batch limit in the event that a
6212       * ScannerContext is not specified during an invocation of next/nextRaw
6213       */
6214      defaultScannerContext = ScannerContext.newBuilder()
6215          .setBatchLimit(scan.getBatch()).build();
6216      this.stopRow = scan.getStopRow();
6217      this.includeStopRow = scan.includeStopRow();
6218
6219      // synchronize on scannerReadPoints so that nobody calculates
6220      // getSmallestReadPoint, before scannerReadPoints is updated.
6221      IsolationLevel isolationLevel = scan.getIsolationLevel();
6222      long mvccReadPoint = PackagePrivateFieldAccessor.getMvccReadPoint(scan);
6223      synchronized (scannerReadPoints) {
6224        if (mvccReadPoint > 0) {
6225          this.readPt = mvccReadPoint;
6226        } else if (nonce == HConstants.NO_NONCE || rsServices == null
6227            || rsServices.getNonceManager() == null) {
6228          this.readPt = getReadPoint(isolationLevel);
6229        } else {
6230          this.readPt = rsServices.getNonceManager().getMvccFromOperationContext(nonceGroup, nonce);
6231        }
6232        scannerReadPoints.put(this, this.readPt);
6233      }
6234      initializeScanners(scan, additionalScanners);
6235    }
6236
6237    protected void initializeScanners(Scan scan, List<KeyValueScanner> additionalScanners)
6238        throws IOException {
6239      // Here we separate all scanners into two lists - scanner that provide data required
6240      // by the filter to operate (scanners list) and all others (joinedScanners list).
6241      List<KeyValueScanner> scanners = new ArrayList<>(scan.getFamilyMap().size());
6242      List<KeyValueScanner> joinedScanners = new ArrayList<>(scan.getFamilyMap().size());
6243      // Store all already instantiated scanners for exception handling
6244      List<KeyValueScanner> instantiatedScanners = new ArrayList<>();
6245      // handle additionalScanners
6246      if (additionalScanners != null && !additionalScanners.isEmpty()) {
6247        scanners.addAll(additionalScanners);
6248        instantiatedScanners.addAll(additionalScanners);
6249      }
6250
6251      try {
6252        for (Map.Entry<byte[], NavigableSet<byte[]>> entry : scan.getFamilyMap().entrySet()) {
6253          HStore store = stores.get(entry.getKey());
6254          KeyValueScanner scanner = store.getScanner(scan, entry.getValue(), this.readPt);
6255          instantiatedScanners.add(scanner);
6256          if (this.filter == null || !scan.doLoadColumnFamiliesOnDemand()
6257              || this.filter.isFamilyEssential(entry.getKey())) {
6258            scanners.add(scanner);
6259          } else {
6260            joinedScanners.add(scanner);
6261          }
6262        }
6263        initializeKVHeap(scanners, joinedScanners, region);
6264      } catch (Throwable t) {
6265        throw handleException(instantiatedScanners, t);
6266      }
6267    }
6268
6269    protected void initializeKVHeap(List<KeyValueScanner> scanners,
6270        List<KeyValueScanner> joinedScanners, HRegion region)
6271        throws IOException {
6272      this.storeHeap = new KeyValueHeap(scanners, comparator);
6273      if (!joinedScanners.isEmpty()) {
6274        this.joinedHeap = new KeyValueHeap(joinedScanners, comparator);
6275      }
6276    }
6277
6278    private IOException handleException(List<KeyValueScanner> instantiatedScanners,
6279        Throwable t) {
6280      // remove scaner read point before throw the exception
6281      scannerReadPoints.remove(this);
6282      if (storeHeap != null) {
6283        storeHeap.close();
6284        storeHeap = null;
6285        if (joinedHeap != null) {
6286          joinedHeap.close();
6287          joinedHeap = null;
6288        }
6289      } else {
6290        // close all already instantiated scanners before throwing the exception
6291        for (KeyValueScanner scanner : instantiatedScanners) {
6292          scanner.close();
6293        }
6294      }
6295      return t instanceof IOException ? (IOException) t : new IOException(t);
6296    }
6297
6298    @Override
6299    public long getMaxResultSize() {
6300      return maxResultSize;
6301    }
6302
6303    @Override
6304    public long getMvccReadPoint() {
6305      return this.readPt;
6306    }
6307
6308    @Override
6309    public int getBatch() {
6310      return this.defaultScannerContext.getBatchLimit();
6311    }
6312
6313    /**
6314     * Reset both the filter and the old filter.
6315     *
6316     * @throws IOException in case a filter raises an I/O exception.
6317     */
6318    protected void resetFilters() throws IOException {
6319      if (filter != null) {
6320        filter.reset();
6321      }
6322    }
6323
6324    @Override
6325    public boolean next(List<Cell> outResults)
6326        throws IOException {
6327      // apply the batching limit by default
6328      return next(outResults, defaultScannerContext);
6329    }
6330
6331    @Override
6332    public synchronized boolean next(List<Cell> outResults, ScannerContext scannerContext)
6333    throws IOException {
6334      if (this.filterClosed) {
6335        throw new UnknownScannerException("Scanner was closed (timed out?) " +
6336            "after we renewed it. Could be caused by a very slow scanner " +
6337            "or a lengthy garbage collection");
6338      }
6339      startRegionOperation(Operation.SCAN);
6340      try {
6341        return nextRaw(outResults, scannerContext);
6342      } finally {
6343        closeRegionOperation(Operation.SCAN);
6344      }
6345    }
6346
6347    @Override
6348    public boolean nextRaw(List<Cell> outResults) throws IOException {
6349      // Use the RegionScanner's context by default
6350      return nextRaw(outResults, defaultScannerContext);
6351    }
6352
6353    @Override
6354    public boolean nextRaw(List<Cell> outResults, ScannerContext scannerContext)
6355        throws IOException {
6356      if (storeHeap == null) {
6357        // scanner is closed
6358        throw new UnknownScannerException("Scanner was closed");
6359      }
6360      boolean moreValues = false;
6361      if (outResults.isEmpty()) {
6362        // Usually outResults is empty. This is true when next is called
6363        // to handle scan or get operation.
6364        moreValues = nextInternal(outResults, scannerContext);
6365      } else {
6366        List<Cell> tmpList = new ArrayList<>();
6367        moreValues = nextInternal(tmpList, scannerContext);
6368        outResults.addAll(tmpList);
6369      }
6370
6371      if (!outResults.isEmpty()) {
6372        readRequestsCount.increment();
6373      }
6374
6375      // If the size limit was reached it means a partial Result is being returned. Returning a
6376      // partial Result means that we should not reset the filters; filters should only be reset in
6377      // between rows
6378      if (!scannerContext.mayHaveMoreCellsInRow()) {
6379        resetFilters();
6380      }
6381
6382      if (isFilterDoneInternal()) {
6383        moreValues = false;
6384      }
6385      return moreValues;
6386    }
6387
6388    /**
6389     * @return true if more cells exist after this batch, false if scanner is done
6390     */
6391    private boolean populateFromJoinedHeap(List<Cell> results, ScannerContext scannerContext)
6392            throws IOException {
6393      assert joinedContinuationRow != null;
6394      boolean moreValues = populateResult(results, this.joinedHeap, scannerContext,
6395          joinedContinuationRow);
6396
6397      if (!scannerContext.checkAnyLimitReached(LimitScope.BETWEEN_CELLS)) {
6398        // We are done with this row, reset the continuation.
6399        joinedContinuationRow = null;
6400      }
6401      // As the data is obtained from two independent heaps, we need to
6402      // ensure that result list is sorted, because Result relies on that.
6403      sort(results, comparator);
6404      return moreValues;
6405    }
6406
6407    /**
6408     * Fetches records with currentRow into results list, until next row, batchLimit (if not -1) is
6409     * reached, or remainingResultSize (if not -1) is reaced
6410     * @param heap KeyValueHeap to fetch data from.It must be positioned on correct row before call.
6411     * @param scannerContext
6412     * @param currentRowCell
6413     * @return state of last call to {@link KeyValueHeap#next()}
6414     */
6415    private boolean populateResult(List<Cell> results, KeyValueHeap heap,
6416        ScannerContext scannerContext, Cell currentRowCell) throws IOException {
6417      Cell nextKv;
6418      boolean moreCellsInRow = false;
6419      boolean tmpKeepProgress = scannerContext.getKeepProgress();
6420      // Scanning between column families and thus the scope is between cells
6421      LimitScope limitScope = LimitScope.BETWEEN_CELLS;
6422      do {
6423        // We want to maintain any progress that is made towards the limits while scanning across
6424        // different column families. To do this, we toggle the keep progress flag on during calls
6425        // to the StoreScanner to ensure that any progress made thus far is not wiped away.
6426        scannerContext.setKeepProgress(true);
6427        heap.next(results, scannerContext);
6428        scannerContext.setKeepProgress(tmpKeepProgress);
6429
6430        nextKv = heap.peek();
6431        moreCellsInRow = moreCellsInRow(nextKv, currentRowCell);
6432        if (!moreCellsInRow) incrementCountOfRowsScannedMetric(scannerContext);
6433        if (moreCellsInRow && scannerContext.checkBatchLimit(limitScope)) {
6434          return scannerContext.setScannerState(NextState.BATCH_LIMIT_REACHED).hasMoreValues();
6435        } else if (scannerContext.checkSizeLimit(limitScope)) {
6436          ScannerContext.NextState state =
6437              moreCellsInRow ? NextState.SIZE_LIMIT_REACHED_MID_ROW : NextState.SIZE_LIMIT_REACHED;
6438          return scannerContext.setScannerState(state).hasMoreValues();
6439        } else if (scannerContext.checkTimeLimit(limitScope)) {
6440          ScannerContext.NextState state =
6441              moreCellsInRow ? NextState.TIME_LIMIT_REACHED_MID_ROW : NextState.TIME_LIMIT_REACHED;
6442          return scannerContext.setScannerState(state).hasMoreValues();
6443        }
6444      } while (moreCellsInRow);
6445      return nextKv != null;
6446    }
6447
6448    /**
6449     * Based on the nextKv in the heap, and the current row, decide whether or not there are more
6450     * cells to be read in the heap. If the row of the nextKv in the heap matches the current row
6451     * then there are more cells to be read in the row.
6452     * @param nextKv
6453     * @param currentRowCell
6454     * @return true When there are more cells in the row to be read
6455     */
6456    private boolean moreCellsInRow(final Cell nextKv, Cell currentRowCell) {
6457      return nextKv != null && CellUtil.matchingRows(nextKv, currentRowCell);
6458    }
6459
6460    /*
6461     * @return True if a filter rules the scanner is over, done.
6462     */
6463    @Override
6464    public synchronized boolean isFilterDone() throws IOException {
6465      return isFilterDoneInternal();
6466    }
6467
6468    private boolean isFilterDoneInternal() throws IOException {
6469      return this.filter != null && this.filter.filterAllRemaining();
6470    }
6471
6472    private boolean nextInternal(List<Cell> results, ScannerContext scannerContext)
6473        throws IOException {
6474      if (!results.isEmpty()) {
6475        throw new IllegalArgumentException("First parameter should be an empty list");
6476      }
6477      if (scannerContext == null) {
6478        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Scanner context cannot be null");
6479      }
6480      Optional<RpcCall> rpcCall = RpcServer.getCurrentCall();
6481
6482      // Save the initial progress from the Scanner context in these local variables. The progress
6483      // may need to be reset a few times if rows are being filtered out so we save the initial
6484      // progress.
6485      int initialBatchProgress = scannerContext.getBatchProgress();
6486      long initialSizeProgress = scannerContext.getDataSizeProgress();
6487      long initialHeapSizeProgress = scannerContext.getHeapSizeProgress();
6488
6489      // Used to check time limit
6490      LimitScope limitScope = LimitScope.BETWEEN_CELLS;
6491
6492      // The loop here is used only when at some point during the next we determine
6493      // that due to effects of filters or otherwise, we have an empty row in the result.
6494      // Then we loop and try again. Otherwise, we must get out on the first iteration via return,
6495      // "true" if there's more data to read, "false" if there isn't (storeHeap is at a stop row,
6496      // and joinedHeap has no more data to read for the last row (if set, joinedContinuationRow).
6497      while (true) {
6498        // Starting to scan a new row. Reset the scanner progress according to whether or not
6499        // progress should be kept.
6500        if (scannerContext.getKeepProgress()) {
6501          // Progress should be kept. Reset to initial values seen at start of method invocation.
6502          scannerContext.setProgress(initialBatchProgress, initialSizeProgress,
6503              initialHeapSizeProgress);
6504        } else {
6505          scannerContext.clearProgress();
6506        }
6507        if (rpcCall.isPresent()) {
6508          // If a user specifies a too-restrictive or too-slow scanner, the
6509          // client might time out and disconnect while the server side
6510          // is still processing the request. We should abort aggressively
6511          // in that case.
6512          long afterTime = rpcCall.get().disconnectSince();
6513          if (afterTime >= 0) {
6514            throw new CallerDisconnectedException(
6515                "Aborting on region " + getRegionInfo().getRegionNameAsString() + ", call " +
6516                    this + " after " + afterTime + " ms, since " +
6517                    "caller disconnected");
6518          }
6519        }
6520
6521        // Let's see what we have in the storeHeap.
6522        Cell current = this.storeHeap.peek();
6523
6524        boolean shouldStop = shouldStop(current);
6525        // When has filter row is true it means that the all the cells for a particular row must be
6526        // read before a filtering decision can be made. This means that filters where hasFilterRow
6527        // run the risk of enLongAddering out of memory errors in the case that they are applied to a
6528        // table that has very large rows.
6529        boolean hasFilterRow = this.filter != null && this.filter.hasFilterRow();
6530
6531        // If filter#hasFilterRow is true, partial results are not allowed since allowing them
6532        // would prevent the filters from being evaluated. Thus, if it is true, change the
6533        // scope of any limits that could potentially create partial results to
6534        // LimitScope.BETWEEN_ROWS so that those limits are not reached mid-row
6535        if (hasFilterRow) {
6536          if (LOG.isTraceEnabled()) {
6537            LOG.trace("filter#hasFilterRow is true which prevents partial results from being "
6538                + " formed. Changing scope of limits that may create partials");
6539          }
6540          scannerContext.setSizeLimitScope(LimitScope.BETWEEN_ROWS);
6541          scannerContext.setTimeLimitScope(LimitScope.BETWEEN_ROWS);
6542          limitScope = LimitScope.BETWEEN_ROWS;
6543        }
6544
6545        if (scannerContext.checkTimeLimit(LimitScope.BETWEEN_CELLS)) {
6546          if (hasFilterRow) {
6547            throw new IncompatibleFilterException(
6548                "Filter whose hasFilterRow() returns true is incompatible with scans that must " +
6549                    " stop mid-row because of a limit. ScannerContext:" + scannerContext);
6550          }
6551          return true;
6552        }
6553
6554        // Check if we were getting data from the joinedHeap and hit the limit.
6555        // If not, then it's main path - getting results from storeHeap.
6556        if (joinedContinuationRow == null) {
6557          // First, check if we are at a stop row. If so, there are no more results.
6558          if (shouldStop) {
6559            if (hasFilterRow) {
6560              filter.filterRowCells(results);
6561            }
6562            return scannerContext.setScannerState(NextState.NO_MORE_VALUES).hasMoreValues();
6563          }
6564
6565          // Check if rowkey filter wants to exclude this row. If so, loop to next.
6566          // Technically, if we hit limits before on this row, we don't need this call.
6567          if (filterRowKey(current)) {
6568            incrementCountOfRowsFilteredMetric(scannerContext);
6569            // early check, see HBASE-16296
6570            if (isFilterDoneInternal()) {
6571              return scannerContext.setScannerState(NextState.NO_MORE_VALUES).hasMoreValues();
6572            }
6573            // Typically the count of rows scanned is incremented inside #populateResult. However,
6574            // here we are filtering a row based purely on its row key, preventing us from calling
6575            // #populateResult. Thus, perform the necessary increment here to rows scanned metric
6576            incrementCountOfRowsScannedMetric(scannerContext);
6577            boolean moreRows = nextRow(scannerContext, current);
6578            if (!moreRows) {
6579              return scannerContext.setScannerState(NextState.NO_MORE_VALUES).hasMoreValues();
6580            }
6581            results.clear();
6582
6583            // Read nothing as the rowkey was filtered, but still need to check time limit
6584            if (scannerContext.checkTimeLimit(limitScope)) {
6585              return true;
6586            }
6587            continue;
6588          }
6589
6590          // Ok, we are good, let's try to get some results from the main heap.
6591          populateResult(results, this.storeHeap, scannerContext, current);
6592          if (scannerContext.checkAnyLimitReached(LimitScope.BETWEEN_CELLS)) {
6593            if (hasFilterRow) {
6594              throw new IncompatibleFilterException(
6595                  "Filter whose hasFilterRow() returns true is incompatible with scans that must "
6596                      + " stop mid-row because of a limit. ScannerContext:" + scannerContext);
6597            }
6598            return true;
6599          }
6600
6601          Cell nextKv = this.storeHeap.peek();
6602          shouldStop = shouldStop(nextKv);
6603          // save that the row was empty before filters applied to it.
6604          final boolean isEmptyRow = results.isEmpty();
6605
6606          // We have the part of the row necessary for filtering (all of it, usually).
6607          // First filter with the filterRow(List).
6608          FilterWrapper.FilterRowRetCode ret = FilterWrapper.FilterRowRetCode.NOT_CALLED;
6609          if (hasFilterRow) {
6610            ret = filter.filterRowCellsWithRet(results);
6611
6612            // We don't know how the results have changed after being filtered. Must set progress
6613            // according to contents of results now.
6614            if (scannerContext.getKeepProgress()) {
6615              scannerContext.setProgress(initialBatchProgress, initialSizeProgress,
6616                  initialHeapSizeProgress);
6617            } else {
6618              scannerContext.clearProgress();
6619            }
6620            scannerContext.incrementBatchProgress(results.size());
6621            for (Cell cell : results) {
6622              scannerContext.incrementSizeProgress(PrivateCellUtil.estimatedSerializedSizeOf(cell),
6623                PrivateCellUtil.estimatedSizeOfCell(cell));
6624            }
6625          }
6626
6627          if (isEmptyRow || ret == FilterWrapper.FilterRowRetCode.EXCLUDE || filterRow()) {
6628            incrementCountOfRowsFilteredMetric(scannerContext);
6629            results.clear();
6630            boolean moreRows = nextRow(scannerContext, current);
6631            if (!moreRows) {
6632              return scannerContext.setScannerState(NextState.NO_MORE_VALUES).hasMoreValues();
6633            }
6634
6635            // This row was totally filtered out, if this is NOT the last row,
6636            // we should continue on. Otherwise, nothing else to do.
6637            if (!shouldStop) {
6638              // Read nothing as the cells was filtered, but still need to check time limit
6639              if (scannerContext.checkTimeLimit(limitScope)) {
6640                return true;
6641              }
6642              continue;
6643            }
6644            return scannerContext.setScannerState(NextState.NO_MORE_VALUES).hasMoreValues();
6645          }
6646
6647          // Ok, we are done with storeHeap for this row.
6648          // Now we may need to fetch additional, non-essential data into row.
6649          // These values are not needed for filter to work, so we postpone their
6650          // fetch to (possibly) reduce amount of data loads from disk.
6651          if (this.joinedHeap != null) {
6652            boolean mayHaveData = joinedHeapMayHaveData(current);
6653            if (mayHaveData) {
6654              joinedContinuationRow = current;
6655              populateFromJoinedHeap(results, scannerContext);
6656
6657              if (scannerContext.checkAnyLimitReached(LimitScope.BETWEEN_CELLS)) {
6658                return true;
6659              }
6660            }
6661          }
6662        } else {
6663          // Populating from the joined heap was stopped by limits, populate some more.
6664          populateFromJoinedHeap(results, scannerContext);
6665          if (scannerContext.checkAnyLimitReached(LimitScope.BETWEEN_CELLS)) {
6666            return true;
6667          }
6668        }
6669        // We may have just called populateFromJoinedMap and hit the limits. If that is
6670        // the case, we need to call it again on the next next() invocation.
6671        if (joinedContinuationRow != null) {
6672          return scannerContext.setScannerState(NextState.MORE_VALUES).hasMoreValues();
6673        }
6674
6675        // Finally, we are done with both joinedHeap and storeHeap.
6676        // Double check to prevent empty rows from appearing in result. It could be
6677        // the case when SingleColumnValueExcludeFilter is used.
6678        if (results.isEmpty()) {
6679          incrementCountOfRowsFilteredMetric(scannerContext);
6680          boolean moreRows = nextRow(scannerContext, current);
6681          if (!moreRows) {
6682            return scannerContext.setScannerState(NextState.NO_MORE_VALUES).hasMoreValues();
6683          }
6684          if (!shouldStop) continue;
6685        }
6686
6687        if (shouldStop) {
6688          return scannerContext.setScannerState(NextState.NO_MORE_VALUES).hasMoreValues();
6689        } else {
6690          return scannerContext.setScannerState(NextState.MORE_VALUES).hasMoreValues();
6691        }
6692      }
6693    }
6694
6695    protected void incrementCountOfRowsFilteredMetric(ScannerContext scannerContext) {
6696      filteredReadRequestsCount.increment();
6697
6698      if (scannerContext == null || !scannerContext.isTrackingMetrics()) return;
6699
6700      scannerContext.getMetrics().countOfRowsFiltered.incrementAndGet();
6701    }
6702
6703    protected void incrementCountOfRowsScannedMetric(ScannerContext scannerContext) {
6704      if (scannerContext == null || !scannerContext.isTrackingMetrics()) return;
6705
6706      scannerContext.getMetrics().countOfRowsScanned.incrementAndGet();
6707    }
6708
6709    /**
6710     * @param currentRowCell
6711     * @return true when the joined heap may have data for the current row
6712     * @throws IOException
6713     */
6714    private boolean joinedHeapMayHaveData(Cell currentRowCell)
6715        throws IOException {
6716      Cell nextJoinedKv = joinedHeap.peek();
6717      boolean matchCurrentRow =
6718          nextJoinedKv != null && CellUtil.matchingRows(nextJoinedKv, currentRowCell);
6719      boolean matchAfterSeek = false;
6720
6721      // If the next value in the joined heap does not match the current row, try to seek to the
6722      // correct row
6723      if (!matchCurrentRow) {
6724        Cell firstOnCurrentRow = PrivateCellUtil.createFirstOnRow(currentRowCell);
6725        boolean seekSuccessful = this.joinedHeap.requestSeek(firstOnCurrentRow, true, true);
6726        matchAfterSeek =
6727            seekSuccessful && joinedHeap.peek() != null
6728                && CellUtil.matchingRows(joinedHeap.peek(), currentRowCell);
6729      }
6730
6731      return matchCurrentRow || matchAfterSeek;
6732    }
6733
6734    /**
6735     * This function is to maintain backward compatibility for 0.94 filters. HBASE-6429 combines
6736     * both filterRow & filterRow({@code List<KeyValue> kvs}) functions. While 0.94 code or older,
6737     * it may not implement hasFilterRow as HBase-6429 expects because 0.94 hasFilterRow() only
6738     * returns true when filterRow({@code List<KeyValue> kvs}) is overridden not the filterRow().
6739     * Therefore, the filterRow() will be skipped.
6740     */
6741    private boolean filterRow() throws IOException {
6742      // when hasFilterRow returns true, filter.filterRow() will be called automatically inside
6743      // filterRowCells(List<Cell> kvs) so we skip that scenario here.
6744      return filter != null && (!filter.hasFilterRow())
6745          && filter.filterRow();
6746    }
6747
6748    private boolean filterRowKey(Cell current) throws IOException {
6749      return filter != null && filter.filterRowKey(current);
6750    }
6751
6752    protected boolean nextRow(ScannerContext scannerContext, Cell curRowCell) throws IOException {
6753      assert this.joinedContinuationRow == null: "Trying to go to next row during joinedHeap read.";
6754      Cell next;
6755      while ((next = this.storeHeap.peek()) != null &&
6756             CellUtil.matchingRows(next, curRowCell)) {
6757        this.storeHeap.next(MOCKED_LIST);
6758      }
6759      resetFilters();
6760
6761      // Calling the hook in CP which allows it to do a fast forward
6762      return this.region.getCoprocessorHost() == null
6763          || this.region.getCoprocessorHost()
6764              .postScannerFilterRow(this, curRowCell);
6765    }
6766
6767    protected boolean shouldStop(Cell currentRowCell) {
6768      if (currentRowCell == null) {
6769        return true;
6770      }
6771      if (stopRow == null || Bytes.equals(stopRow, HConstants.EMPTY_END_ROW)) {
6772        return false;
6773      }
6774      int c = comparator.compareRows(currentRowCell, stopRow, 0, stopRow.length);
6775      return c > 0 || (c == 0 && !includeStopRow);
6776    }
6777
6778    @Override
6779    public synchronized void close() {
6780      if (storeHeap != null) {
6781        storeHeap.close();
6782        storeHeap = null;
6783      }
6784      if (joinedHeap != null) {
6785        joinedHeap.close();
6786        joinedHeap = null;
6787      }
6788      // no need to synchronize here.
6789      scannerReadPoints.remove(this);
6790      this.filterClosed = true;
6791    }
6792
6793    KeyValueHeap getStoreHeapForTesting() {
6794      return storeHeap;
6795    }
6796
6797    @Override
6798    public synchronized boolean reseek(byte[] row) throws IOException {
6799      if (row == null) {
6800        throw new IllegalArgumentException("Row cannot be null.");
6801      }
6802      boolean result = false;
6803      startRegionOperation();
6804      Cell kv = PrivateCellUtil.createFirstOnRow(row, 0, (short) row.length);
6805      try {
6806        // use request seek to make use of the lazy seek option. See HBASE-5520
6807        result = this.storeHeap.requestSeek(kv, true, true);
6808        if (this.joinedHeap != null) {
6809          result = this.joinedHeap.requestSeek(kv, true, true) || result;
6810        }
6811      } finally {
6812        closeRegionOperation();
6813      }
6814      return result;
6815    }
6816
6817    @Override
6818    public void shipped() throws IOException {
6819      if (storeHeap != null) {
6820        storeHeap.shipped();
6821      }
6822      if (joinedHeap != null) {
6823        joinedHeap.shipped();
6824      }
6825    }
6826
6827    @Override
6828    public void run() throws IOException {
6829      // This is the RPC callback method executed. We do the close in of the scanner in this
6830      // callback
6831      this.close();
6832    }
6833  }

6835  // Utility methods
6836  /**
6837   * A utility method to create new instances of HRegion based on the
6838   * {@link HConstants#REGION_IMPL} configuration property.
6839   * @param tableDir qualified path of directory where region should be located,
6840   * usually the table directory.
6841   * @param wal The WAL is the outbound log for any updates to the HRegion
6842   * The wal file is a logfile from the previous execution that's
6843   * custom-computed for this HRegion. The HRegionServer computes and sorts the
6844   * appropriate wal info for this HRegion. If there is a previous file
6845   * (implying that the HRegion has been written-to before), then read it from
6846   * the supplied path.
6847   * @param fs is the filesystem.
6848   * @param conf is global configuration settings.
6849   * @param regionInfo - RegionInfo that describes the region
6850   * is new), then read them from the supplied path.
6851   * @param htd the table descriptor
6852   * @return the new instance
6853   */
6854  static HRegion newHRegion(Path tableDir, WAL wal, FileSystem fs,
6855      Configuration conf, RegionInfo regionInfo, final TableDescriptor htd,
6856      RegionServerServices rsServices) {
6857    try {
6858      @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
6859      Class<? extends HRegion> regionClass =
6860          (Class<? extends HRegion>) conf.getClass(HConstants.REGION_IMPL, HRegion.class);
6861
6862      Constructor<? extends HRegion> c =
6863          regionClass.getConstructor(Path.class, WAL.class, FileSystem.class,
6864              Configuration.class, RegionInfo.class, TableDescriptor.class,
6865              RegionServerServices.class);
6866
6867      return c.newInstance(tableDir, wal, fs, conf, regionInfo, htd, rsServices);
6868    } catch (Throwable e) {
6869      // todo: what should I throw here?
6870      throw new IllegalStateException("Could not instantiate a region instance.", e);
6871    }
6872  }
6873
6874  /**
6875   * Convenience method creating new HRegions. Used by createTable.
6876   *
6877   * @param info Info for region to create.
6878   * @param rootDir Root directory for HBase instance
6879   * @param wal shared WAL
6880   * @param initialize - true to initialize the region
6881   * @return new HRegion
6882   * @throws IOException
6883   */
6884  public static HRegion createHRegion(final RegionInfo info, final Path rootDir,
6885        final Configuration conf, final TableDescriptor hTableDescriptor,
6886        final WAL wal, final boolean initialize)
6887  throws IOException {
6888    LOG.info("creating HRegion " + info.getTable().getNameAsString()
6889        + " HTD == " + hTableDescriptor + " RootDir = " + rootDir +
6890        " Table name == " + info.getTable().getNameAsString());
6891    FileSystem fs = FileSystem.get(conf);
6892    Path tableDir = FSUtils.getTableDir(rootDir, info.getTable());
6893    HRegionFileSystem.createRegionOnFileSystem(conf, fs, tableDir, info);
6894    HRegion region = HRegion.newHRegion(tableDir, wal, fs, conf, info, hTableDescriptor, null);
6895    if (initialize) region.initialize(null);
6896    return region;
6897  }
6898
6899  public static HRegion createHRegion(final RegionInfo info, final Path rootDir,
6900                                      final Configuration conf,
6901                                      final TableDescriptor hTableDescriptor,
6902                                      final WAL wal)
6903    throws IOException {
6904    return createHRegion(info, rootDir, conf, hTableDescriptor, wal, true);
6905  }

6931   * WAL#setSequenceNumber(long) passing the result of the call to
6932   * HRegion#getMinSequenceId() to ensure the wal id is properly kept
6933   * up.  HRegionStore does this every time it opens a new region.

6954   * @param wal WAL for region to use. This method will call
6955   * WAL#setSequenceNumber(long) passing the result of the call to
6956   * HRegion#getMinSequenceId() to ensure the wal id is properly kept
6957   * up.  HRegionStore does this every time it opens a new region.
6958   * @param conf The Configuration object to use.

6960   * @throws IOException

6962  public static HRegion openHRegion(Path rootDir, final RegionInfo info,

6964  throws IOException {
6965    return openHRegion(rootDir, info, htd, wal, conf, null, null);

6967
6968  /**
6969   * Open a Region.
6970   * @param rootDir Root directory for HBase instance
6971   * @param info Info for region to be opened.
6972   * @param htd the table descriptor
6973   * @param wal WAL for region to use. This method will call
6974   * WAL#setSequenceNumber(long) passing the result of the call to
6975   * HRegion#getMinSequenceId() to ensure the wal id is properly kept
6976   * up.  HRegionStore does this every time it opens a new region.
6977   * @param conf The Configuration object to use.
6978   * @param rsServices An interface we can request flushes against.
6979   * @param reporter An interface we can report progress against.
6980   * @return new HRegion
6981   * @throws IOException
6982   */
6983  public static HRegion openHRegion(final Path rootDir, final RegionInfo info,
6984      final TableDescriptor htd, final WAL wal, final Configuration conf,
6985      final RegionServerServices rsServices,
6986      final CancelableProgressable reporter)
6987  throws IOException {
6988    FileSystem fs = null;
6989    if (rsServices != null) {
6990      fs = rsServices.getFileSystem();
6991    }
6992    if (fs == null) {
6993      fs = FileSystem.get(conf);
6994    }
6995    return openHRegion(conf, fs, rootDir, info, htd, wal, rsServices, reporter);
6996  }

6998  /**
6999   * Open a Region.
7000   * @param conf The Configuration object to use.
7001   * @param fs Filesystem to use
7002   * @param rootDir Root directory for HBase instance
7003   * @param info Info for region to be opened.
7004   * @param htd the table descriptor
7005   * @param wal WAL for region to use. This method will call
7006   * WAL#setSequenceNumber(long) passing the result of the call to
7007   * HRegion#getMinSequenceId() to ensure the wal id is properly kept
7008   * up.  HRegionStore does this every time it opens a new region.
7009   * @return new HRegion
7010   * @throws IOException
7011   */
7012  public static HRegion openHRegion(final Configuration conf, final FileSystem fs,
7013      final Path rootDir, final RegionInfo info, final TableDescriptor htd, final WAL wal)
7014      throws IOException {
7015    return openHRegion(conf, fs, rootDir, info, htd, wal, null, null);
7016  }

7018  /**
7019   * Open a Region.
7020   * @param conf The Configuration object to use.
7021   * @param fs Filesystem to use
7022   * @param rootDir Root directory for HBase instance
7023   * @param info Info for region to be opened.
7024   * @param htd the table descriptor
7025   * @param wal WAL for region to use. This method will call
7026   * WAL#setSequenceNumber(long) passing the result of the call to
7027   * HRegion#getMinSequenceId() to ensure the wal id is properly kept
7028   * up.  HRegionStore does this every time it opens a new region.
7029   * @param rsServices An interface we can request flushes against.
7030   * @param reporter An interface we can report progress against.
7031   * @return new HRegion
7032   * @throws IOException
7033   */
7034  public static HRegion openHRegion(final Configuration conf, final FileSystem fs,
7035      final Path rootDir, final RegionInfo info, final TableDescriptor htd, final WAL wal,
7036      final RegionServerServices rsServices, final CancelableProgressable reporter)
7037      throws IOException {
7038    Path tableDir = FSUtils.getTableDir(rootDir, info.getTable());
7039    return openHRegion(conf, fs, rootDir, tableDir, info, htd, wal, rsServices, reporter);
7040  }

7042  /**
7043   * Open a Region.
7044   * @param conf The Configuration object to use.
7045   * @param fs Filesystem to use
7046   * @param rootDir Root directory for HBase instance
7047   * @param info Info for region to be opened.
7048   * @param htd the table descriptor
7049   * @param wal WAL for region to use. This method will call
7050   * WAL#setSequenceNumber(long) passing the result of the call to
7051   * HRegion#getMinSequenceId() to ensure the wal id is properly kept
7052   * up.  HRegionStore does this every time it opens a new region.
7053   * @param rsServices An interface we can request flushes against.
7054   * @param reporter An interface we can report progress against.
7055   * @return new HRegion
7056   * @throws IOException
7057   */
7058  public static HRegion openHRegion(final Configuration conf, final FileSystem fs,
7059      final Path rootDir, final Path tableDir, final RegionInfo info, final TableDescriptor htd,
7060      final WAL wal, final RegionServerServices rsServices,
7061      final CancelableProgressable reporter)
7062      throws IOException {
7063    if (info == null) throw new NullPointerException("Passed region info is null");
7064    if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
7065      LOG.debug("Opening region: " + info);
7066    }
7067    HRegion r = HRegion.newHRegion(tableDir, wal, fs, conf, info, htd, rsServices);
7068    return r.openHRegion(reporter);
7069  }

7073    return this.replicationScope;

7076  /**
7077   * Useful when reopening a closed region (normally for unit tests)
7078   * @param other original object
7079   * @param reporter An interface we can report progress against.
7080   * @return new HRegion
7081   * @throws IOException
7082   */
7083  public static HRegion openHRegion(final HRegion other, final CancelableProgressable reporter)
7084      throws IOException {
7085    HRegionFileSystem regionFs = other.getRegionFileSystem();
7086    HRegion r = newHRegion(regionFs.getTableDir(), other.getWAL(), regionFs.getFileSystem(),
7087        other.baseConf, other.getRegionInfo(), other.getTableDescriptor(), null);
7088    return r.openHRegion(reporter);
7089  }
7090
7091  public static Region openHRegion(final Region other, final CancelableProgressable reporter)
7092        throws IOException {
7093    return openHRegion((HRegion)other, reporter);
7094  }
7095
7096  /**
7097   * Open HRegion.
7098   * Calls initialize and sets sequenceId.
7099   * @return Returns <code>this</code>
7100   */
7101  protected HRegion openHRegion(final CancelableProgressable reporter)
7102  throws IOException {
7103    // Refuse to open the region if we are missing local compression support
7104    checkCompressionCodecs();
7105    // Refuse to open the region if encryption configuration is incorrect or
7106    // codec support is missing
7107    checkEncryption();
7108    // Refuse to open the region if a required class cannot be loaded
7109    checkClassLoading();
7110    this.openSeqNum = initialize(reporter);
7111    this.mvcc.advanceTo(openSeqNum);
7112    if (wal != null && getRegionServerServices() != null && !writestate.readOnly) {
7113      // Only write the region open event marker to WAL if we are not read-only.
7114      writeRegionOpenMarker(wal, openSeqNum);
7115    }
7116    return this;
7117  }
7118
7119  /**
7120   * Open a Region on a read-only file-system (like hdfs snapshots)
7121   * @param conf The Configuration object to use.
7122   * @param fs Filesystem to use
7123   * @param info Info for region to be opened.
7124   * @param htd the table descriptor
7125   * @return new HRegion
7126   * @throws IOException e
7127   */
7128  public static HRegion openReadOnlyFileSystemHRegion(final Configuration conf, final FileSystem fs,
7129      final Path tableDir, RegionInfo info, final TableDescriptor htd) throws IOException {
7130    if (info == null) {
7131      throw new NullPointerException("Passed region info is null");
7132    }
7133    if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
7134      LOG.debug("Opening region (readOnly filesystem): " + info);
7135    }
7136    if (info.getReplicaId() <= 0) {
7137      info = RegionInfoBuilder.newBuilder(info).setReplicaId(1).build();
7138    }
7139    HRegion r = HRegion.newHRegion(tableDir, null, fs, conf, info, htd, null);
7140    r.writestate.setReadOnly(true);
7141    return r.openHRegion(null);
7142  }
7143
7144  public static void warmupHRegion(final RegionInfo info,
7145      final TableDescriptor htd, final WAL wal, final Configuration conf,
7146      final RegionServerServices rsServices,
7147      final CancelableProgressable reporter)
7148      throws IOException {
7149
7150    if (info == null) throw new NullPointerException("Passed region info is null");
7151
7152    if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
7153      LOG.debug("HRegion.Warming up region: " + info);
7154    }
7155
7156    Path rootDir = FSUtils.getRootDir(conf);
7157    Path tableDir = FSUtils.getTableDir(rootDir, info.getTable());
7158
7159    FileSystem fs = null;
7160    if (rsServices != null) {
7161      fs = rsServices.getFileSystem();
7162    }
7163    if (fs == null) {
7164      fs = FileSystem.get(conf);
7165    }
7166
7167    HRegion r = HRegion.newHRegion(tableDir, wal, fs, conf, info, htd, null);
7168    r.initializeWarmup(reporter);
7169  }

7175      CompressionTest.testCompression(fam.getCompactionCompressionType());
7176    }
7177  }

7180    for (ColumnFamilyDescriptor fam: this.htableDescriptor.getColumnFamilies()) {
7181      EncryptionTest.testEncryption(conf, fam.getEncryptionType(), fam.getEncryptionKey());
7182    }
7183  }

7187    RegionCoprocessorHost.testTableCoprocessorAttrs(conf, this.htableDescriptor);
7188  }

7218  /**
7219   * Determines if the specified row is within the row range specified by the
7220   * specified RegionInfo
7221   *
7222   * @param info RegionInfo that specifies the row range
7223   * @param row row to be checked
7224   * @return true if the row is within the range specified by the RegionInfo
7225   */
7226  public static boolean rowIsInRange(RegionInfo info, final byte [] row) {
7227    return ((info.getStartKey().length == 0) ||
7228        (Bytes.compareTo(info.getStartKey(), row) <= 0)) &&
7229        ((info.getEndKey().length == 0) ||
7230            (Bytes.compareTo(info.getEndKey(), row) > 0));
7231  }
7232
7233  public static boolean rowIsInRange(RegionInfo info, final byte [] row, final int offset,
7234      final short length) {
7235    return ((info.getStartKey().length == 0) ||
7236        (Bytes.compareTo(info.getStartKey(), 0, info.getStartKey().length,
7237          row, offset, length) <= 0)) &&
7238        ((info.getEndKey().length == 0) ||
7239          (Bytes.compareTo(info.getEndKey(), 0, info.getEndKey().length, row, offset, length) > 0));
7240  }

7242  @Override
7243  public Result get(final Get get) throws IOException {
7244    prepareGet(get);
7245    List<Cell> results = get(get, true);
7246    boolean stale = this.getRegionInfo().getReplicaId() != 0;
7247    return Result.create(results, get.isCheckExistenceOnly() ? !results.isEmpty() : null, stale);
7248  }
7249
7250  void prepareGet(final Get get) throws IOException {
7251    checkRow(get.getRow(), "Get");
7252    // Verify families are all valid
7253    if (get.hasFamilies()) {
7254      for (byte[] family : get.familySet()) {
7255        checkFamily(family);
7256      }
7257    } else { // Adding all families to scanner
7258      for (byte[] family : this.htableDescriptor.getColumnFamilyNames()) {
7259        get.addFamily(family);
7260      }
7261    }
7262  }
7263
7264  @Override
7265  public List<Cell> get(Get get, boolean withCoprocessor) throws IOException {
7266    return get(get, withCoprocessor, HConstants.NO_NONCE, HConstants.NO_NONCE);
7267  }
7268
7269  public List<Cell> get(Get get, boolean withCoprocessor, long nonceGroup, long nonce)
7270      throws IOException {
7271    List<Cell> results = new ArrayList<>();
7272    long before =  EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime();
7273
7274    // pre-get CP hook
7275    if (withCoprocessor && (coprocessorHost != null)) {
7276      if (coprocessorHost.preGet(get, results)) {
7277        metricsUpdateForGet(results, before);
7278        return results;
7279      }
7280    }
7281    Scan scan = new Scan(get);
7282    if (scan.getLoadColumnFamiliesOnDemandValue() == null) {
7283      scan.setLoadColumnFamiliesOnDemand(isLoadingCfsOnDemandDefault());
7284    }
7285    RegionScanner scanner = null;
7286    try {
7287      scanner = getScanner(scan, null, nonceGroup, nonce);
7288      scanner.next(results);
7289    } finally {
7290      if (scanner != null)
7291        scanner.close();
7292    }
7293
7294    // post-get CP hook
7295    if (withCoprocessor && (coprocessorHost != null)) {
7296      coprocessorHost.postGet(get, results);
7297    }
7298
7299    metricsUpdateForGet(results, before);
7300
7301    return results;
7302  }
7303
7304  void metricsUpdateForGet(List<Cell> results, long before) {
7305    if (this.metricsRegion != null) {
7306      this.metricsRegion.updateGet(EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime() - before);
7307    }
7308  }
