7310  @Override
7311  public void mutateRow(RowMutations rm) throws IOException {
7312    // Don't need nonces here - RowMutations only supports puts and deletes
7313    final List<Mutation> m = rm.getMutations();
7314    batchMutate(m.toArray(new Mutation[m.size()]), true, HConstants.NO_NONCE,
7315        HConstants.NO_NONCE);
7316  }
7317
7318  /**
7319   * Perform atomic (all or none) mutations within the region.
7320   * @param mutations The list of mutations to perform.
7321   * <code>mutations</code> can contain operations for multiple rows.
7322   * Caller has to ensure that all rows are contained in this region.
7323   * @param rowsToLock Rows to lock
7324   * @param nonceGroup Optional nonce group of the operation (client Id)
7325   * @param nonce Optional nonce of the operation (unique random id to ensure "more idempotence")
7326   * If multiple rows are locked care should be taken that
7327   * <code>rowsToLock</code> is sorted in order to avoid deadlocks.
7328   * @throws IOException
7329   */
7330  @Override
7331  public void mutateRowsWithLocks(Collection<Mutation> mutations,
7332      Collection<byte[]> rowsToLock, long nonceGroup, long nonce) throws IOException {
7333    batchMutate(new MutationBatchOperation(this, mutations.toArray(new Mutation[mutations.size()]),
7334        true, nonceGroup, nonce) {
7335      @Override
7336      public MiniBatchOperationInProgress<Mutation> lockRowsAndBuildMiniBatch(
7337          List<RowLock> acquiredRowLocks) throws IOException {
7338        RowLock prevRowLock = null;
7339        for (byte[] row : rowsToLock) {
7340          try {
7341            RowLock rowLock = region.getRowLockInternal(row, false, prevRowLock); // write lock
7342            if (rowLock != prevRowLock) {
7343              acquiredRowLocks.add(rowLock);
7344              prevRowLock = rowLock;
7345            }
7346          } catch (IOException ioe) {
7347            LOG.warn("Failed getting lock, row=" + Bytes.toStringBinary(row), ioe);
7348            throw ioe;
7349          }
7350        }
7351        return createMiniBatch(size(), size());
7352      }
7353    });
7354  }
7355
7356  /**
7357   * @return statistics about the current load of the region
7358   */
7359  public ClientProtos.RegionLoadStats getLoadStatistics() {
7360    if (!regionStatsEnabled) {
7361      return null;
7362    }
7363    ClientProtos.RegionLoadStats.Builder stats = ClientProtos.RegionLoadStats.newBuilder();
7364    stats.setMemStoreLoad((int) (Math.min(100, (this.memStoreSize.getHeapSize() * 100) / this
7365        .memstoreFlushSize)));
7366    if (rsServices.getHeapMemoryManager() != null) {
7367      // the HeapMemoryManager uses -0.0 to signal a problem asking the JVM,
7368      // so we could just do the calculation below and we'll get a 0.
7369      // treating it as a special case analogous to no HMM instead so that it can be
7370      // programatically treated different from using <1% of heap.
7371      final float occupancy = rsServices.getHeapMemoryManager().getHeapOccupancyPercent();
7372      if (occupancy != HeapMemoryManager.HEAP_OCCUPANCY_ERROR_VALUE) {
7373        stats.setHeapOccupancy((int)(occupancy * 100));
7374      }
7375    }
7376    stats.setCompactionPressure((int) (rsServices.getCompactionPressure() * 100 > 100 ? 100
7377        : rsServices.getCompactionPressure() * 100));
7378    return stats.build();
7379  }
7380
7381  @Override
7382  public void processRowsWithLocks(RowProcessor<?,?> processor) throws IOException {
7383    processRowsWithLocks(processor, rowProcessorTimeout, HConstants.NO_NONCE, HConstants.NO_NONCE);
7384  }
7385
7386  @Override
7387  public void processRowsWithLocks(RowProcessor<?,?> processor, long nonceGroup, long nonce)
7388      throws IOException {
7389    processRowsWithLocks(processor, rowProcessorTimeout, nonceGroup, nonce);
7390  }
7391
7392  @Override
7393  public void processRowsWithLocks(RowProcessor<?,?> processor, long timeout,
7394      long nonceGroup, long nonce) throws IOException {
7395    for (byte[] row : processor.getRowsToLock()) {
7396      checkRow(row, "processRowsWithLocks");
7397    }
7398    if (!processor.readOnly()) {
7399      checkReadOnly();
7400    }
7401    checkResources();
7402    startRegionOperation();
7403    WALEdit walEdit = new WALEdit();
7404
7405    // STEP 1. Run pre-process hook
7406    preProcess(processor, walEdit);
7407    // Short circuit the read only case
7408    if (processor.readOnly()) {
7409      try {
7410        long now = EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime();
7411        doProcessRowWithTimeout(processor, now, this, null, null, timeout);
7412        processor.postProcess(this, walEdit, true);
7413      } finally {
7414        closeRegionOperation();
7415      }
7416      return;
7417    }
7418
7419    boolean locked = false;
7420    List<RowLock> acquiredRowLocks = null;
7421    List<Mutation> mutations = new ArrayList<>();
7422    Collection<byte[]> rowsToLock = processor.getRowsToLock();
7423    // This is assigned by mvcc either explicity in the below or in the guts of the WAL append
7424    // when it assigns the edit a sequencedid (A.K.A the mvcc write number).
7425    WriteEntry writeEntry = null;
7426    MemStoreSizing memstoreAccounting = new MemStoreSizing();
7427    try {
7428      boolean success = false;
7429      try {
7430        // STEP 2. Acquire the row lock(s)
7431        acquiredRowLocks = new ArrayList<>(rowsToLock.size());
7432        RowLock prevRowLock = null;
7433        for (byte[] row : rowsToLock) {
7434          // Attempt to lock all involved rows, throw if any lock times out
7435          // use a writer lock for mixed reads and writes
7436          RowLock rowLock = getRowLockInternal(row, false, prevRowLock);
7437          if (rowLock != prevRowLock) {
7438            acquiredRowLocks.add(rowLock);
7439            prevRowLock = rowLock;
7440          }
7441        }
7442        // STEP 3. Region lock
7443        lock(this.updatesLock.readLock(), acquiredRowLocks.isEmpty() ? 1 : acquiredRowLocks.size());
7444        locked = true;
7445        long now = EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime();
7446        // STEP 4. Let the processor scan the rows, generate mutations and add waledits
7447        doProcessRowWithTimeout(processor, now, this, mutations, walEdit, timeout);
7448        if (!mutations.isEmpty()) {
7449          writeRequestsCount.add(mutations.size());
7450          // STEP 5. Call the preBatchMutate hook
7451          processor.preBatchMutate(this, walEdit);
7452
7453          // STEP 6. Append and sync if walEdit has data to write out.
7454          if (!walEdit.isEmpty()) {
7455            writeEntry = doWALAppend(walEdit, getEffectiveDurability(processor.useDurability()),
7456                processor.getClusterIds(), now, nonceGroup, nonce);
7457          } else {
7458            // We are here if WAL is being skipped.
7459            writeEntry = this.mvcc.begin();
7460          }
7461
7462          // STEP 7. Apply to memstore
7463          long sequenceId = writeEntry.getWriteNumber();
7464          for (Mutation m : mutations) {
7465            // Handle any tag based cell features.
7466            // TODO: Do we need to call rewriteCellTags down in applyToMemStore()? Why not before
7467            // so tags go into WAL?
7468            rewriteCellTags(m.getFamilyCellMap(), m);
7469            for (CellScanner cellScanner = m.cellScanner(); cellScanner.advance();) {
7470              Cell cell = cellScanner.current();
7471              if (walEdit.isEmpty()) {
7472                // If walEdit is empty, we put nothing in WAL. WAL stamps Cells with sequence id.
7473                // If no WAL, need to stamp it here.
7474                PrivateCellUtil.setSequenceId(cell, sequenceId);
7475              }
7476              applyToMemStore(getStore(cell), cell, memstoreAccounting);
7477            }
7478          }
7479
7480          // STEP 8. call postBatchMutate hook
7481          processor.postBatchMutate(this);
7482
7483          // STEP 9. Complete mvcc.
7484          mvcc.completeAndWait(writeEntry);
7485          writeEntry = null;
7486
7487          // STEP 10. Release region lock
7488          if (locked) {
7489            this.updatesLock.readLock().unlock();
7490            locked = false;
7491          }
7492
7493          // STEP 11. Release row lock(s)
7494          releaseRowLocks(acquiredRowLocks);
7495        }
7496        success = true;
7497      } finally {
7498        // Call complete rather than completeAndWait because we probably had error if walKey != null
7499        if (writeEntry != null) mvcc.complete(writeEntry);
7500        if (locked) {
7501          this.updatesLock.readLock().unlock();
7502        }
7503        // release locks if some were acquired but another timed out
7504        releaseRowLocks(acquiredRowLocks);
7505      }
7506
7507      // 12. Run post-process hook
7508      processor.postProcess(this, walEdit, success);
7509    } finally {
7510      closeRegionOperation();
7511      if (!mutations.isEmpty()) {
7512        this.incMemStoreSize(memstoreAccounting);
7513        requestFlushIfNeeded();
7514      }
7515    }
7516  }
7517
7518  private void preProcess(final RowProcessor<?,?> processor, final WALEdit walEdit)
7519  throws IOException {
7520    try {
7521      processor.preProcess(this, walEdit);
7522    } catch (IOException e) {
7523      closeRegionOperation();
7524      throw e;
7525    }
7526  }
7527
7528  private void doProcessRowWithTimeout(final RowProcessor<?,?> processor,
7529                                       final long now,
7530                                       final HRegion region,
7531                                       final List<Mutation> mutations,
7532                                       final WALEdit walEdit,
7533                                       final long timeout) throws IOException {
7534    // Short circuit the no time bound case.
7535    if (timeout < 0) {
7536      try {
7537        processor.process(now, region, mutations, walEdit);
7538      } catch (IOException e) {
7539        String row = processor.getRowsToLock().isEmpty() ? "" :
7540          " on row(s):" + Bytes.toStringBinary(processor.getRowsToLock().iterator().next()) + "...";
7541        LOG.warn("RowProcessor:" + processor.getClass().getName() +
7542            " throws Exception" + row, e);
7543        throw e;
7544      }
7545      return;
7546    }
7547
7548    // Case with time bound
7549    FutureTask<Void> task = new FutureTask<>(new Callable<Void>() {
7550        @Override
7551        public Void call() throws IOException {
7552          try {
7553            processor.process(now, region, mutations, walEdit);
7554            return null;
7555          } catch (IOException e) {
7556            String row = processor.getRowsToLock().isEmpty() ? "" :
7557              " on row(s):" + Bytes.toStringBinary(processor.getRowsToLock().iterator().next()) + "...";
7558            LOG.warn("RowProcessor:" + processor.getClass().getName() +
7559                " throws Exception" + row, e);
7560            throw e;
7561          }
7562        }
7563      });
7564    rowProcessorExecutor.execute(task);
7565    try {
7566      task.get(timeout, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
7567    } catch (TimeoutException te) {
7568      String row = processor.getRowsToLock().isEmpty() ? "" :
7569        " on row(s):" + Bytes.toStringBinary(processor.getRowsToLock().iterator().next()) + "...";
7570      LOG.error("RowProcessor timeout:" + timeout + " ms" + row);
7571      throw new IOException(te);
7572    } catch (Exception e) {
7573      throw new IOException(e);
7574    }
7575  }
7576

7584  }

7589  }
7590
7591  public Result increment(Increment mutation, long nonceGroup, long nonce) throws IOException {
7592    return doDelta(Operation.INCREMENT, mutation, nonceGroup, nonce, mutation.isReturnResults());
7593  }
7594
7595  /**
7596   * Add "deltas" to Cells. Deltas are increments or appends. Switch on <code>op</code>.
7597   *
7598   * <p>If increment, add deltas to current values or if an append, then
7599   * append the deltas to the current Cell values.
7600   *
7601   * <p>Append and Increment code paths are mostly the same. They differ in just a few places.
7602   * This method does the code path for increment and append and then in key spots, switches
7603   * on the passed in <code>op</code> to do increment or append specific paths.
7604   */
7605  private Result doDelta(Operation op, Mutation mutation, long nonceGroup, long nonce,
7606      boolean returnResults) throws IOException {
7607    checkReadOnly();
7608    checkResources();
7609    checkRow(mutation.getRow(), op.toString());
7610    checkFamilies(mutation.getFamilyCellMap().keySet());
7611    this.writeRequestsCount.increment();
7612    WriteEntry writeEntry = null;
7613    startRegionOperation(op);
7614    List<Cell> results = returnResults? new ArrayList<>(mutation.size()): null;
7615    RowLock rowLock = null;
7616    MemStoreSizing memstoreAccounting = new MemStoreSizing();
7617    try {
7618      rowLock = getRowLockInternal(mutation.getRow(), false, null);
7619      lock(this.updatesLock.readLock());
7620      try {
7621        Result cpResult = doCoprocessorPreCall(op, mutation);
7622        if (cpResult != null) {
7623          // Metrics updated below in the finally block.
7624          return returnResults? cpResult: null;
7625        }
7626        Durability effectiveDurability = getEffectiveDurability(mutation.getDurability());
7627        Map<HStore, List<Cell>> forMemStore = new HashMap<>(mutation.getFamilyCellMap().size());
7628        // Reckon Cells to apply to WAL --  in returned walEdit -- and what to add to memstore and
7629        // what to return back to the client (in 'forMemStore' and 'results' respectively).
7630        WALEdit walEdit = reckonDeltas(op, mutation, effectiveDurability, forMemStore, results);
7631        // Actually write to WAL now if a walEdit to apply.
7632        if (walEdit != null && !walEdit.isEmpty()) {
7633          writeEntry = doWALAppend(walEdit, effectiveDurability, nonceGroup, nonce);
7634        } else {
7635          // If walEdits is empty, it means we skipped the WAL; update LongAdders and start an mvcc
7636          // transaction.
7637          recordMutationWithoutWal(mutation.getFamilyCellMap());
7638          writeEntry = mvcc.begin();
7639          updateSequenceId(forMemStore.values(), writeEntry.getWriteNumber());
7640        }
7641        // Now write to MemStore. Do it a column family at a time.
7642        for (Map.Entry<HStore, List<Cell>> e : forMemStore.entrySet()) {
7643          applyToMemStore(e.getKey(), e.getValue(), true, memstoreAccounting);
7644        }
7645        mvcc.completeAndWait(writeEntry);
7646        if (rsServices != null && rsServices.getNonceManager() != null) {
7647          rsServices.getNonceManager().addMvccToOperationContext(nonceGroup, nonce,
7648            writeEntry.getWriteNumber());
7649        }
7650        writeEntry = null;
7651      } finally {
7652        this.updatesLock.readLock().unlock();
7653      }
7654      // If results is null, then client asked that we not return the calculated results.
7655      return results != null && returnResults? Result.create(results): Result.EMPTY_RESULT;
7656    } finally {
7657      // Call complete always, even on success. doDelta is doing a Get READ_UNCOMMITTED when it goes
7658      // to get current value under an exclusive lock so no need so no need to wait to return to
7659      // the client. Means only way to read-your-own-increment or append is to come in with an
7660      // a 0 increment.
7661      if (writeEntry != null) mvcc.complete(writeEntry);
7662      if (rowLock != null) {
7663        rowLock.release();
7664      }
7665      // Request a cache flush if over the limit.  Do it outside update lock.
7666      incMemStoreSize(memstoreAccounting);
7667      requestFlushIfNeeded();
7668      closeRegionOperation(op);
7669      if (this.metricsRegion != null) {
7670        switch (op) {
7671          case INCREMENT:
7672            this.metricsRegion.updateIncrement();
7673            break;
7674          case APPEND:
7675            this.metricsRegion.updateAppend();
7676            break;
7677          default:
7678            break;
7679        }
7680      }
7681    }
7682  }
7683
7684  private WriteEntry doWALAppend(WALEdit walEdit, Durability durability, long nonceGroup,
7685      long nonce)
7686  throws IOException {
7687    return doWALAppend(walEdit, durability, WALKey.EMPTY_UUIDS, System.currentTimeMillis(),
7688      nonceGroup, nonce);
7689  }
7690
7691  private WriteEntry doWALAppend(WALEdit walEdit, Durability durability, List<UUID> clusterIds,
7692      long now, long nonceGroup, long nonce) throws IOException {
7693    return doWALAppend(walEdit, durability, clusterIds, now, nonceGroup, nonce,
7694        SequenceId.NO_SEQUENCE_ID);
7695  }
7696
7697  /**
7698   * @return writeEntry associated with this append
7699   */
7700  private WriteEntry doWALAppend(WALEdit walEdit, Durability durability, List<UUID> clusterIds,
7701      long now, long nonceGroup, long nonce, long origLogSeqNum) throws IOException {
7702    Preconditions.checkArgument(walEdit != null && !walEdit.isEmpty(),
7703        "WALEdit is null or empty!");
7704    Preconditions.checkArgument(!walEdit.isReplay() || origLogSeqNum != SequenceId.NO_SEQUENCE_ID,
7705        "Invalid replay sequence Id for replay WALEdit!");
7706    // Using default cluster id, as this can only happen in the originating cluster.
7707    // A slave cluster receives the final value (not the delta) as a Put. We use HLogKey
7708    // here instead of WALKeyImpl directly to support legacy coprocessors.
7709    WALKeyImpl walKey = walEdit.isReplay()?
7710        new WALKeyImpl(this.getRegionInfo().getEncodedNameAsBytes(),
7711          this.htableDescriptor.getTableName(), SequenceId.NO_SEQUENCE_ID, now, clusterIds,
7712            nonceGroup, nonce, mvcc) :
7713        new WALKeyImpl(this.getRegionInfo().getEncodedNameAsBytes(),
7714            this.htableDescriptor.getTableName(), SequenceId.NO_SEQUENCE_ID, now, clusterIds,
7715            nonceGroup, nonce, mvcc, this.getReplicationScope());
7716    if (walEdit.isReplay()) {
7717      walKey.setOrigLogSeqNum(origLogSeqNum);
7718    }
7719    WriteEntry writeEntry = null;
7720    try {
7721      long txid = this.wal.append(this.getRegionInfo(), walKey, walEdit, true);
7722      // Call sync on our edit.
7723      if (txid != 0) {
7724        sync(txid, durability);
7725      }
7726      writeEntry = walKey.getWriteEntry();
7727    } catch (IOException ioe) {
7728      if (walKey != null && walKey.getWriteEntry() != null) {
7729        mvcc.complete(walKey.getWriteEntry());
7730      }
7731      throw ioe;
7732    }
7733    return writeEntry;
7734  }
7735
7736  /**
7737   * Do coprocessor pre-increment or pre-append call.
7738   * @return Result returned out of the coprocessor, which means bypass all further processing and
7739   *  return the proffered Result instead, or null which means proceed.
7740   */
7741  private Result doCoprocessorPreCall(final Operation op, final Mutation mutation)
7742  throws IOException {
7743    Result result = null;
7744    if (this.coprocessorHost != null) {
7745      switch(op) {
7746        case INCREMENT:
7747          result = this.coprocessorHost.preIncrementAfterRowLock((Increment)mutation);
7748          break;
7749        case APPEND:
7750          result = this.coprocessorHost.preAppendAfterRowLock((Append)mutation);
7751          break;
7752        default: throw new UnsupportedOperationException(op.toString());
7753      }
7754    }
7755    return result;
7756  }
7757
7758  /**
7759   * Reckon the Cells to apply to WAL, memstore, and to return to the Client; these Sets are not
7760   * always the same dependent on whether to write WAL or if the amount to increment is zero (in
7761   * this case we write back nothing, just return latest Cell value to the client).
7762   *
7763   * @param results Fill in here what goes back to the Client if it is non-null (if null, client
7764   *  doesn't want results).
7765   * @param forMemStore Fill in here what to apply to the MemStore (by Store).
7766   * @return A WALEdit to apply to WAL or null if we are to skip the WAL.
7767   */
7768  private WALEdit reckonDeltas(Operation op, Mutation mutation, Durability effectiveDurability,
7769      Map<HStore, List<Cell>> forMemStore, List<Cell> results) throws IOException {
7770    WALEdit walEdit = null;
7771    long now = EnvironmentEdgeManager.currentTime();
7772    final boolean writeToWAL = effectiveDurability != Durability.SKIP_WAL;
7773    // Process a Store/family at a time.
7774    for (Map.Entry<byte [], List<Cell>> entry: mutation.getFamilyCellMap().entrySet()) {
7775      final byte[] columnFamilyName = entry.getKey();
7776      List<Cell> deltas = entry.getValue();
7777      HStore store = this.stores.get(columnFamilyName);
7778      // Reckon for the Store what to apply to WAL and MemStore.
7779      List<Cell> toApply =
7780        reckonDeltasByStore(store, op, mutation, effectiveDurability, now, deltas, results);
7781      if (!toApply.isEmpty()) {
7782        forMemStore.put(store, toApply);
7783        if (writeToWAL) {
7784          if (walEdit == null) {
7785            walEdit = new WALEdit();
7786          }
7787          walEdit.getCells().addAll(toApply);
7788        }
7789      }
7790    }
7791    return walEdit;
7792  }
7793
7794  /**
7795   * Reckon the Cells to apply to WAL, memstore, and to return to the Client in passed
7796   * column family/Store.
7797   *
7798   * Does Get of current value and then adds passed in deltas for this Store returning the result.
7799   *
7800   * @param op Whether Increment or Append
7801   * @param mutation The encompassing Mutation object
7802   * @param deltas Changes to apply to this Store; either increment amount or data to append
7803   * @param results In here we accumulate all the Cells we are to return to the client; this List
7804   *  can be larger than what we return in case where delta is zero; i.e. don't write
7805   *  out new values, just return current value. If null, client doesn't want results returned.
7806   * @return Resulting Cells after <code>deltas</code> have been applied to current
7807   *  values. Side effect is our filling out of the <code>results</code> List.
7808   */
7809  private List<Cell> reckonDeltasByStore(HStore store, Operation op, Mutation mutation,
7810      Durability effectiveDurability, long now, List<Cell> deltas, List<Cell> results)
7811      throws IOException {
7812    byte[] columnFamily = store.getColumnFamilyDescriptor().getName();
7813    List<Cell> toApply = new ArrayList<>(deltas.size());
7814    // Get previous values for all columns in this family.
7815    TimeRange tr = null;
7816    switch (op) {
7817      case INCREMENT:
7818        tr = ((Increment)mutation).getTimeRange();
7819        break;
7820      case APPEND:
7821        tr = ((Append)mutation).getTimeRange();
7822        break;
7823      default:
7824        break;
7825    }
7826    List<Cell> currentValues = get(mutation, store, deltas,null, tr);
7827    // Iterate the input columns and update existing values if they were found, otherwise
7828    // add new column initialized to the delta amount
7829    int currentValuesIndex = 0;
7830    for (int i = 0; i < deltas.size(); i++) {
7831      Cell delta = deltas.get(i);
7832      Cell currentValue = null;
7833      boolean firstWrite = false;
7834      if (currentValuesIndex < currentValues.size() &&
7835          CellUtil.matchingQualifier(currentValues.get(currentValuesIndex), delta)) {
7836        currentValue = currentValues.get(currentValuesIndex);
7837        if (i < (deltas.size() - 1) && !CellUtil.matchingQualifier(delta, deltas.get(i + 1))) {
7838          currentValuesIndex++;
7839        }
7840      } else {
7841        firstWrite = true;
7842      }
7843      // Switch on whether this an increment or an append building the new Cell to apply.
7844      Cell newCell = null;
7845      MutationType mutationType = null;
7846      boolean apply = true;
7847      switch (op) {
7848        case INCREMENT:
7849          mutationType = MutationType.INCREMENT;
7850          // If delta amount to apply is 0, don't write WAL or MemStore.
7851          long deltaAmount = getLongValue(delta);
7852          // TODO: Does zero value mean reset Cell? For example, the ttl.
7853          apply = deltaAmount != 0;
7854          final long newValue = currentValue == null ? deltaAmount : getLongValue(currentValue) + deltaAmount;
7855          newCell = reckonDelta(delta, currentValue, columnFamily, now, mutation, (oldCell) -> Bytes.toBytes(newValue));
7856          break;
7857        case APPEND:
7858          mutationType = MutationType.APPEND;
7859          // Always apply Append. TODO: Does empty delta value mean reset Cell? It seems to.
7860          newCell = reckonDelta(delta, currentValue, columnFamily, now, mutation, (oldCell) ->
7861            ByteBuffer.wrap(new byte[delta.getValueLength() + oldCell.getValueLength()])
7862                    .put(oldCell.getValueArray(), oldCell.getValueOffset(), oldCell.getValueLength())
7863                    .put(delta.getValueArray(), delta.getValueOffset(), delta.getValueLength())
7864                    .array()
7865          );
7866          break;
7867        default: throw new UnsupportedOperationException(op.toString());
7868      }
7869
7870      // Give coprocessors a chance to update the new cell
7871      if (coprocessorHost != null) {
7872        newCell =
7873            coprocessorHost.postMutationBeforeWAL(mutationType, mutation, currentValue, newCell);
7874      }
7875      // If apply, we need to update memstore/WAL with new value; add it toApply.
7876      if (apply || firstWrite) {
7877        toApply.add(newCell);
7878      }
7879      // Add to results to get returned to the Client. If null, cilent does not want results.
7880      if (results != null) {
7881        results.add(newCell);
7882      }
7883    }
7884    return toApply;
7885  }
7886
7887  private static Cell reckonDelta(final Cell delta, final Cell currentCell,
7888                                  final byte[] columnFamily, final long now,
7889                                  Mutation mutation, Function<Cell, byte[]> supplier) throws IOException {
7890    // Forward any tags found on the delta.
7891    List<Tag> tags = TagUtil.carryForwardTags(delta);
7892    tags = TagUtil.carryForwardTTLTag(tags, mutation.getTTL());
7893    if (currentCell != null) {
7894      tags = TagUtil.carryForwardTags(tags, currentCell);
7895      byte[] newValue = supplier.apply(currentCell);
7896      return ExtendedCellBuilderFactory.create(CellBuilderType.SHALLOW_COPY)
7897              .setRow(mutation.getRow(), 0, mutation.getRow().length)
7898              .setFamily(columnFamily, 0, columnFamily.length)
7899              // copy the qualifier if the cell is located in shared memory.
7900              .setQualifier(CellUtil.cloneQualifier(delta))
7901              .setTimestamp(Math.max(currentCell.getTimestamp() + 1, now))
7902              .setType(KeyValue.Type.Put.getCode())
7903              .setValue(newValue, 0, newValue.length)
7904              .setTags(TagUtil.fromList(tags))
7905              .build();
7906    } else {
7907      PrivateCellUtil.updateLatestStamp(delta, now);
7908      return CollectionUtils.isEmpty(tags) ? delta : PrivateCellUtil.createCell(delta, tags);
7909    }
7910  }
7911
7912  /**
7913   * @return Get the long out of the passed in Cell
7914   */
7915  private static long getLongValue(final Cell cell) throws DoNotRetryIOException {
7916    int len = cell.getValueLength();
7917    if (len != Bytes.SIZEOF_LONG) {
7918      // throw DoNotRetryIOException instead of IllegalArgumentException
7919      throw new DoNotRetryIOException("Field is not a long, it's " + len + " bytes wide");
7920    }
7921    return PrivateCellUtil.getValueAsLong(cell);
7922  }
7923
7924  /**
7925   * Do a specific Get on passed <code>columnFamily</code> and column qualifiers.
7926   * @param mutation Mutation we are doing this Get for.
7927   * @param store Which column family on row (TODO: Go all Gets in one go)
7928   * @param coordinates Cells from <code>mutation</code> used as coordinates applied to Get.
7929   * @return Return list of Cells found.
7930   */
7931  private List<Cell> get(Mutation mutation, HStore store, List<Cell> coordinates,
7932      IsolationLevel isolation, TimeRange tr) throws IOException {
7933    // Sort the cells so that they match the order that they appear in the Get results. Otherwise,
7934    // we won't be able to find the existing values if the cells are not specified in order by the
7935    // client since cells are in an array list.
7936    // TODO: I don't get why we are sorting. St.Ack 20150107
7937    sort(coordinates, store.getComparator());
7938    Get get = new Get(mutation.getRow());
7939    if (isolation != null) {
7940      get.setIsolationLevel(isolation);
7941    }
7942    for (Cell cell: coordinates) {
7943      get.addColumn(store.getColumnFamilyDescriptor().getName(), CellUtil.cloneQualifier(cell));
7944    }
7945    // Increments carry time range. If an Increment instance, put it on the Get.
7946    if (tr != null) {
7947      get.setTimeRange(tr.getMin(), tr.getMax());
7948    }
7949    return get(get, false);
7950  }
7951
7952  /**
7953   * @return Sorted list of <code>cells</code> using <code>comparator</code>
7954   */
7955  private static List<Cell> sort(List<Cell> cells, final CellComparator comparator) {
7956    cells.sort(comparator);
7957    return cells;
7958  }

7961  // New HBASE-880 Helpers
7962  //
7963
7964  void checkFamily(final byte [] family)
7965  throws NoSuchColumnFamilyException {
7966    if (!this.htableDescriptor.hasColumnFamily(family)) {
7967      throw new NoSuchColumnFamilyException("Column family " +
7968          Bytes.toString(family) + " does not exist in region " + this
7969          + " in table " + this.htableDescriptor);
7970    }
7971  }
7972
7973  public static final long FIXED_OVERHEAD = ClassSize.align(
7974      ClassSize.OBJECT +
7975      ClassSize.ARRAY +
7976      51 * ClassSize.REFERENCE + 3 * Bytes.SIZEOF_INT +
7977      (14 * Bytes.SIZEOF_LONG) +
7978      3 * Bytes.SIZEOF_BOOLEAN);
7979
7980  // woefully out of date - currently missing:
7981  // 1 x HashMap - coprocessorServiceHandlers
7982  // 6 x LongAdder - numMutationsWithoutWAL, dataInMemoryWithoutWAL,
7983  //   checkAndMutateChecksPassed, checkAndMutateChecksFailed, readRequestsCount,
7984  //   writeRequestsCount
7985  // 1 x HRegion$WriteState - writestate
7986  // 1 x RegionCoprocessorHost - coprocessorHost
7987  // 1 x RegionSplitPolicy - splitPolicy
7988  // 1 x MetricsRegion - metricsRegion
7989  // 1 x MetricsRegionWrapperImpl - metricsRegionWrapper
7990  public static final long DEEP_OVERHEAD = FIXED_OVERHEAD +
7991      ClassSize.OBJECT + // closeLock
7992      (2 * ClassSize.ATOMIC_BOOLEAN) + // closed, closing
7993      (3 * ClassSize.ATOMIC_LONG) + // numPutsWithoutWAL, dataInMemoryWithoutWAL,
7994                                    // compactionsFailed
7995      (2 * ClassSize.CONCURRENT_HASHMAP) +  // lockedRows, scannerReadPoints
7996      WriteState.HEAP_SIZE + // writestate
7997      ClassSize.CONCURRENT_SKIPLISTMAP + ClassSize.CONCURRENT_SKIPLISTMAP_ENTRY + // stores
7998      (2 * ClassSize.REENTRANT_LOCK) + // lock, updatesLock
7999      MultiVersionConcurrencyControl.FIXED_SIZE // mvcc
8000      + 2 * ClassSize.TREEMAP // maxSeqIdInStores, replicationScopes
8001      + 2 * ClassSize.ATOMIC_INTEGER // majorInProgress, minorInProgress
8002      + ClassSize.STORE_SERVICES // store services
8003      + StoreHotnessProtector.FIXED_SIZE
8004      ;
8005
8006  @Override
8007  public long heapSize() {
8008    // this does not take into account row locks, recent flushes, mvcc entries, and more
8009    return DEEP_OVERHEAD + stores.values().stream().mapToLong(HStore::heapSize).sum();
8010  }
8011
8012  /**
8013   * Registers a new protocol buffer {@link Service} subclass as a coprocessor endpoint to
8014   * be available for handling Region#execService(com.google.protobuf.RpcController,
8015   *    org.apache.hadoop.hbase.protobuf.generated.ClientProtos.CoprocessorServiceCall) calls.
8016   *
8017   * <p>
8018   * Only a single instance may be registered per region for a given {@link Service} subclass (the
8019   * instances are keyed on {@link com.google.protobuf.Descriptors.ServiceDescriptor#getFullName()}.
8020   * After the first registration, subsequent calls with the same service name will fail with
8021   * a return value of {@code false}.
8022   * </p>
8023   * @param instance the {@code Service} subclass instance to expose as a coprocessor endpoint
8024   * @return {@code true} if the registration was successful, {@code false}
8025   * otherwise
8026   */
8027  public boolean registerService(com.google.protobuf.Service instance) {
8028    /*
8029     * No stacking of instances is allowed for a single service name
8030     */
8031    com.google.protobuf.Descriptors.ServiceDescriptor serviceDesc = instance.getDescriptorForType();
8032    String serviceName = CoprocessorRpcUtils.getServiceName(serviceDesc);
8033    if (coprocessorServiceHandlers.containsKey(serviceName)) {
8034      LOG.error("Coprocessor service " + serviceName +
8035          " already registered, rejecting request from " + instance);
8036      return false;
8037    }
8038
8039    coprocessorServiceHandlers.put(serviceName, instance);
8040    if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
8041      LOG.debug("Registered coprocessor service: region=" +
8042          Bytes.toStringBinary(getRegionInfo().getRegionName()) +
8043          " service=" + serviceName);
8044    }
8045    return true;
8046  }
8047
8048  /**
8049   * Executes a single protocol buffer coprocessor endpoint {@link Service} method using
8050   * the registered protocol handlers.  {@link Service} implementations must be registered via the
8051   * {@link #registerService(com.google.protobuf.Service)}
8052   * method before they are available.
8053   *
8054   * @param controller an {@code RpcContoller} implementation to pass to the invoked service
8055   * @param call a {@code CoprocessorServiceCall} instance identifying the service, method,
8056   *     and parameters for the method invocation
8057   * @return a protocol buffer {@code Message} instance containing the method's result
8058   * @throws IOException if no registered service handler is found or an error
8059   *     occurs during the invocation
8060   * @see #registerService(com.google.protobuf.Service)
8061   */
8062  public com.google.protobuf.Message execService(com.google.protobuf.RpcController controller,
8063      CoprocessorServiceCall call) throws IOException {
8064    String serviceName = call.getServiceName();
8065    com.google.protobuf.Service service = coprocessorServiceHandlers.get(serviceName);
8066    if (service == null) {
8067      throw new UnknownProtocolException(null, "No registered coprocessor service found for " +
8068          serviceName + " in region " + Bytes.toStringBinary(getRegionInfo().getRegionName()));
8069    }
8070    com.google.protobuf.Descriptors.ServiceDescriptor serviceDesc = service.getDescriptorForType();
8071
8072    String methodName = call.getMethodName();
8073    com.google.protobuf.Descriptors.MethodDescriptor methodDesc =
8074        CoprocessorRpcUtils.getMethodDescriptor(methodName, serviceDesc);
8075
8076    com.google.protobuf.Message.Builder builder =
8077        service.getRequestPrototype(methodDesc).newBuilderForType();
8078
8079    org.apache.hadoop.hbase.protobuf.ProtobufUtil.mergeFrom(builder,
8080        call.getRequest().toByteArray());
8081    com.google.protobuf.Message request =
8082        CoprocessorRpcUtils.getRequest(service, methodDesc, call.getRequest());
8083
8084    if (coprocessorHost != null) {
8085      request = coprocessorHost.preEndpointInvocation(service, methodName, request);
8086    }
8087
8088    final com.google.protobuf.Message.Builder responseBuilder =
8089        service.getResponsePrototype(methodDesc).newBuilderForType();
8090    service.callMethod(methodDesc, controller, request,
8091        new com.google.protobuf.RpcCallback<com.google.protobuf.Message>() {
8092      @Override
8093      public void run(com.google.protobuf.Message message) {
8094        if (message != null) {
8095          responseBuilder.mergeFrom(message);
8096        }
8097      }
8098    });
8099
8100    if (coprocessorHost != null) {
8101      coprocessorHost.postEndpointInvocation(service, methodName, request, responseBuilder);
8102    }
8103    IOException exception =
8104        org.apache.hadoop.hbase.ipc.CoprocessorRpcUtils.getControllerException(controller);
8105    if (exception != null) {
8106      throw exception;
8107    }
8108
8109    return responseBuilder.build();
8110  }
8111
8112  boolean shouldForceSplit() {
8113    return this.splitRequest;
8114  }
8115
8116  byte[] getExplicitSplitPoint() {
8117    return this.explicitSplitPoint;
8118  }
8119
8120  void forceSplit(byte[] sp) {
8121    // This HRegion will go away after the forced split is successful
8122    // But if a forced split fails, we need to clear forced split.
8123    this.splitRequest = true;
8124    if (sp != null) {
8125      this.explicitSplitPoint = sp;
8126    }
8127  }
8128
8129  void clearSplit() {
8130    this.splitRequest = false;
8131    this.explicitSplitPoint = null;
8132  }
8133
8134  /**
8135   * Return the splitpoint. null indicates the region isn't splittable
8136   * If the splitpoint isn't explicitly specified, it will go over the stores
8137   * to find the best splitpoint. Currently the criteria of best splitpoint
8138   * is based on the size of the store.
8139   */
8140  public byte[] checkSplit() {
8141    // Can't split META
8142    if (this.getRegionInfo().isMetaRegion() ||
8143        TableName.NAMESPACE_TABLE_NAME.equals(this.getRegionInfo().getTable())) {
8144      if (shouldForceSplit()) {
8145        LOG.warn("Cannot split meta region in HBase 0.20 and above");
8146      }
8147      return null;
8148    }
8149
8150    // Can't split a region that is closing.
8151    if (this.isClosing()) {
8152      return null;
8153    }
8154
8155    if (!splitPolicy.shouldSplit()) {
8156      return null;
8157    }
8158
8159    byte[] ret = splitPolicy.getSplitPoint();
8160
8161    if (ret != null) {
8162      try {
8163        checkRow(ret, "calculated split");
8164      } catch (IOException e) {
8165        LOG.error("Ignoring invalid split", e);
8166        return null;
8167      }
8168    }
8169    return ret;
8170  }
8171
8172  /**
8173   * @return The priority that this region should have in the compaction queue
8174   */
8175  public int getCompactPriority() {
8176    return stores.values().stream().mapToInt(HStore::getCompactPriority).min()
8177        .orElse(Store.NO_PRIORITY);
8178  }

8186  @VisibleForTesting

8189  }
8190
8191  @Override
8192  public void startRegionOperation() throws IOException {
8193    startRegionOperation(Operation.ANY);
8194  }
8195
8196  @Override
8197  public void startRegionOperation(Operation op) throws IOException {
8198    switch (op) {
8199      case GET:  // read operations
8200      case SCAN:
8201        checkReadsEnabled();
8202        break;
8203      default:
8204        break;
8205    }
8206    if (op == Operation.MERGE_REGION || op == Operation.SPLIT_REGION
8207        || op == Operation.COMPACT_REGION) {
8208      // split, merge or compact region doesn't need to check the closing/closed state or lock the
8209      // region
8210      return;
8211    }
8212    if (this.closing.get()) {
8213      throw new NotServingRegionException(getRegionInfo().getRegionNameAsString() + " is closing");
8214    }
8215    lock(lock.readLock());
8216    if (this.closed.get()) {
8217      lock.readLock().unlock();
8218      throw new NotServingRegionException(getRegionInfo().getRegionNameAsString() + " is closed");
8219    }
8220    // The unit for snapshot is a region. So, all stores for this region must be
8221    // prepared for snapshot operation before proceeding.
8222    if (op == Operation.SNAPSHOT) {
8223      stores.values().forEach(HStore::preSnapshotOperation);
8224    }
8225    try {
8226      if (coprocessorHost != null) {
8227        coprocessorHost.postStartRegionOperation(op);
8228      }
8229    } catch (Exception e) {
8230      lock.readLock().unlock();
8231      throw new IOException(e);
8232    }
8233  }
8234
8235  @Override
8236  public void closeRegionOperation() throws IOException {
8237    closeRegionOperation(Operation.ANY);
8238  }
8239
8240  @Override
8241  public void closeRegionOperation(Operation operation) throws IOException {
8242    if (operation == Operation.SNAPSHOT) {
8243      stores.values().forEach(HStore::postSnapshotOperation);
8244    }
8245    lock.readLock().unlock();
8246    if (coprocessorHost != null) {
8247      coprocessorHost.postCloseRegionOperation(operation);
8248    }
8249  }
8250
8251  /**
8252   * This method needs to be called before any public call that reads or
8253   * modifies stores in bulk. It has to be called just before a try.
8254   * #closeBulkRegionOperation needs to be called in the try's finally block
8255   * Acquires a writelock and checks if the region is closing or closed.
8256   * @throws NotServingRegionException when the region is closing or closed
8257   * @throws RegionTooBusyException if failed to get the lock in time
8258   * @throws InterruptedIOException if interrupted while waiting for a lock
8259   */
8260  private void startBulkRegionOperation(boolean writeLockNeeded)
8261      throws NotServingRegionException, RegionTooBusyException, InterruptedIOException {
8262    if (this.closing.get()) {
8263      throw new NotServingRegionException(getRegionInfo().getRegionNameAsString() + " is closing");
8264    }
8265    if (writeLockNeeded) lock(lock.writeLock());
8266    else lock(lock.readLock());
8267    if (this.closed.get()) {
8268      if (writeLockNeeded) lock.writeLock().unlock();
8269      else lock.readLock().unlock();
8270      throw new NotServingRegionException(getRegionInfo().getRegionNameAsString() + " is closed");
8271    }
8272  }
8273
8274  /**
8275   * Closes the lock. This needs to be called in the finally block corresponding
8276   * to the try block of #startRegionOperation
8277   */
8278  private void closeBulkRegionOperation(){
8279    if (lock.writeLock().isHeldByCurrentThread()) lock.writeLock().unlock();
8280    else lock.readLock().unlock();
8281  }
8282
8283  /**
8284   * Update LongAdders for number of puts without wal and the size of possible data loss.
8285   * These information are exposed by the region server metrics.
8286   */
8287  private void recordMutationWithoutWal(final Map<byte [], List<Cell>> familyMap) {
8288    numMutationsWithoutWAL.increment();
8289    if (numMutationsWithoutWAL.sum() <= 1) {
8290      LOG.info("writing data to region " + this +
8291               " with WAL disabled. Data may be lost in the event of a crash.");
8292    }
8293
8294    long mutationSize = 0;
8295    for (List<Cell> cells: familyMap.values()) {
8296      // Optimization: 'foreach' loop is not used. See:
8297      // HBASE-12023 HRegion.applyFamilyMapToMemstore creates too many iterator objects
8298      assert cells instanceof RandomAccess;
8299      int listSize = cells.size();
8300      for (int i=0; i < listSize; i++) {
8301        Cell cell = cells.get(i);
8302        mutationSize += KeyValueUtil.length(cell);
8303      }
8304    }
8305
8306    dataInMemoryWithoutWAL.add(mutationSize);
8307  }
8308
8309  private void lock(final Lock lock) throws RegionTooBusyException, InterruptedIOException {
8310    lock(lock, 1);
8311  }
8312
8313  /**
8314   * Try to acquire a lock.  Throw RegionTooBusyException
8315   * if failed to get the lock in time. Throw InterruptedIOException
8316   * if interrupted while waiting for the lock.
8317   */
8318  private void lock(final Lock lock, final int multiplier)
8319      throws RegionTooBusyException, InterruptedIOException {
8320    try {
8321      final long waitTime = Math.min(maxBusyWaitDuration,
8322          busyWaitDuration * Math.min(multiplier, maxBusyWaitMultiplier));
8323      if (!lock.tryLock(waitTime, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS)) {
8324        // Don't print millis. Message is used as a key over in
8325        // RetriesExhaustedWithDetailsException processing.
8326        throw new RegionTooBusyException("Failed to obtain lock; regionName=" +
8327            (this.getRegionInfo() == null? "unknown":
8328                this.getRegionInfo().getRegionNameAsString()) +
8329            ", server=" + (this.getRegionServerServices() == null? "unknown":
8330                this.getRegionServerServices().getServerName()));
8331      }
8332    } catch (InterruptedException ie) {
8333      LOG.info("Interrupted while waiting for a lock");
8334      InterruptedIOException iie = new InterruptedIOException();
8335      iie.initCause(ie);
8336      throw iie;
8337    }
8338  }
8339
8340  /**
8341   * Calls sync with the given transaction ID
8342   * @param txid should sync up to which transaction
8343   * @throws IOException If anything goes wrong with DFS
8344   */
8345  private void sync(long txid, Durability durability) throws IOException {
8346    if (this.getRegionInfo().isMetaRegion()) {
8347      this.wal.sync(txid);
8348    } else {
8349      switch(durability) {
8350      case USE_DEFAULT:
8351        // do what table defaults to
8352        if (shouldSyncWAL()) {
8353          this.wal.sync(txid);
8354        }
8355        break;
8356      case SKIP_WAL:
8357        // nothing do to
8358        break;
8359      case ASYNC_WAL:
8360        // nothing do to
8361        break;
8362      case SYNC_WAL:
8363      case FSYNC_WAL:
8364        // sync the WAL edit (SYNC and FSYNC treated the same for now)
8365        this.wal.sync(txid);
8366        break;
8367      default:
8368        throw new RuntimeException("Unknown durability " + durability);
8369      }
8370    }
8371  }
8372
8373  /**
8374   * Check whether we should sync the wal from the table's durability settings
8375   */
8376  private boolean shouldSyncWAL() {
8377    return regionDurability.ordinal() >  Durability.ASYNC_WAL.ordinal();
8378  }

8420  @Override
8421  public CompactionState getCompactionState() {
8422    boolean hasMajor = majorInProgress.get() > 0, hasMinor = minorInProgress.get() > 0;
8423    return (hasMajor ? (hasMinor ? CompactionState.MAJOR_AND_MINOR : CompactionState.MAJOR)
8424        : (hasMinor ? CompactionState.MINOR : CompactionState.NONE));
8425  }
8426
8427  public void reportCompactionRequestStart(boolean isMajor){
8428    (isMajor ? majorInProgress : minorInProgress).incrementAndGet();
8429  }
8430
8431  public void reportCompactionRequestEnd(boolean isMajor, int numFiles, long filesSizeCompacted) {
8432    int newValue = (isMajor ? majorInProgress : minorInProgress).decrementAndGet();
8433
8434    // metrics
8435    compactionsFinished.increment();
8436    compactionNumFilesCompacted.add(numFiles);
8437    compactionNumBytesCompacted.add(filesSizeCompacted);
8438
8439    assert newValue >= 0;
8440  }

8499  //// method for debugging tests
8500  void throwException(String title, String regionName) {
8501    StringBuilder buf = new StringBuilder();
8502    buf.append(title + ", ");
8503    buf.append(getRegionInfo().toString());
8504    buf.append(getRegionInfo().isMetaRegion() ? " meta region " : " ");
8505    buf.append("stores: ");
8506    for (HStore s : stores.values()) {
8507      buf.append(s.getColumnFamilyDescriptor().getNameAsString());
8508      buf.append(" size: ");
8509      buf.append(s.getMemStoreSize().getDataSize());
8510      buf.append(" ");
8511    }
8512    buf.append("end-of-stores");
8513    buf.append(", memstore size ");
8514    buf.append(getMemStoreDataSize());
8515    if (getRegionInfo().getRegionNameAsString().startsWith(regionName)) {
8516      throw new RuntimeException(buf.toString());
8517    }
8518  }

8520  @Override
8521  public void requestCompaction(String why, int priority, boolean major,
8522      CompactionLifeCycleTracker tracker) throws IOException {
8523    if (major) {
8524      stores.values().forEach(HStore::triggerMajorCompaction);
8525    }
8526    rsServices.getCompactionRequestor().requestCompaction(this, why, priority, tracker,
8527      RpcServer.getRequestUser().orElse(null));
8528  }
8529
8530  @Override
8531  public void requestCompaction(byte[] family, String why, int priority, boolean major,
8532      CompactionLifeCycleTracker tracker) throws IOException {
8533    HStore store = stores.get(family);
8534    if (store == null) {
8535      throw new NoSuchColumnFamilyException("column family " + Bytes.toString(family) +
8536          " does not exist in region " + getRegionInfo().getRegionNameAsString());
8537    }
8538    if (major) {
8539      store.triggerMajorCompaction();
8540    }
8541    rsServices.getCompactionRequestor().requestCompaction(this, store, why, priority, tracker,
8542      RpcServer.getRequestUser().orElse(null));
8543  }
8544
8545  private void requestFlushIfNeeded() throws RegionTooBusyException {
8546    if(isFlushSize(memStoreSize)) {
8547      requestFlush();
8548    }
8549  }
8550
8551  private void requestFlush() {
8552    if (this.rsServices == null) {
8553      return;
8554    }
8555    requestFlush0(FlushLifeCycleTracker.DUMMY);
8556  }
8557
8558  private void requestFlush0(FlushLifeCycleTracker tracker) {
8559    boolean shouldFlush = false;
8560    synchronized (writestate) {
8561      if (!this.writestate.isFlushRequested()) {
8562        shouldFlush = true;
8563        writestate.flushRequested = true;
8564      }
8565    }
8566    if (shouldFlush) {
8567      // Make request outside of synchronize block; HBASE-818.
8568      this.rsServices.getFlushRequester().requestFlush(this, false, tracker);
8569      if (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {
8570        LOG.debug("Flush requested on " + this.getRegionInfo().getEncodedName());
8571      }
8572    } else {
8573      tracker.notExecuted("Flush already requested on " + this);
8574    }
8575  }
8576
8577  @Override
8578  public void requestFlush(FlushLifeCycleTracker tracker) throws IOException {
8579    requestFlush0(tracker);
8580  }
